 yad pada ambhoruha dhyāna vidhvasta aśeṣa kalmaṣaḥ vastu tām upayātaḥ aham yāmunā iyam namāmi tam śriyaḥ patiḥ nikhila heya pratyanīka kalyāṇa ekatānaḥ sva itara samasta vastu vilakṣaṇa ananta jñana ānanda eka svarūpaḥ svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya jñāna balāi śvarya vīrya śakti tejaḥ prabhṛti asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa mahodadhiḥ sva abhimata anurūpa eka rūpa acintya divya adbhuta nitya niravadya niratiśayāujjvalya saundarya saugandhya saukumārya lāvaṇya yauvana ādi ananta guṇa nidhi divy sva ucita vividha vicitra ananta āścarya nitya niravadya aparimita divya bhūṣaṇaḥ sva anurūpā saṃkhyeya acintya śakti nitya niravadya niratiśaya kalyāṇa divya āyudhaḥ sva abhimata anurūpa nitya niravadya sva rūpa rūpa guṇa vibhavāi śvarya śīla ādi anavadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa śrīvallabhaḥ sva saṅkalpa anuvidhāyi svarūpa sthiti pravṛtti bheda aśeṣa seṣatā eka rati rūpa nitya niravadya niratiśaya jñāna kriyāiśvarya ādi ananta guṇa gaṇa aparimit anavarata abhiṣṭuta caraṇa yugalaḥ vāc manasā aparicchedya svarūpa svabhāvaḥ sva ucita vividha vicitra ananta bhogya bhoga upakaraṇa bhoga sthāna samṛddha ananta āḥ caryā ananta mahā vibhava ananta parimāṇa nitya niravadya akṣara parama vyoma vividha vicitra ananta bhogya bhoktṛ varga paripūrṇa nikhila jagat udaya vibhava laya līlaḥ param brahma puruṣottamaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ brahma ādi sthāvara antam akhilam jagat sṛṣṭvā svena rūpeṇa avasthitaḥ brahma ādi deva manuṣyāṇām dhyāna ārādhana ādi agocaraḥ apāra kāruṇya sauśīlya vātsalyauu dārya mahā udadhiḥ svam eva rūpam tad tad sajātīya saṃsthānam sva svabhāvam ajahad eva kurvan teṣu teṣu lokeṣu avatīrya avatīrya taiḥ taiḥ ārādhitaḥ tad tad iṣṭa anurūpam dharma artha kāma mokṣa ākhyam phalam prayacchan bhū bhāra avatāraṇa apadeśena asmad ādīnām api samāśrayaṇīya tvāya avatīrya urvyām sakalam anuja nayana viṣaya tām gataḥ parāvara nikhila jana manaḥ nayana hāri divya ceṣṭitāni kurvan pūta nāśa kaṭaya mala arjuna ariṣṭa pralamba dhenuka kāliya keśi kuvalaya āpīḍacāṇūra muṣṭika tosala kaṃsa ādīn nihatya anavadhika dayā sauhārda anurāga garbha avalokana ālāpa amṛtaiḥ viśvam āpyāyayan niratiśaya saundarya sauśīlya ādi guṇa gaṇa āviṣkāreṇa akrūra mālā ākāra ādīn parama bhāgavatān kṛtvā pāṇḍu tanaya yuddha protsāhana vyājena parama puruṣa artha lakṣaṇa mokṣa sādhana tayā vedānta uditam sva viṣayam jñāna karma anugṛhītam bhakti yogam avatārayām āsa tatra pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca yuddhe prārabdhe sa bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ jagat upakṛti martyaḥ āśrita vātsalya vivaśaḥ pārtham rathinam ātmānam ca sārathim sarva loka sākṣikam cakāra evam jñātvā api sarva ātmanā andhaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhana vijaya bubhutsayā sañjayam papraccha duryodhanaḥ svayam eva bhīma abhirakṣitam pāṇḍavānām balam ātmīyam ca bhīṣma abhirakṣitam balam avalokya ātma vijaye tasya balasya paryāpta tām ātmīyasya balasya tad vijaye ca aparya āpta tām ācāryāya nivedya antar viṣaṇṇaḥ abhavat tasya viṣādam ālakṣya bhīṣmaḥ tasya harṣam janayitum siṃhanādam śaṅkha dhmānam ca kṛtvā śaṅkha bherī ninādaiḥ ca vijaya abhiśaṃsinam ghoṣam ca akārayat tataḥ tam ghoṣam ākarṇya sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ pārtha sārathī rathī ca pāṇḍu tanayaḥ trailokya vijaya upakaraṇa bhūte mahati syandane sthitau trailokyam kampayantau śrīmat pāñcajanya devadattau divyau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ tataḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vṛkodara ādayaḥ ca svakīyān śaṅkhān pṛthak pṛthak pradadhmuḥ sa ghoṣaḥ duryodhana pramukhānām sarveṣām eva bhavat putrāṇām hṛdayāni bibheda adya eva naṣṭam kurūṇām balam iti dhārtarāṣṭrā menire evam tad vijayā abhikāṅkṣiṇe dhṛtarāṣṭrāya sañjayaḥ akathayat atha yuyutsūn avasthitān dhārtarāṣṭrān dṛṣṭvā laṅkā dahana vānara dhvajaḥ pāṇḍu tanayaḥ jñāna śakti balāi śvarya vīrya tejasām nidhim sva saṅkalpa kṛta jagat udaya vibhava laya līlam hṛṣīkeśam parāvara nikhila jana antara bāhya karaṇānām sarva prakāra niyamane avasthitam āśrita vātsalya vivaśa tayā sva sārathye avasthitam yuyutsūn yathāvat avekṣitum tad īkṣana kṣame sthāne ratham sthāpaya iti acodayat sa ca tena coditaḥ tad kṣaṇāt eva bhhīṣma ḍroṇa ādīnām sarveṣām eva mahīkṣitām paśyatām yathā coditam akarot īdṛśī bhavadīyānām vijaya sthitiḥ iti ca avocat sa tu pārthaḥ mahāmanāḥ parama kāruṇikaḥ dīrgha bandhuḥ parama dhārmikaḥ sa bhrātṛkaḥ bhavadbhiḥ ati ghoraiḥ māraṇaiḥ jatu gṛha dāha ādibhiḥ asakṛt vañcitaḥ api parama puruṣa sahāyena ātmanā haniṣya māṇān bhavadīyān vilokya bandhu snehena parayā kṛpayā dharma bhayena ca atimātra sanna sarva gātraḥ sarvathā aham na yotsyāmi iti uktvā bandhu viśleṣa janita śoka saṃvigna mānasaḥ sa śaram cāpam visṛjya rathopastha upāviśat evam upaviṣṭe pārthe kutaḥ ayam asthāne samupasthitaḥ śoka iti ākṣipya tam imam viṣama stham śokam avidvat sevitam para loka virodhinam akīrti karam ati kṣudram hṛdaya daurbalya kṛtam parityajya yuddhāya uttiṣṭha iti śrī bhagavān uvāca punar api pārthaḥ sneha kāruṇya dharma adharma bhaya ākulaḥ bhagavat uktam hitatamam ajānan  idam uvāca bhīṣma droṇa ādikān gurūn bahu mantavyān katham aham haniṣyāmi kathaṃtarām bhogeṣu atimātra saktān tān hatvā taiḥ bhujyamānān  tān eva bhogān tad rudhireṇa upasicya teṣu āsaneṣu upaviśya bhuñjīya evam yuddham ārabhya nivṛtta vyāpārān bhavataḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ prasahya hanyuḥ iti ced astu tad vadha labdha vijayāt adharmyāt asmākam dharma adharmau  ajānadbhiḥ taiḥ hananam eva garīya iti me pratibhāti iti uktvā yad mahyam śreya iti niścitam tad śaraṇa āgatāya tava śiṣyāya me brūhi iti atimātra kṛpaṇaḥ bhagavat pādau  upasasāda evam asthāne samupasthita sneha kāruṇyābhyām aprakṛtim gatam kṣatriyāṇām yuddham parama dharmam api adharmam manvānam dharma bubhutsayā ca śaraṇa āgatam pārtham uddiśya ātmayāthātmya jñānena yuddhasya phala abhisandhirahitasya ātma prāpti upāyatā jñānena ca vinā asya mohaḥ na śāmyati iti matvā bhagavatā parama puruṣeṇa adhyātma śāstra avataraṇam kṛtam tad uktam sthāna sneha kāruṇya dharma adharma dhiyā ākulam pārtham prapannam uddiśya śāstra avataraṇam kṛtam iti evam deha ātmanā ūr yāthātmya ajñāna nimitta śoka āviṣṭam deha atirikta ātma jñāna nimittam ca dharmam bhāṣamāṇam paraspara viruddha guṇa anvitam ubhayoḥ senayoḥ yuddhāya udyuktayoḥ madhye akasmāt nirudyogam pārtham ālokya parama puruṣaḥ prahasan  iva idam uvāca parihāsa vākyam vadan  iva ātma paramātma yāthātmya tad prāpti upāya bhūta karma yoga jñāna yoga bhakti yoga gocaram na tu eva aham jātu na asam iti ārabhya aham tvā sarva pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ iti etad antam vacanam uvāca iti arthaḥ aśocyān prati anuśocasi patanti pitaraḥ hi eṣām lupta piṇḍa udaka kriyāḥ iti ādikān deha ātma svabhāva prajñā nimitta vāda an  ca bhāṣase deha ātma svabhāva jñānavatām na atra kiṃcid choka nimittam asti gatāsūn dehān agatāsūn ātmanaḥ ca prati tad svabhāva yāthātmya vidaḥ na śocanti ataḥ tvayi vipratiṣiddham idam upalabhyate yad etān haniṣyāmi iti anuśocanam yad ca deha atirikta ātma jñāna kṛtam dharma adharma bhāṣaṇam ataḥ deha svabhāvam ca na jānāsi tad atiriktam ātmānam ca nityam tad prāpti upāya bhūtam yuddha ādikam dharmam ca idam ca yuddham phala abhisandhi rahitam ātmayāthātmya avāpti upāya bhūtam ātmā hi na janma adhīna sadbhāvaḥ na maraṇa adhīna vināśa ḥ ca tasya janma maraṇayoḥ abhāvāt ataḥ sa na śoka sthānam dehaḥ tu acetanaḥ pariṇāma svabhāvaḥ tasya utpatti vināśa yogaḥ svābhāvika iti saḥ api na śoka sthānam iti abhiprāyaḥ prathamam tāvat ātmanām svabhāvam śṛṇu aham sarva īśvara ḥ tāvat ataḥ vartamānāt pūrvasmin anādau kāle na nāsam api tu āsam tvad mukhāḥ ca ete īśitavyāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ na nāsam api tu āsan aham ca yūyam ca sarve vayam ataḥ parasmin anante kāle na ca eva na bhaviṣyāmaḥ api tu bhaviṣyāma eva yathā aham sarva īśvaraḥ paramātmā nitya iti na atra saṃśayaḥ tathā eva bhavantaḥ kṣetrajñā ātmānaḥ api nityā eva iti mantavyāḥ evam bhagavataḥ sarva īśvara āt atmanām parasparam ca bhedaḥ pāramārthika iti bhagavatā eva uktam iti pratīyate ajñāna mohitam prati tad nivṛttaye pārma arthika nitya tva upadeśa samaye aham tvam ime sarve vayam iti vyapadeśāt aupacārika ātma bheda vāde hi ātma bhedasya atāttvika tvena tattva upadeśa samaye bheda nirdeśaḥ na saṃgacchate bhagavat ukta ātma bhedaḥ svābhāvika iti śrutiḥ api āha nityaḥ nityānām cetanaḥ cetanānām ekaḥ bahūnām yaḥ vidadhāti kāmān  iti nityānām bahūnām cetanānām ya ekaḥ nityaḥ cetanaḥ san kāmān vidadhāti iti arthaḥ ajñāna kṛta bheda dṛṣṭi vāde tu parama puruṣasya parama artha dṛṣteḥ nirviśeṣa kūṭa stha nitya caitanya ātma yāthātmya sākṣātkārān nivṛtta ajñāna tad kārya tayā ajñāna kṛta bheda darśanam tad mūla upadeśa ādi vyavahārāḥ ca na saṃgacchante atha parama puruṣasya adhigatāt vaita jñānasya bādhita anuvṛtti rūpam idam bheda jñānam dagdha paṭa ādivan na bandhakam iti ucyate na etad upapadyate marīcikā jala jñāna ādikam hi bādhitam anuvartamānam na jala āharaṇa ādi pravṛtti hetuḥ evam atra api advaita jñānena bādhitam bheda jñānam anuvartamānam api mithyā artha viṣaya tva niścayān na upadeśa ādi pravṛtti hetuḥ bhavati na ca īśvarasya pūrvam ajñasya śāstra adhigata tattva jñāna tayā bādhita anuvṛttiḥ śakyate vaktum yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva vit  parāsya śaktiḥ vividhā eva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñāna bala kriyā ca  veda aham samatītāni vartamānāni ca arjuna bhaviṣyāṇi ca bhūtāni mām tu veda na kaścana iti śruti smṛti virodhāt kim ca parama puruṣaḥ ca idānīṃtana guru paramparā ca advitīya ātma svarūpa niścaye sati anuvartamāne api bheda jñāne sva niścaya anurūpam advitīya ātma jñānam kasmā upadiśati iti vaktavyam pratibimbavat pratīyamānebhyaḥ arjuna ādibhya iti ced na etad upapadyate na hi anunmattaḥ kaḥ api maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādiṣu pratīyamāneṣu sva ātma pratibimbeṣu teṣām sva ātmanaḥ ananya tvam jānan tebhyaḥ kim api upadiśati bādhita anuvṛttiḥ api taiḥ na śakyate vaktum bādhakena advitīya ātma jñānena ātma vyatirikta bheda jñāna kāraṇasya anādeḥ vinaṣṭa tvāt dvi candra jñāna ādau tu candra eka tva jñānena pāramārthika timira ādi doṣasya dvi candra jñāna hetoḥ avinaṣṭa tvāt bādhita anuvṛttiḥ yuktā anuvartamānam api prabala pramāṇa bādhita tvena akiṃcitkaram iha tu bheda jñānasya sa viṣayasya sa kāraṇasya apāramārthika tvena vastu yāthātmya jñāna vinaṣṭa tvān na kathañcid api bādhita anuvṛttiḥ saṃbhavati ataḥ sarva īśvarasya idānīṃtana guru paramparāya āḥ ca tattva jñānam asti ced bheda darśana tad kārya upadeśa ādi asaṃbhavaḥ na asti ced ajñānasya tad hetoḥ sthita tvena ajña tvāt eva sutarām upadeśaḥ na saṃbhavati kim ca guroḥ advitīya ātma vijñānāt eva brahma ajñānasya sa kāryasya vinaṣṭa tvāt śiṣyam praty upadeśaḥ niṣprayojanaḥ guruḥ tad jñānam ca kalpitam iti ced śiṣya tad jñānayoḥ api kalpita tvāt tad api anivartakam kalpita tve api pūrva virodhi tvena nivartakam iti ced tad acārya jñāne api samānam iti tad eva nivartakam bhavati iti upadeśa ānarthakyam eva iti kṛtam asamīcīnavādaiḥ ekasmin dehe vartamānasya dehinaḥ kaumāra avasthām vihāya yauvana ādi avasthā prāptau ātmanaḥ sthira tva buddhyā yathā ātmā naṣṭa iti na śocati dehāt deha antara prāptau  api tathā eva sthira ātmā iti buddhimān na śocati ata ātmanām nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ na śoka sthānam etāvat atra kartavyam ātmanām nityānām eva anādi karma vaśya tayā tad tad karma ucita deha saṃsṛṣṭānām taiḥ eva dehaiḥ bandha nivṛttaye śāstrī iyam sva varṇa ucitam yuddha ādikam anabhisaṃhita phalam karma kurvatām avarjanīya tayā indriyaiḥ indriya artha sparśāḥ śīta uṣṇa ādi prayukta sukha duḥkha dā bhavanti te tu yāvat śāstrīya karma samāpti kṣantavyā iti imam artham anantaram eva āha śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāḥ sa āśrayāḥ tanmātrā kārya tvān mātrā iti ucyante śrotra ādibhiḥ teṣām sparśāḥ śīta uṣṇa mṛdu paruṣa ādi rūpa sukha duḥkha dāḥ bhavanti śīta uṣṇa śabdaḥ pradarśana arthaḥ tān dhairyeṇa yāvat yuddha ādi śāstrīya karma samāpti titikṣasva te ca āgama apāyi tvāt dhairyavatām kṣantum yogyāḥ anityāḥ ca te bandha hetu bhūta karma nāśe sati āgama apāyi tvena api na vartante iti arthaḥ tad kṣamā kimartha iti atra āha yam puruṣam dhairya yuktam avarjanīya duḥkham sukhavan manyamānam amṛta tva sādhana tayā sva varṇa ucitam yuddha ādi karma anabhisaṃhita phalam kurvāṇam tad antargatāḥ śastra pāta ādi mṛdu krūra sparśāḥ na vyathayanti sa eva amṛta tvam sādhayati na tvādṛśaḥ duḥkha asahiṣṇuḥ iti arthaḥ ātmanām nitya tvāt etāvat atra kartavyam iti arthaḥ yad tu ātmanām nitya tvam dehānām svābhāvikam nāśi tvam ca śoka animittam uktam gata asūn agatāsūnḥ ca na anuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ iti tad upapādayitum ārabhate asataḥ dehasya sadbhāvaḥ na vidyate sataḥ ca ātmanaḥ na asadbhāvaḥ ubhayoḥ deha ātmanā ūr upalabhyamānayoḥ yathā upalabdhi tattva darśibhiḥ antaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ nirṇaya antatvān nirūpaṇasya nirṇaya iha anta śabdena ucyate dehasya acit vastunaḥ asattvam eva svarūpam ātmanaḥ cetanasya sattvam eva svarūpam iti nirṇayaḥ dṛṣṭa iti arthaḥ vināśa svabhāvaḥ hi asattvam avināśa svabhāva ḥ ca sattvam yathā uktam bhagavatā parāśareṇa tasmāt na vijñānam ṛte asti kiṃcid kvacid kadācid dvija vastu jātam  sadbhāva evam bhavataḥ mayā uktaḥ jñānam yathā satyam asatyam anyat  anāśī parama artha ḥ ca prājñaiḥ abhyupagamyate tad tu nāśi na saṃdehaḥ nāśidravya upapāditam  yad tu kāla antareṇa api na anya saṃjñām upaiti vai pariṇāma ādi saṃbhūtām tad vastu nṛpa tad ca kim iti atra api antavanta ime dehāḥ  avināśi tu tad viddhi iti hi ucyate tad eva sattva asattva vyapadeśa hetuḥ iti gamyate atra tu satkārya vādasya aprastuta tvān na tad paraḥ ayam ślokaḥ deha ātma svabhāva ajñāna mohitasya tad moha śāntaye hi ubhayoḥ nāśitvā nāśi tva rūpa svabhāva viveka eva vaktavyaḥ sa eva gata asūn agatāsūn  iti ca prastutaḥ sa eva ca avināśi tu tad viddhi  antavanta ime dehāḥ iti anantaram upapādyate ataḥ yathā ukta eva arthaḥ ātmanaḥ tu avināśi tvam katham avagamyata iti atra āha tad atma tattvam avināśī iti viddhi yena ātma tattvena cetanena tad vyatiriktam idam acetana tattvam sarvam tatam vyāptam vyāpaka tvena niratiśaya sūkṣma tvāt ātmanaḥ vināśān arhasya tad vyatiriktaḥ na kaścid padārthaḥ vināśam kartum arhati tad vyāpya tayā tasmāt sthūla tvāt nāśakam hi śastra jala agni vāyu ādikam nāśyam vyāpya śithilīkaroti mudrā ādayaḥ api hi vegavat saṃyogena vāyum utpādya tad dvāreṇa nāśayanti ata ātma tattvam avināśi dehānām tu vināśi tvam eva svabhāva iti āha diha upacaye iti upacaya rūpā ime dehā antavantaḥ vināśa svabhāvāḥ upacaya ātmakā hi ghaṭa ādayaḥ antavantaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ nityasya śarīriṇaḥ karma phala bhoga artha tayā bhūta saṃghāta rūpā dehāḥ puṇyaḥ puṇyena ityādi śāstraiḥ uktāḥ karma avasāna vināśinaḥ ātmā tu avināśī kutaḥ aprameya tvāt na hi ātmā prameyatayā upalabhyate api tu pramātṛ tayā tathā ca vakṣyate etad yaḥ vetti tam prāhuḥ kṣetrajña iti tad vidaḥ iti na ca aneka upacaya ātmaka ātma upalabhayate sarvatra dehe aham idam jānāmi iti dehasya ca anyasya ca pramātṛ tayā eka rūpeṇa upalabdheḥ na ca deha ādeḥ iva pradeśa bhede pramātuḥ ākāra bheda upalabhyate ata eka rūpa tvena anupacaya ātmaka tvāt pramātṛ tvāt vyāpaka tvāt ca ātmā nityaḥ dehaḥ tu upacaya ātmaka tvāt śarīriṇaḥ karma phala bhoga artha tvāt aneka rūpa tvāt vyāpya tvāt ca vināśī tasmāt dehasya vināśa svabhāva tvāt atmanaḥ nitya tvāt ca ubhayau  api na śoka sthānam iti śastra pāta ādi puruṣa sparśān avarjanīyān sva gatān anya gatān  ca ghairyeṇa soḍhvā amṛta tva prāptaye anabhisaṃhita phalam yuddha ākhyam karma ārabhasva enam ukta svabhāvam ātmānam prati hantāram hanana hetum kam api yaḥ manyate yaḥ ca enam kena api hetunā hatam manyate tau  ubhau na vijānītaḥ uktaiḥ hetubhiḥ asya nitya tvāt eva enam ayam na hanti asya ayam hanana hetuḥ na bhavati ata eva ca ayam ātmā na hanyate hantidhātuḥ api ātma karmakaḥ śarīra viyoga karaṇa vācī na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtāni  brāhmaṇaḥ na hantavyaḥ ityādīni api śāstrāṇi avihita śarīra viyoga karaṇa viṣayāṇi uktaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ nitya tvena apariṇāmi tvāt ātmanaḥ janana maraṇa ādayaḥ sarva eva acetana deha dharmā na santi iti ucyate tatra jāyate mriyate iti vartamāna tayā sarveṣu deheṣu sarvaiḥ anubhūyamāne janana maraṇe kadācid api ātmānam na spṛśataḥ na ayam bhūtvā bhavitā vā na bhūyaḥ ayam kalpa ādau bhūtvā bhūyaḥ kalpa ante ca na na bhavitā keṣucid prajāpati prabhṛti deheṣu āgamena upalabhyamānam kalpa ādau jananam kalpa ante ca maraṇam ātmānam na spṛśati iti arthaḥ ataḥ sarva deha gata ātmā ajaḥ ata eva nityaḥ śāśvataḥ prakṛtivat aviśada satata pariṇāmaiḥ api na anvīyate purāṇaḥ purā api navaḥ sarvadā apūrvavat anubhāvya iti arthaḥ ataḥ śarīre hanyamāne na hanyate ayam ātmā evam avināśi tvena aja tvena vyayān arha tvena ca nityam enam ātmānam yaḥ puruṣaḥ veda sa puruṣaḥ deva manuṣya tiryak sthāvara śarīra avasthiteṣu ātmasu kam api ātmānam katham ghātayati kam vā katham hanti katham nāśayati katham vā tad prayojakaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ etān ātmanaḥ ghātayāmi hanmi iti anuśocanam ātma svarūpa yāthātmya ajñāna mūlam eva iti abhiprāyaḥ yadi api nityānām ātmanām śarīra viśleṣa mātram kriyate tathā api ramaṇīya bhoga sādhaneṣu śarīreṣu naśyatsu tad viyoga rūpam śoka nimittam asti eva iti atra āha dharma yuddhe śarīram tyajatām tyakta śarīrāt adhikatara kalyāṇa śarīra grahaṇam śāstra ād avagamyata iti jīrṇāni vāsāṃsi vihāya navāni kalyāṇāni vāsāṃsi gṛhṇatām iva harṣa nimittam eva atra upalabhyate punar api avināśi tu tad viddhi yena sarvam idam tatam iti pūrva uktam avināśi tvam sukha grahaṇāya vyañjayan draḍhayati śastra agni ambu vāyavaḥ chedana dahana kledana śoṣaṇāni ātmānam prati kartum na śaknuvanti sarva gata tvāt ātmanaḥ sarva tattva vyāpana svabhāvatayā sarvebhyaḥ tattvebhyaḥ sūkṣma tvāt asya taiḥ vyāpti anarha tvāt vyāpya kartavya tvāt ca chedana dahana kledana śoṣaṇānām ata ātmā nityaḥ sthāṇuḥ acalaḥ ayam sanātanaḥ sthira svabhāvaḥ aprakampyaḥ purātanaḥ ca chedana ādi yogyāni vastūni yaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ vyajyante taiḥ ayam ātmā na vyajyata iti avyaktaḥ ataḥ chedya ādi visajātīyaḥ acintya ḥ ca sarva vastu vijātīya tvena tad tad svabhāva yukta tayā cintayitum api na arhaḥ ataḥ ca avikāryaḥ vikārān arhaḥ tasmāt ukta lakṣaṇam enam ātmānam viditvā tad kṛte na anuśocitum arhasi atha nitya jātam nitya mṛtam deham eva enam ātmānam manuṣe na deha atiriktam ukta lakṣaṇam tathā api evam atimātram na śocitum arhasi pariṇāma svabhāvasya dehasya utpatti vināśayoḥ avarjanīya tvāt utpannasya vināśaḥ dhruvaḥ avarjanīya upalabhyate tathā vinaṣṭasya api janma avarjanīyam katham idam upapadyate vinaṣṭasya utpattiḥ iti sata eva utpatti upalabdheḥ asataḥ ca anupalabdheḥ utpatti vināśa ādayaḥ sataḥ dravyasya avasthā viśeṣāḥ tantu prabhṛtīni hi dravyāṇi santi eva racanā viśeṣa yuktāni paṭa ādīni ucyante asat kārya vādinā api etāvat eva upalabhyate na hi tatra tantu saṃsthāna viśeṣa atirekeṇa dravya antaram pratīyate kāraka vyāpāra nāma antara bhajana vyavahāra viśeṣāṇām etāvatā eva upapatteḥ na dravya antara kalpanā yuktā ataḥ utpatti vināśa ādayaḥ sataḥ dravyasya avasthā viśeṣāḥ utpatti ākhyām avasthām upayātasya dravyasya tad virodhi avasthā antara prāptiḥ vināśa iti ucyate mṛd dravyasya piṇḍa tva ghaṭa tva kapāla tva cūrṇa tva ādivat  pariṇāmi dravyasya pariṇāma paramparā avarjanīyā tatra pūrva avasthasya dravyasya uttara avasthā prāptiḥ vināśaḥ sā eva tad avasthasya ca utpattiḥ evam utpatti vināśa ākhya pariṇāma paramparā pariṇāminaḥ dravyasya aparihārya iti na tatra śocitum arhasi sataḥ dravyasya pūrva avasthā virodhi avasthā antara prāpti darśanena yaḥ alpīyān śokaḥ saḥ api manuṣya ādi bhūteṣu na saṃbhavati iti āha manuṣya ādīni bhūtāni santi eva dravyāṇi anupalabdha pūrva avasthāni upalabdha manuṣya tva ādi madhyamā avasthāni anupalabdha uttara avasthāni sveṣu svabhāveṣu vartanta iti na tatra paridevanā nimittam asti evam śarīra ātma vāde api na asti śoka nimittam iti uktvā śarīra atirikte āścarya svarūpe ātmani draṣṭā vaktā śravaṇa āyatta ātma niścayaḥ ca durlabha iti āha evam ukta svabhāvam sva itara samasta vastu visajātīya tayā āścaryavat  asthitam ananteṣu jantuṣu mahatā tapasā kṣīṇa pāpaḥ upacita puṇyaḥ kaścid paśyati tathāvidhaḥ kaścid parasmai vadati evam kaścid eva śṛṇoti śrutvā api enam yathāvat avasthitam tattvataḥ na kaścid veda cakārāt draṣṭṛ vaktṛ śrotṛṣv api tattvataḥ darśanam tattvataḥ vacanam tattvata ḥ śravaṇam durlabham iti uktam bhavati sarvasya deva ādi dehinaḥ dehe vadhyamāne api ayam dehī nityam avadhyaḥ mantavyaḥ tasmāt sarvāṇi deva ādi sthāvara antāni bhūtāni viṣama ākārāṇi api uktena svabhāvena svarūpataḥ samānāni nityāni ca deha gatam tu vaiṣamyam anitya tvam ca tataḥ deva ādīni sarvāṇi bhūtāni uddiśya na śocitum arhasi na kevalam bhīṣma ādīn prati api ca idam prārabdham yuddham prāṇi māraṇam api agnīṣomīya ādivat  svadharmam avekṣya na vikampitum arhasi dharmyān nyāyataḥ pravṛttāt yuddhāt anyan na hi kṣatriyasya śreyaḥ vidyate śauryam tejaḥ dhṛtiḥ dākṣyam yuddhe ca api apalāyanam dānam īśvara bhāvaḥ ca kṣātram karma svabhāva jam  iti hi vakṣyate agnīṣomīya ādiṣu ca na hiṃsā paśoḥ nihīna tara chāga ādi deha parityāga pūrvaka kalyāṇatara deha svarga ādi prāpaka tva śruteḥ saṃjñapanasya na vā u etad mriyase na riṣyasi devām ideṣi pathibhiḥ surebhiḥ yatra yanti sukṛtaḥ na api duṣkṛtaḥ tatra tvā devaḥ savitā dadhātu iti hi śrūyate iha ca yuddhe mṛtānām kalyāṇatara deha prāptiḥ uktā vāsāṃsi jīrṇāni yathā vihāya navāni gṛhṇāti ityādinā ataḥ cikitsaka śalya ādi karma āturasya iva asya rakṣaṇam eva agnīṣomīya ādiṣu saṃjñapanam ayatna upanatam idam niratiśaya sukha upāya bhūtam nirvighnam īdṛśam yuddham sukhinaḥ puṇyavantaḥ kṣatriyā labhante atha kṣatriyasya svadharma bhūtam imam ārabdham saṃgrāmam mohān na kariṣyasi ced tataḥ prārabdhasya dharmasya akaraṇāt svadharma phalam niratiśaya sukham vijayena niratiśayām ca kīrtim hitvā pāpam niratiśayam avāpsyasi na te kevalam niratiśaya sukha kīrti hāni mātram pārthaḥ yuddhe prārabdhe palāyitaḥ iti avyayām sarva deśa kāla vyāpinīm akīrtim ca samarthāni asamarthāni api sarvāṇi bhūtāni kathayiṣyanti tataḥ kim iti ced śairya vīrya parākrama ādibhiḥ sarva saṃbhāvitasya tad viparyaya jā hi akīrtiḥ maraṇāt atiricyate evaṃvidhāyā akīrteḥ maraṇam eva tava śreya iti arthaḥ bandhu snehāt kāruṇyāt ca yuddhān nivṛttasya śūrasya mama akīrtiḥ katham āgamiṣyati iti atra āha yeṣām karṇa duryodhana ādīnām mahā rathānām itaḥ pūrvam tvam śūraḥ vairī iti bahu mataḥ bhūtvā idānīm yuddhe samupasthite nivṛtta vyāpāra tayā lāghavam sugraha tām yāsyasi te mahā ratha aḥ tvām bhayāt yuddhāt uparatam maṃsyante śūrāṇām hi vairiṇām śatru bhayāt rte bandhu sneha ādinā yuddhāt uparatiḥ na upapadyate kim ca śūrāṇām asmākam sannidhau katham ayam pārthaḥ kṣaṇam api sthātum śaknuyāt asmad sannidhānāt anyatra hi asya sāmarthyam iti tava sāmarthyam nindantaḥ śūrāṇām avācya vādān  ca bahūn vadiṣyanti tava śatravaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ tataḥ adhikataram duḥkham kim tava evaṃvidha avācya śravaṇān maraṇam eva śreya iti tvam eva maṃsyase ataḥ śūrasya ātmanā pareṣām hananam ātmanaḥ vā paraiḥ hananam ubhayam api śreyase bhavati iti āha dharma yuddhe paraiḥ hata ḥ ced tataḥ eva parama niḥśreyasam prāpsyasi parān vā hatvā akaṇṭakam rājyam bhokṣyase anabhisaṃhita phalasya yuddha ākhyasya dharmasya parama niḥśreyasa upāya tvāt tad ca parama niḥśreyasam prāpsyasi tasmāt yuddhāya udyogaḥ parama puruṣa artha lakṣaṇa mokṣa sādhanam iti niścitya tad artham uttiṣṭha kuntī putrasya tava etad eva yuktam iti abhiprāyaḥ mumukṣoḥ yuddha anuṣṭhāna prakāram āha evam deha atiriktam aspṛṣṭa samasta deha svabhāvam nityam ātmānam jñātvā yuddhe ca āvarjanīya śastra pāta ādi nimitta sukha duḥkha artha lābha ālābha jaya parājayeṣu avikṛta buddhiḥ svarga ādi phala abhisandhi rahitaḥ kevala kārya buddhyā yuddham ārabhasva evam kurvāṇaḥ na pāpam avāpsyasi pāpam duḥkha rūpam saṃsāram na avāpsyasi saṃsāra bandhān mokṣyase iti arthaḥ evam ātma yāthātmya jñānam upadiśya tad pūrvakam mokṣa sādhana bhūtam karma yogam vaktum ārabhate saṅkhyā buddhiḥ buddhyā avadhāraṇīyam ātma tattvam sāṅkhyam jñātavye ātma tattve tad jñānāya yā buddhiḥ abhidheyā na tu eva aham iti ārabhya tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni na tvam śocitum arhasi iti antena sā eṣā te abhihitā ātma jñāna pūrvaka mokṣa sādhana bhūta karma anuṣṭhāne yaḥ buddhi yogaḥ vaktavyaḥ sa iha yoga śabdena ucyate dūreṇa hi avaram karma buddhi yogāt iti hi vakṣyate tatra yoge yā buddhiḥ vaktavyā tām imām abhidhīyamānām śṛṇu yayā buddhyā yuktaḥ karma bandham prahāsyasi karmaṇā bandhaḥ karma bandhaḥ saṃsāra bandha iti arthaḥ vakṣyamāṇa buddhi yuktasya karmaṇaḥ māhātmyam āha iha karma yoge na abhikrama nāśaḥ asti abhikramaḥ ārambhaḥ nāśaḥ phala sādhana bhāva nāśaḥ ārabdhasya asamāptasya vicchinnasya api na niṣphala tvam ārabdhasya vicchede pratyavāyaḥ api na vidyate asya karma yoga ākhyasya dharmasya su alpa aṃśa u api mahataḥ bhayāt saṃsāra bhayāt trāyate ayam arthaḥ pārtha na eva iha na amutra vināśa ḥ tasya vidyate iti uttaratra prapañcayiṣyate anyāni hi laukikāni vaidikāni ca sādhanāni vicchinnāni na phalāya bhavanti pratyavāyāya ca bhavanti kāmya karma viṣayāyā buddheḥ mokṣa sādhana bhūta karma viṣayām buddhim viśinaṣṭi iha śāstrīye sarvasmin karmaṇi vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ ekā mumukṣuṇā anuṣṭheye karmaṇi buddhiḥ vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ vyavasāyaḥ niścayaḥ sā hi buddhiḥ ātma yāthātmya niścaya pūrvikā kāmya karma viṣayā tu buddhiḥ avyavasāya ātmikā tatra hi kāma adhikāre deha atirikta ātmā astitva jñāna mātram apekṣitam na ātma svarūpa yāthātmya niścayaḥ svarūpa yāthātmyā niścaye api svarga ādi phala arthi tva tad sādhana anuṣṭhāna tad phala anubhavānām saṃbhavāt avirodhāt ca sā iyam vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ eka phala sādhana viṣaya tayā ekā ekasmai mokṣa ākhya phalāya hi mumukṣoḥ sarvāṇi karmāṇi vidhīyante ataḥ śāstra arthasya eka tvāt sarva karma viṣayā buddhiḥ ekā eva yathā eka phala sādhana tayā āgneya ādīnām ṣaṇṇām sa iti kartavya tākānām eka śāstra artha tayā tad viṣayā buddhiḥ ekā tadvat iti arthaḥ avyavasāyinām tu svarga putra paśu anna ādi phala sādhana karma adhikṛtānām buddhayaḥ phala ānantyāt anantāḥ tatra api bahu śākhāḥ ekasmai phalāya codite api darśa pūrṇamāsa ādau karmaṇiāyuḥ āśāḥ te iti ādi avagatauvāntara phala bhedena bahu śākha tvam ca vidyate ataḥ avyavasāyinām buddhayaḥ anantā bahu śākhāḥ ca etad uktam bhavati nityeṣu naimittikeṣu karmasu pradhāna phalāni avāntara phalāni ca yāni śrūyamāṇāni tāni sarvāṇi parityajya mokṣa eka phala tayā sarvāṇi karmāṇi eka śāstra artha tayā anuṣṭheyāni kāmyāni ca sva varṇa āśrama ucitāni tad tad phalāni parityajya mokṣa sādhana tayā nitya naimittikaiḥ ekīkṛtya yathābalam anuṣṭheyāni iti atha kāmya karma adhikṛtān nindati yām imām puṣpitām puṣpa mātra phalām āpāta ramaṇīyām vācam avipaścitaḥ alpa jñāḥ bhogāi śvarya gatim prati vartamānām pravadanti veda vāda ratāḥ vedeṣu ye svarga ādi phala vādāḥ teṣu saktāḥ na anyat asti iti vādinaḥ tad saṅga atirekeṇa svarga ādeḥ adhikam phalam na anyat asti iti vadantaḥ kām ātmānaḥ kām apravaṇa manasaḥ svarga parāḥ svarga parāyaṇāḥ svarga ādi phala avasāne punar janma karma ākhya phala pradām kriyā viśeṣa bahulām tattva jñāna rahita tayā kriyā viśeṣa pracurām bhogāi śvarya gatim prati vartamānām yām imām puṣpitām vācam ye pravadanti iti saṃbandhaḥ teṣām bhogāi śvarya prasaktānām tayā vācā bhogāi śvarya viṣayayā apahṛta jñānānām yathā udita vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ samādhau manasi na vidhīyate na utpadyate samādhīyate asmin  ātma jñānam iti samādhiḥ manaḥ teṣām manasi ātmayāthātmya niścaya pūrvaka mokṣa sādhana bhūta karma viṣayā buddhiḥ kadācid api na utpadyate iti arthaḥ ataḥ kāmyeṣu karmasu mumukṣuṇā na saṅgaḥ kartavyaḥ evam ati alpa phalāni punar janma prasavāni karmāṇi mātā pitṛ sahasrebhyaḥ api vatsalatara tayā ātma ujjīvane pravṛttā vedāḥ kim artham vadanti katham vā veda uditam tyājyatayā ucyate iti ata āha trayaḥ guṇa aḥ traiguṇyam sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi sattva rajaḥ tamaḥ pracurāḥ puruṣāḥ traiguṇya śabdena ucyante tad viṣayā vedāḥ tamaḥ pracurāṇām rajaḥ pracurāṇām sattva pracurāṇām ca vatsalatara tayā eva hitam avabodhayanti vedāḥ yadi eṣām sva guṇa anuguṇyena svarga ādi sādhanam eva hitam na avabodhayanti tadā ete rajaḥ tamaḥ pracura tayā sāttvika phala mokṣa vimukhāḥ svāpekṣita phala sādhanam ajānantaḥ kāma prāvaṇya vivaśā anupādeyeṣu upādeya bhrāntyā praviṣṭāḥ pranaṣṭā bhaveyuḥ ataḥ traiguṇya viṣayā vedāḥ tvam tu nistraiguṇyaḥ bhava idānīm sattva pracuraḥ tvam tad eva vardhaya na anyonya saṅkīrṇa guṇatraya pracuraḥ bhava na tad prācuryam vardhaya iti arthaḥ nirdvandvaḥ nirgata sakala sāṃsārika svabhāvaḥ nitya sattva sthaḥ guṇa dvaya rahita nitya pravṛddha sattva sthaḥ bhava katham iti ced niryogakṣemaḥ ātma svarūpa tad prāpti upāya bahiḥ bhūtānām arthānām yogam prāptānām ca kṣemam parityajya ātmavān bhava ātma svarūpān veṣaṇa paraḥ bhava aprāptasya prāptiḥ yogaḥ prāptasya parikṣaṇam kṣemaḥ evam vartamānasya te rajaḥ tamaḥ pracura tā naśyati sattvam ca vardhate na ca veda uditam sarvam sarvasya upādeyam yathā sarva artha parikalpite sarvataḥ saṃpluta udake udapāne pipāsoḥ yāvān arthaḥ yāvat eva prayojanam tāvat eva tena upādīyate na sarvam evam sarveṣu ca vedeṣu brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥ vaidikasya mumukṣoḥ yad eva mokṣa sādhanam tad eva u pādeyam na anyat ataḥ sattva sthasya mumukṣoḥ etāvat eva upādeyam iti āha nitye naimittike kāmye ca kenacid phala viśeṣeṇa saṃbandhi tayā śrūyamāṇe karmaṇi nitya sattva sthasya mumukṣoḥ te karma mātre adhikāraḥ tad saṃbandhi tayā avagateṣu phaleṣu na kadācid api adhikāraḥ saphalasya bandha rūpa tvāt phala rahitasya kevalasya mad ārādhana rūpasya mokṣa hetu tvāc ca mā ca karma phalayoḥ hetu bhūḥ tvayā anuṣṭhīyamāne api karmaṇi nitya sattva sthasya mumukṣoḥ tava akartṛ tvam api anusandheyam phalasya api kṣut nivṛtti ādeḥ na tvam hetuḥ iti anusandheyam tad ubhayam guṇeṣu vā sarva īśvare mayi vā anusandheyam iti uttaratra vakṣyate evam anusandhāya karma kuru akarmaṇi ananuṣṭhāne na yotsyāmi iti yad tvayā abhihitam na tatra te saṅgaḥ astu uktena prakāreṇa yuddha ādi karmaṇi eva saṅgaḥ astu iti arthaḥ etad eva sphuṭīkaroti rājya bandhu prabhṛtiṣu saṅgam tyaktvā yuddha ādīni karmāṇi yoga sthaḥ kuru tad antarbhūta vijaya ādi siddhi asiddhyoḥ samaḥ bhūtvā kuru tad idam siddhi asiddhyoḥ sama tvam yoga stha iti atra yoga śabdena ucyate yogaḥ siddhi asiddhiyoḥ samatva rūpam citta samādhānam kim artham idam asakṛt ucyata iti ata āha yaḥ ayam pradhāna phala tyāga viṣayaḥ avāntara phala siddhi asiddhyoḥ sama tva viṣaya ḥ ca buddhi yogaḥ tad yuktāt karmaṇa itarat karma dūreṇa avaram mahat idam dvayoḥ utkarṣa apakarṣa rūpam vairūpyam ukta buddhi yoga yuktam karma nikhila sāṃsārika duḥkham vinivartya parama puruṣa artha lakṣaṇam ca mokṣam prāpayati itarat aparimita duḥkha rūpam saṃsāram iti ataḥ karmaṇi kriyamāṇe uktāyām buddhau śaraṇam anviccha śaraṇam vāsasthānam tasyām eva buddhau vartasva iti arthaḥ kṛpaṇāḥ phala hetavaḥ phala saṅga ādinā karma kurvāṇāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ saṃsāriṇaḥ bhaveyuḥ buddhi yoga yukta ḥ tu karma kurvāṇaḥ ubhe sukṛta duṣkṛte anādi kāla sañcite anante bandha hetu bhūte jahāti tasmāt uktāya buddhi yogāya yujyasva yogaḥ karmasu kauśalam karmasu kriyamāṇeṣu ayam buddhi yogaḥ kauśalam ati sāmarthyam ati sāmarthī sādhya iti arthaḥ buddhi yoga yuktāḥ karma jam phalam tyaktvā karma kurvantaḥ tasmāt janma bandha vinirmuktāḥ anāmayam padam gacchanti hi prasiddham hi etad sarvāsu upaniṣatsu iti arthaḥ ukta prakāreṇa karmaṇi vartamānasya tayā vṛttyā nirdhūta kalmaṣasya te buddhiḥ yadā moha kalilam ati alpa phala saṅga hetu bhūtam moha rūpam kaluṣam vyatitariṣyati tadā asmattaḥ itaḥ pūrvam tyājya tayā śrutasya phala ādeḥ itaḥ paścāt śrotavyasya ca kṛte svayam eva nirvedam gantāsi gamiṣyasi yoge tu imām śṛṇu ityādinā uktasya ātma yāthātmya jñāna pūrvakasya buddhi viśeṣa saṃskṛtasya dharma anuṣṭhānasya lakṣa bhūtam yoga ākhyam phalam āha śrutiḥ śravaṇam asmattaḥ śravaṇena viśeṣataḥ pratipannā sakala itara visajātīya nitya niratiśaya sūkṣma tattva ātma viṣayā svayam acalā eka rūpā buddhiḥ asaṅga karma anuṣṭhānena nirmalīkṛte manasi yadā niścalā sthāsyati tadā yogam ātma avalokanam avāpsyasi etad uktam bhavati śāstra janya ātma jñāna pūrvaka karma yogaḥ sthita prajña tā ākhya jñāna niṣṭhām āpādayati jñāna niṣṭhā rūpā sthita prajña tā tu yoga ākhyam ātma avalokanam sādhayati iti etad uktaḥ pārthaḥ asaṅga karma anuṣṭhāna rūpa karma yoga sādhya sthita prajña tāyāḥ yoga sādhana bhūtāyāḥ svarūpam sthita prajñasya anuṣṭhāna prakāram ca pṛcchati samādhi sthasya sthita prajñasya kā bhāṣā kaḥ vācakaḥ śabdaḥ tasya svarūpam kīdṛśam iti arthaḥ sthita prajñaḥ kim ca bhāṣā ādikam karoti vṛtti viśeṣa kathanena svarūpam api uktam bhavati iti vṛtti viśeṣa ucyate ātmani eva ātmanā manasā ātmā eka avalambanena tuṣṭaḥ tena toṣeṇa tad vyatiriktān sarvān manaḥ gatān kāmān yadā prakarṣeṇa jahāti tadā ayam sthita prajña iti ucyate jñāna niṣṭhā kāṣṭheyam anantaram jñāna niṣṭhasya tataḥ arvācī nādūra viprakṛṣṭa avasthā ucyate priya viśleṣa ādi duḥkha nimitteṣu upasthiteṣu anudvigna manāḥ na duḥkhī bhavati sukheṣu vigata spṛhaḥ priyeṣu sannihiteṣu api vigata spṛhaḥ vīta rāga bhaya krodhaḥ anāgateṣu spṛhā rāgaḥ tad rahitaḥ priya viśleṣa apriya āgamana hetu darśana nimittam duḥkham bhayam tad rahitaḥ priya viśleṣa apriya āgamana hetu bhūta cetana antara gata duḥkha hetu bhūta sva manaḥ vikāraḥ krodhaḥ tad rahitaḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ muniḥ ātma manana śīlaḥ sthita dhīr iti ucyate tataḥ arvā cīnadaśā procyate yaḥ sarvatra priyeṣu anabhisnehaḥ udāsīnaḥ priya saṃśleṣa viśleṣa rūpam śubha aśubham prāpya abhinandana dveṣa rahitaḥ saḥ api sthita prajñaḥ tataḥ arvā cīnadaśām āha yadā indriyāṇi indriya arthān spṛṣṭum udyuktāni tadā eva kūrmaḥ aṅgāni iva indriya arthebhyaḥ sarvaśaḥ pratisaṃhṛtya mana ātmani avasthāpayati saḥ api sthita prajñaḥ evam caturvidhā jñāna niṣṭhā pūrva pūrvā uttarottra niṣpādyā idānīm jñāna niṣṭhāyā duṣprāpatām tad prāpti upāyam ca āha indriyāṇām āhārā viṣayāḥ nirāhārasya viṣayebhyaḥ pratyāhṛta indriyasya dehinaḥ viṣayā vinivartamānā rasa varjam vinivartante rasaḥ rāgaḥ viṣaya rāgaḥ na nivartata iti arthaḥ rāgaḥ api ātma svarūpam viṣayebhyaḥ param sukhataram dṛṣṭvā nivartate ātma darśanena vinā viṣaya rāgaḥ na nivartate anivṛtte viṣaya rāge vipaścitaḥ yatamānasya api puruṣasya indriyāṇi pramāthīni balavanti manaḥ prasahya haranti evam indriya jayaḥ ātma darśana adhīnaḥ ātma darśanam indriya jaya adhīnam iti jñāna niṣṭhā duṣprāpā asya sarvasya parijihīrṣayā viṣaya anurāga yukta tayā durjayāni indriyāṇi saṃyamya cetasaḥ śubha āśraya bhūte mayi manaḥ avasthāpya samāhita āsīta manasi mad viṣaye sati nirdagdha aśeṣa kalmaṣa tayā nirmalīkṛtam viṣaya anurāga rahitam mana indriyāṇi sva vaśāni karoti tataḥ vaśya indriyam mana ātma darśanāya prabhavati yathā uktam yathā agniḥ uddhata śikhaḥ kakṣam dahati sa anilaḥ tathā citta sthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ yoginām sarva kilbiṣam  iti tad āha vaśe hi yasya indriyāṇi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā iti evam mayi aniveśya manaḥ sva yatna gauraveṇa indriya jaye pravṛttaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati iti āha anirasta viṣaya anurāgasya hi mayi aniveśita manasa indriyāṇi saṃyamya avasthitasya api anādi pāpa vāsanayā viṣaya dhyānam avarjanīyam syāt dhyāyataḥ viṣayān puṃsaḥ punar api saṅgaḥ atipravṛddhaḥ jāyate saṅgāt saṃjāte kāmaḥ kāmaḥ nāma saṅgasya vipāka daśā puruṣaḥ yām daśām āpannaḥ viṣayān abhuktvā sthātum na śaknoti sa kāmaḥ kāmāt krodhaḥ abhijāyate kāme vartamāne viṣaye ca āsannihite sannihitān puruṣān prati ebhiḥ asmat iṣṭam vihitam iti krodhaḥ bhavati krodhāt bhavati saṃmohaḥ saṃmohaḥ kṛtyā kṛtya viveka śūnyatā tayā sarvam karoti tataḥ ca prārabdhe indriya jaya ādike prayatne smṛti bhraṃśaḥ bhavati smṛti bhraṃśāt buddhi nāśaḥ ātma jñāne yaḥ vyavasāyaḥ kṛtaḥ tasya nāśaḥ syāt buddhi nāśāt punar api saṃsāre nimagnaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati uktena prakāreṇa mayi sarva īśvare cetasaḥ śubha āśraya bhūte nyasta manāḥ nirdagdha aśeṣa kalmaṣa tayā rāga dveṣa viyuktaiḥ ātma vaśyaiḥ indriyaiḥ viṣayāṃ  caran viṣayān  tiraskṛtya vartamānaḥ vidheya ātmā vidheya manāḥ prasādam adhigacchati nirmala antaḥkaraṇaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ asya puruṣasya manaḥ prasāde sati prakṛti saṃsarga prayukta sarva duḥkhānām hāniḥ upajāyate prasanna cetasaḥ ātma avalokana virodhi doṣa rahita manasaḥ tadānīm eva hi vivikta ātma viṣayā buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhate ataḥ manaḥ prasāde sarva duḥkhānām hāniḥ bhavati eva mayi sannyasta manorahitasya sva yatnena indriya niyamane pravṛttasya kadācid api vivikta ātma viṣayā buddhiḥ na setsyati ata eva tasya tad bhāvanā ca na saṃbhavati vivikta ātmānam abhāvayataḥ viṣaya spṛhā śāntiḥ na bhavati aśāntasya viṣaya spṛhā yuktasya kutaḥ nitya niratiśaya sukha prāptiḥ punar api uktena prakāreṇa indriya niyamanam akurvataḥ anartham āha indriyāṇām viṣayeṣu caratām vartamānānām vartanam anu yad manaḥ vidhīyate puruṣeṇa anuvartyate tad manaḥ asya vivikta ātma pravaṇām prajñām harati viṣaya pravaṇām karoti iti arthaḥ yathā ambhasi nīyamānām nāvam pratikūlaḥ vāyuḥ prasahya harati tasmāt uktena prakāreṇa śubha āśraye mayi niviṣṭa manasaḥ yasya indriyāṇi indriya arthebhyaḥ sarvaśaḥ nigṛhītāni tasya eva ātmani prajñā pratiṣṭhitā bhavati evam niyata indriyasya prasanna manasaḥ siddhim āha yā ātma viṣayā buddhiḥ sarva bhūtānām niśā niśā iva aprakāśā tasyām ātma viṣayāyām buddhau indriya saṃyamī prasanna manāḥ jāgarti ātmānam avalokayan āsta iti arthaḥ yasyām śabda ādi viṣayāyām buddhau sarvāṇi bhūtāni jāgrati prabuddhāni bhavanti sā śabda ādi viṣayā buddhiḥ ātmānam paśyataḥ muneḥ niśā iva aprakāśā bhavati yathā svena eva āpūryamāṇam eka rūpam samudram nādeyya āpaḥ praviśanti āsām apām praveśe api apraveśe ca samudraḥ na kañcana viśeṣam āpadyate evam sarve kāmāḥ śabda ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ yam saṃyaminam praviśanti indriya gocara tām yānti sa śāntim āpnoti śabda ādiṣu indriya gocara tām āpanneṣu anāpanneṣu ca sva ātma avalokana tṛptyā eva yaḥ na vikāram āpnoti sa eva śāntim āpnoti iti arthaḥ na kāma kāmī yaḥ śabda ādibhiḥ vikriyate sa kadācid api na śāntim āpnoti kāmyanta iti kāmāḥ śabda ādayaḥ yaḥ pumān śabda ādīn sarvān viṣayān vihāya tatra nisspṛhaḥ tatra mamatā rahita ḥ ca anātmani dehe ātma abhimāna rahita ḥ carati sa ātmānam dṛṣṭvā śāntim adhigacchati eṣā nitya ātma jñāna pūrvikā asaṅga karmaṇi sthitiḥ sthita dhīlakṣā brāhmī brahmaprāpikā īdṛśīm karmaṇi sthitim prāpya na vimuhyati punar saṃsāram na āpnoti asyāḥ sthityām antime api vayasi sthitvā brahma nirvāṇam ṛcchati nirvāṇa mayam brahma gacchati sukha eka tānam ātmānam avāpnoti iti arthaḥ evam ātmayāthātmyam yuddha ākhyasya ca karmaṇaḥ tad prāpti sādhana tām ajānataḥ śarīra ātma jñānena mohitasya tena ca mohena yuddhān nivṛttasya moha śāntaye nitya ātma viṣayā sāṅkhya buddhiḥ tad pūrvikā ca asaṅga karma anuṣṭhāna rūpa karma yoga viṣayā buddhiḥ sthita prajña tā yoga sādhana bhūtāḥ dvitīye adhyāye proktā tad uktam nitya ātma asaṅga karma iha agocarā sāṅkhya yoga dhīḥ dvitīye sthita dhīlakṣā proktā tad moha śāntaye iti tad evam mumukṣubhiḥ prāpyatayā vedānta udita nirasta nikhila avidyā ādi doṣa gandhāna vadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa para brahma puruṣa uttama prāpti upāya bhūta vedanā upāsana dhy vaktum tad aṅga bhūtam ya ātma apahata pāpmā ityādi prajāpati vākya uditam prāptuḥ ātmanaḥ yāthātmya darśanam tad nitya tā jñāna pūrva kāsaṅga karma niṣpādya jñāna yoga sādhyam uktam prajāpati vākye hi dahara vākya udita para vidyā aśeṣa tayā prāptuḥ ātmanaḥ sva rūpa darśanam yaḥ tam ātmānam anuvidya vijānāti iti uktvā jāgarita svapna suṣupti atītam pratyagātma svarūpam aśarīram pratipādya evam eva eṣa saṃprasādaḥ asmāc śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate iti dahara vidyā phalena upasaṃhṛtam anyatra api adhyātma yoga adhigamena devam matvā dhīraḥ harṣa śokau jahāti iti evam ādiṣu devam matvā iti vidhīyamāna para vidyā aṅga tayā adhyātma yoga adhigamena iti pratyagātma jñānam api vidhāya na jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit ityādinā pratyagātma svarūpam viśodhya aṇoḥ aṇīyān iti ārabhya mahāntam vibhum ātmānam matvā dhīraḥ na śocati  na ayam ātmā pravacanena labhyaḥ na medhayā na bahunā śrutena yam eva eṣa vṛṇute tena labhya ḥ tasya eṣa ātmā vivṛṇute tanūm svām  ityādibhiḥ para svarūpam tad upāsanam upāsanasya ca bhakti rūpa tām pratipādya vijñāna sārathiḥ yaḥ tu manaḥ pragrahavān naraḥ saḥ adhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti tad viṣṇoḥ paramam padam  iti para vidyā phalena upasaṃhṛtam ataḥ param adhyāya catuṣṭayena idam eva prāptuḥ pratyak ātmanaḥ darśanam sa sādhanam prapañcayati yadi karmaṇaḥ buddhiḥ eva jyāyasi iti te matā kim artham tarhi ghore karmaṇi mām niyojayasi etad uktam bhavati jñāna niṣṭhā eva ātma avalokana sādhanam karma niṣṭhā tu tasyāḥ niṣpādikā ātma avalokana sādhana bhūtāḥ ca jñāna niṣṭhā sakala indriya manasām śabda ādi viṣaya vyāpāra uparati niṣpādya iti abhihitā indriya vyāpāra uparati niṣpādyam ātma avalokanam ced siṣā dhayiṣitam sakala karma nivṛtti pūrvaka jñāna niṣṭhāyām eva aham niyojayitavyaḥ kim artham ghore karmaṇi sarva indriya vyāpāra rūpe ātma avalokana virodhini karmaṇi mām niyojayasi iti ataḥ miśra vākyena mām mohayasi iva pratibhāti tathā hi ātma avalokana sādhana bhūtāyāḥ sarva indriya vyāpāra uparati rūpāyāḥ jñāna niṣṭhāyāḥ tad viparyaya rūpam karma sādhanam tad eva kurv iti vākyam viruddham vyāmiśram eva tasmāt ekam amiśra rūpam vākyam vada yena vākyena aham anuṣṭheya rūpam niścitya śreyaḥ prāpnuyām pūrva uktam na samyak avadhṛtam tvayā purā hi asmin loke vicitra adhikāri pūrṇe dvividhā niṣṭhā jñāna karma viṣayā yathā adhikāram asaṅkīrṇā eva mayā uktā na hi sarvaḥ laukikaḥ puruṣaḥ saṃjāta mokṣa abhilāṣaḥ tadānīm eva jñāna yoga adhikāre prabhavati api tu anabhisaṃhita phalena kevala parama puruṣa ārādhana veṣeṇa anuṣṭhitena karmaṇā vidhvasta sva anta malaḥ avyākula indriyaḥ jñāna niṣṭhāyām adhikaroti yataḥ pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yena sarvam idam tatam sva karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ iti parama puruṣa ārādhana eka veṣa tā karmaṇām vakṣyate iha api karmaṇi eva adhikāra ḥ te ityādinā anabhisaṃhita phalam karma anuṣṭheyam vidhāya tena viṣaya vyākula tā rūpa mohāt uttīrṇa buddheḥ prajahāti yadā kāmān  ityādinā jñāna yoga uditaḥ ataḥ sāṅkhyānām eva jñāna yogena sthitiḥ uktā yoginām tu karma yogena saṅkhyā buddhiḥ tad yuktāḥ sāṅkhyāḥ ātma eka viṣayayā buddhyā saṃbandhinaḥ sāṅkhyāḥ atadarhāḥ karma yoga adhikāriṇaḥ yoginaḥ viṣaya vyākula buddhi yuktānām karma yoge adhikāraḥ avyākula buddhīnām tu jñāna yoge adhikāra ukta iti na kiṃcid iha viruddham vyāmiśram abhihitam sarvasya laukikasya puruṣasya mokṣa icchāyām jātāyām sahasā eva jñāna yogaḥ duṣkara iti āha na śāstrīyāṇām karmaṇām anārambhāt eva puruṣaḥ naiṣkarmyam jñāna niṣṭhām prāpnoti na ca ārabdhasya śāstrīyasya tyāgāt yataḥ anabhisaṃhita phalasya parama puruṣa ārādhana veṣasya karmaṇaḥ siddhiḥ sā ataḥ tena vinā tām na prāpnoti anabhisaṃhita phalaiḥ karmabhiḥ anārādhita govindaiḥ avinaṣṭa anādi kāla pravṛtta anantapāpa sañcayaiḥ avyākula indriya tāpūrvikā ātma niṣṭhā dussaṃpādā etad eva upapādayati na hi asmin loke vartamānaḥ puruṣaḥ kaścid kadācid api karma akurvāṇa ḥ tiṣṭhati na kiṃcid karomi iti vyavasitaḥ api sarvaḥ puruṣaḥ prakṛti saṃbhavaiḥ sattva rajaḥ tamobhiḥ prācīna karma anuguṇam pravṛddhaiḥ guṇaiḥ sva ucitam karma prati avaśaḥ kāryate pravartyate ata ukta lakṣaṇena karma yogena prācīnam pāpa saṃcayam nāśayitvā guṇa anḥ ca sattva ādīn vaśe kṛtvā nirmala antaḥkaraṇena saṃpādyaḥ jñāna yogaḥ anyathā jñāna yogāya pravṛttaḥ mithyā ācāraḥ bhavati iti āha avinaṣṭa pāpa tayā ajita antaḥkaraṇaḥ ātma jñānāya pravṛttaḥ viṣaya pravaṇa tayā ātmani vimukhīkṛta manāḥ viṣayān eva smaran ya āste anyathā saṃkalpya anyathā carati iti sa mithyā ācāra ucyate ātma jñānāya udyuktaḥ viparītaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ ataḥ pūrva abhyasta viṣaya sajātīye śāstrīye karmaṇi indriyāṇi ātma avalokana pravṛttena manasā niyamya taiḥ svata eva karma pravaṇaiḥ indriyaiḥ asaṅga pūrvakam yaḥ karma yogam ārabhate saḥ asaṃbhāvyamāna pramāda tvena jñāna niṣṭhād api puruṣāt viśiṣyate niyatam vyāptam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭena hi vyāptam karma anādi vāsanayā prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭaḥ tvam niyata tvena suśaka tvāt asaṃbhāvita pramāda tvāt ca karmaṇaḥ karma eva kuru akarmaṇaḥ jñāna niṣṭhāyā api karma eva jyāyaḥ naiṣkarmyam puruṣaḥ aśunute iti prakramāt akarma śabdena jñāna niṣṭhā eva ucyate jñāna niṣṭha adhikāriṇaḥ api anabhyasta pūrva tayā hi aniyata tvena duḥśaka tvāt sa pramāda tvāt ca jñāna niṣṭhāyāḥ karma niṣṭhā eva jyāyasī karmaṇi kriyamāṇe ca ātmayāthātmya jñānena ātmanaḥ akartṛ tva anusandhānam anantaram eva vakṣyate ata ātma jñānasya api karma yoga antargata tvāt sa eva jyāyān iti arthaḥ karmaṇaḥ jñāna niṣṭhāyā jyāyaḥ tu avacanam jñāna niṣṭhāyām adhikāre sati eva upapadyate yadi sarvam karma parityajya kevalam jñāna niṣṭhāyām adhikāraḥ api tarhi akarmaṇaḥ jñāna niṣṭhasya jñāna niṣṭhā upakāriṇī śarīra yātrā api na setsyati yāvat sādhana samāpti śarīra dhāraṇam ca avaśyam kāryam nyāya arjita dhanena mahāyajña ādikam kṛtvā tad śiṣṭa aśanena eva śarīra dhāraṇam kāryamāhāra śuddhau sattva śuddhiḥ sattva śuddhau dhrutvā smṛtiḥ ityādi śruteḥ te tu agham bhuñjate pāpā ye pacanti ātma kāraṇāt iti vakṣyate ataḥ jñāna niṣṭhasya api karma akurvataḥ deha yātrā api na setsyati yataḥ jñāna niṣṭhasya api dhriyamāṇa śarīrasya yāvat sādhana samāpti mahāyajña ādi nitya naimittikam karma avaśyam kartavyam yataḥ ca karma yoge api ātmanaḥ akartṛ tva bhāvanayā ātma yāthātmya anusandhānam antarbhūtam yataḥ ca prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya karma yogaḥ suśakaḥ apramādaḥ ca ataḥ jñāna niṣṭhā yogyasya api jñāna yogāt karma yogaḥ jyāyān tasmāt tvam karma yogam eva kurv iti abhiprāyaḥ evam tarhi dravya arjana ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ ahaṅkāram amakāra ādi sarva indriya vyakula tā garbha tvena asya puruṣasya karma vāsanayā bandhanam bhaviṣyati iti atra āha yajña ādi śāstrīya karma śeṣa bhūtāt dravya arjana ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ anyatra ātmīya prayojana śeṣa bhūte karmaṇi kriyamāṇe ayam lokaḥ karma bandhanaḥ bhavati ataḥ tvam yajña artham dravya arjana ādikam karma samācara tatra ātma prayojana sādhana tayā yaḥ saṅgaḥ tasmāt saṅgān mukta ḥ tam samācara evam mukta saṅgena yajña ādi artha tayā karmaṇi kriyamāṇe yajña ādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ ārādhitaḥ parama puruṣaḥ asya ana ādi kāla pravṛtta karma vāsanām ucchidya avyākula ātma avalokanam dadāti iti arthaḥ yajña śiṣṭena eva sarva puruṣa artha sādhana niṣṭhānām śarīra dhāraṇa kartavyatām ayajña śiṣṭena śarīra dhāraṇam kurvatām doṣam ca āha patim viśvasya ityādi śruteḥ nirupādhikaḥ prajāpati śabdaḥ sarveśvaram viśvasya sraṣṭāram viśvātmānam parāyaṇam nārāyaṇam āha purā sarga kāle sa bhagavān prajāpatiḥ anādi kāla pravṛtta acid saṃsarga vivaśāḥ upasaṃhṛta nāma rūpa vibhāgāḥ svasmin pralīnāḥ sakala puruṣa arthān arhāḥ cetanā itara kalpāḥ prajāḥ samīkṣya parama kāruṇikaḥ tad ujjīvayiṣayā sva ārādhana bhūta yajña nirvṛttaye yajñaiḥ saha tāḥ sṛṣṭvā evam uvāca anena yajñena prasaviṣyadhvam ātmanaḥ vṛddhim kurudhvam eṣa vaḥ yajñaḥ parama puruṣa artha lakṣaṇa mokṣa ākhyasya kāmasya tad anuguṇānāam ca kāmānām prapūrayitā bhavatu katham anena devatā ārādhana bhūtena devān mad śarīra bhūtān mad ātmakān ārādhayata aham hi sarva yajñānām bhoktā ca prabhuḥ eva ca iti hi vakṣyate yajñena ārādhitāḥ te devāḥ mad ātmakāḥ svārādhana apekṣita anna pāna ādikaiḥ yuṣmān puṣṇantu evam parasparam bhāvayantaḥ param śreyaḥ mokṣa ākhyam avāpsyatha yajña bhāvitāḥ yajñena ārādhitāḥ mad ātmakā devāḥ iṣṭān vaḥ dāsyante uttama puruṣa artha lakṣaṇam mokṣam sādhayatām ye iṣṭā bhogāḥ tān pūrva pūrva yajña bhāvitā devāḥ dāsyante uttarottara ārādhana upekṣitān sarvān bhogān vaḥ dāsyante iti arthaḥ sva ārādhana artha tayā taiḥ dattān bhogān tebhyaḥ apradāya yaḥ bhuṅkte cora eva saḥ couryam hi nāma anyadīye tad prayojanāya eva parikḷpte vastuni svakīyatā buddhim kṛtvā tena sva ātma poṣaṇam ataḥ asya na parama puruṣa arthān arha tā mātram api tu niraya gāmi tvam ca bhaviṣyati iti abhiprāyaḥ tad eva vivṛṇoti indra ādi ātmanā avasthita parama puruṣa ārādhana artha tayā eva dravyāṇi upādāya vipacya taiḥ yathā avasthitam parama puruṣam ārādhya tad śiṣṭa aśanena ye śarīra yātrām kurvate te tu anādi kāla upārjitaiḥ kilbiṣaiḥ ātma yāthātmya avalokana virodhibhiḥ sarvaiḥ mucyante ye tu parama puruṣeṇa indra ādi ātmanā sva ārādhanāya dattāni ātma arthatya upādāya vipacya aśnanti te pāpa ātmanaḥ agham eva bhuñjate agha pariṇāmi tvāt agham iti ucyate ātma avalokana vimukhāḥ narakāya eva pacante punar api loka dṛṣṭyā śāstra dṛṣṭyā ca sarvasya yajña mūla tvam darśayitvā yajña anuvartanasya avaśya kārya tām ananuvartane doṣam ca āha annāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhavanti parjanyāc ca anna saṃbhavaḥ iti sarva loka sākṣikam yajñāt parjanyaḥ bhavati iti ca śāstreṇa avagamyate agnau prāsta āhutiḥ samyak ādityam upatiṣṭhate āditya at jāyate vṛṣṭiḥ ityādinā yajñaḥ ca dravya arjana ādi kartṛ vyāpāra rūpa karma samudbhavaḥ karma ca brahma udbhavam atra ca brahma śabda nirdiṣṭam prakṛti pariṇāma rūpam śarīram tasmāt etad brahma nāma rūpam annam ca jāyate iti hi brahma śabdena prakṛti nirdiṣṭā iha api mama yoniḥ mahat brahma iti vakṣyate ataḥ karma brahma udbhavam iti prakṛti pariṇāma rūpa śarīra udbhavam karma iti uktam bhavati brahma akṣara samudbhavam iti atra akṣara śabda nirdiṣṭaḥ jīvātmā anna pāna ādinā tṛpta akṣara adhiṣṭhitam śarīram karmaṇe prabhavati iti karma sādhana bhūtam śarīram akṣara samudbhavam tasmāt sarva gatam brahma sarva adhikāri gatam śarīram nityam yajñe pratiṣṭhitam yajña mūlam iti arthaḥ evam parama puruṣeṇa pravartitam idam cakram anna ād bhūta śabda nirdiṣṭāni sa jīvāni śarīrāṇi paryjanyāt annam yajñāt parjanyaḥ yajñaḥ ca kartṛ vyāpāra rūpāt karmaṇaḥ karma ca sa jīvā c śarīrāt sa jīvam śarīram punar api anna ād iti anyonya kārya kāraṇa bhāvena cakravat  parivartamānam iha sādhane vartamānaḥ yaḥ karma yoga adhikārī jñāna yoga adhikārī vā na anuvartayati na pravartayati yajña śiṣṭena deha dhāraṇam akurvan saḥ aghāyuḥ bhavati agha ārambhāya eva yasya āyuḥ agha pariṇatam vā ubhaya rūpam vā saḥ aghāyuḥ ata eva indriya ārāmaḥ bhavati na ātma ārāmaḥ indriyāṇi eva asya udyānāni bhavanti ayajña śiṣṭa vardhita deha manaḥ tvena udrikta rajaḥ tamaskaḥ ātma avalokana vimukha tayā viṣaya bhoga eka ratiḥ bhavati ataḥ jñāna yoga ādau yatamānaḥ api niṣphala prayatna tayā mogham pārtha sa jīvati asādhana āyatta ātma darśanasya muktasya iva mahāyajña ādi varṇa āśrama ucita karma anārambha iti āha yaḥ tu jñāna yoga karma yoga sādhana nirapekṣaḥ svata eva ātma ratiḥ ātma abhimukhaḥ ātmanā eva tṛptaḥ na anna pāna ādibhiḥ ātma vyatiriktaiḥ ātmani eva ca santuṣṭaḥ na udyāna sraj candana gīta vāditra nṛtta ādau dhāraṇa poṣaṇa bhogya ādikam sarvam atmā eva yasya tasya ātma darśanāya kartavyam na vidyate svata eva sarvadā dṛṣṭa ātma svarūpa tvāt ata eva tasya ātma darśanāya kṛtena tad sādhanena na arthaḥ na kiṃcid prayojanam akṛtena ātma darśana sādhanena na kaścid anarthaḥ asādhana āyatta ātma darśana tvāt svata eva ātma vyatirikta sakala ācit vastu vimukhasya asya sarveṣu prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣeṣu ākāśa ādiṣu sa kāryeṣu na kaścid prayojana tayā sādhana tayā vā vyapāśrayaḥ yataḥ tad vimukhīkaraṇāya sādhana ārambhaḥ sa hi mukta eva yasmāt asādhana āyatta ātma darśanasya eva sādhana apravṛttiḥ yasmāt ca sādhane pravṛttasya api suśaka tvāt ca apramāda tvāt antargata ātma yāthātmya anusandhāna tvāt ca jñāna yoginaḥ api mātrayā karma anuvṛtti apekṣa tvāt ca karma yoga eva ātma darśana nirvṛttau śreyān tasmāt asaṅga pūrvakam kāryam iti eva satatam yāvat ātma prāpti karma eva samācara asaktaḥ kāryam iti vakṣyamāṇa ākartṛ tva anusandhāna pūrvakam ca karma ācaran puruṣaḥ karma yogena eva param āpnoti ātmānam prāpnoti iti arthaḥ yataḥ jñāna yoga adhikāriṇaḥ api karma yoga eva ātma darśane śreyān ata eva hi janakādayaḥ rājarṣayaḥ jñāninām agresarāḥ karma yogena eva saṃsiddhim āsthitāḥ ātmānam prāptavantaḥ evam prathamam mumukṣoḥ jñāna yogān arha tayā karma yoga adhikāriṇaḥ karma yoga eva kārya iti uktvā jñāna yoga adhikāriṇaḥ api jñāna yogāt karma yoga eva śreyān iti sa hetukam uktam idānīm śiṣṭa tayā vyapadeśyasya sarvathā karma yoga eva kārya iti ucyate loka saṃgraham paśyan  api karma eva kartum arhasi śreṣṭhaḥ kṛtsna śāstra jñātayā anuṣṭhātṛtayā ca prathitaḥ yad yad ācarati tad tad eva akṛtsna vij janaḥ api ācarati anuṣṭhīyamānam api karma śreṣṭhaḥ yad pramāṇam yad aṅga yuktam anutiṣṭhati tad aṅga yuktam eva ākṛtsna vid lokaḥ api anutiṣṭhati ataḥ loka rakṣā artham śiṣṭa tayā prathitena śreṣṭhena sva varṇa āśrama ucitam karma sakalam sarvadā anuṣṭheyam anyathā loka nāśa janitam pāpam jñāna yogāt api enam pracyāvayet na me sarva īśvarasya āpta kāmasya sarvajñasya satya saṅkalpasya triṣu lokeṣu deva manuṣya ādi rūpeṇa svacchandataḥ vartamānasya kiṃcid api kartavyam asti yataḥ anavāptam karmaṇā avāptavyam na kiṃcid api asti atha api loka rakṣāyai karmaṇi eva varte aham sarva īśvaraḥ satya saṅkalpaḥ sva saṅkalpa kṛta jagat udaya vibhava laya līlaḥ chandataḥ jagat upakṛti martyaḥ jātaḥ api manuṣyeṣu śiṣṭa jana agresara vasudeva gṛhe avatīrṇaḥ tad kula ucite karmaṇi atandrita ḥ sarvadā yadi na varteya mama śiṣṭa jana agresara vasudeva sūnoḥ vartma akṛtsna vidaḥ śiṣṭāḥ sarva prakāreṇa ayam eva dharma iti anuvartante te ca sva kartavyān anuṣṭhānena akaraṇe pratyavāyena ca ātmānam alabdhvā niraya gāminaḥ bhaveyuḥ aham kula ucitam karma na ced kuryām evam eva sarve śiṣṭa lokā madācara āyatta dharma niścayāḥ akaraṇāt eva utsīdeyuḥ naṣṭā bhaveyuḥ śāstrīyācārān anupālanāt sarveṣām śiṣṭa kulānām saṃkarasya ca kartā syām ata eva imāḥ prajāḥ upahanyām evam eva tvam api śiṣṭa jana agresara pāṇḍu tanayaḥ yudhiṣṭhira anujaḥ arjuna ḥ san yadi jñāna niṣṭhāyām adhikaroṣi tataḥ tvad ācāra anuvartinaḥ akṛtsna vidaḥ śiṣṭā mumukṣavaḥ sva adhikāram ajānantaḥ karma niṣṭhāyām na adhikurvantaḥ vinaśyeyuḥ ataḥ vyapadeśyena viduṣā karma eva kartavyam avidvāṃsaḥ ātmani akṛtsna vidaḥ karmaṇi saktāḥ karmaṇi avarjanīya saṃbandhāḥ ātmani akṛtsna vittayā tad abhyāsa rūpa jñāna yoge anadhikṛtāḥ karma yoga adhikāriṇaḥ karma yogam eva yathā ātma darśanāya kurvate tathā ātmani kṛtsna vittayā karmaṇi asaktaḥ jñāna yoga adhikāra yogyaḥ api vyapadeśyaḥ śiṣṭaḥ loka rakṣā artham su ācāreṇa śiṣṭa lokānām dharma niścayam cikīrṣuḥ karma yogam eva kuryāt ajñānām ātmani akṛtsna vittayā jñāna yoga upādāna aśaktānām mumukṣūṇām karma saṅginām anādi karma vāsanayā karmaṇi eva niyata tvena karma yoga adhikāriṇām karma yogāt anyat ātma avalokana sādhanam asti iti na buddhi bhedam janayet kim tarhi ātmani kṛtsna vittayā jñāna yoga śaktaḥ api pūrva ukta rītyā karma yoga eva jñāna yoga nirapekṣaḥ ātma avalokana sādhanam iti buddhyā yuktaḥ karma eva ācaran sakala karmasu akṛtsna vidām prītim janayet karma yogam anutiṣṭhataḥ viduṣaḥ aviduṣaḥ ca viśeṣam pradarśayan karma yoga apekṣitam ātmanaḥ akartṛ tva anusandhāna prakāram upadiśati prakṛteḥ guṇaiḥ sattva ādibhiḥ sva anurūpam kriyamāṇāni karmāṇi prati ahaṅkāra vimūḍha ātmā aham kartā iti manyate ahaṅkāreṇa vimūḍha ātmā yasya asau  ahaṅkāra vimūḍha ātmā ahaṅkāraḥ nāma anaham arthe prakṛtau  aham abhimānaḥ tena ajñāta svarūpaḥ guṇa karmasu aham kartā iti manyata iti arthaḥ guṇa karma vibhāgayoḥ sattva ādi guṇa vibhāge tad tad karma vibhāge ca tattva vid guṇa aḥ sattva ādayaḥ guṇeṣu sveṣu kāryeṣu vartanta iti matvā guṇa karmasu aham kartā iti na sajjate akṛtsna vidaḥ sva ātma darśanāya pravṛttāḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa tayā prakṛteḥ guṇaiḥ yathā avasthita ātmani saṃmūḍhāḥ guṇa karmasu kriyāsu eva sajjante na tad vivikta ātma svarūpe ataḥ te jñāna yogāya na prabhavanti iti karma yoga eva teṣām adhikāraḥ evaṃbhūtān  tān mandān akṛtsna vidaḥ kṛtsna vid svayam jñāna yoga avasthānena na vicālayet te kila mandāḥ śreṣṭha jana ācāra anuvartinaḥ karma yogāt utthitam enam dṛṣṭvā karma yogāt pracalita manasaḥ bhaveyuḥ ataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ svayam api karma yoge tiṣṭhan ātmayāthātmya jñānena ātmanaḥ akartṛ tvam anusandhānaḥ karma yoga eva ātma avalokane nirapekṣa sādhanam iti darśayitvā tān akṛtsna vidaḥ joṣayet iti arthaḥ jñāna yoga adhikāriṇaḥ api jñāna yogāt asya eva jyāyaḥ tvam pūrvam eva uktam ataḥ vyapadeśyaḥ loka saṃgrahāya etam eva kuryāt prakṛti vivikta ātma svabhāva nirūpaṇena guṇeṣu kartṛ tvam āropya karma anuṣṭhāna prakāra uktaḥ guṇeṣu kartṛ tva anusandhānam ca idam eva ātmanaḥ na svarūpa prayuktam idam kartṛ tvam api tu guṇa samparka kṛtam iti prāpta aprāpta vivekena guṇa kṛtam iti anusandhānam idānīm ātmanām parama puruṣa śarīra tayā tad niyāmya tva svarūpa nirūpaṇena bhagavati puruṣottame sarva ātma bhūte guṇa kṛtam ca kartṛ tvam āropya karma kartavyatā ucyate mayi sarva īśvare sarva bhūta antarātma bhūte sarvāṇi karmāṇi adhyātma cetasā saṃnyasya nirāśīḥ nirmamaḥ ca vigata jvaraḥ yuddha ādikam sarvam coditam karma kuruṣva ātmani yad cetaḥ tad adhyātma cetaḥ ātma svarūpa viṣayeṇa śruti śata siddhena jñānena iti arthaḥ antaḥ praviṣṭaḥ śāstā janānām sarva ātmā antar praviṣṭam kartāram etam ātmani tiṣṭhan ātmanaḥ antaraḥ yam ātmā na veda yasya ātmā śarīram ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati sa ta ātmā antaryāmī amṛtaḥ iti evam ādyāḥ śrutayaḥ parama puruṣa pravartyam tad śarīra bhūtam enam ātmānam parama puruṣam ca pravartayitāram ācakṣate smṛtayaḥ ca praśāsitāram sarveṣām  ityādyāḥ sarvasya ca aham hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ mattaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam ca  īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan sarva bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā  iti vakṣyate ataḥ mad śarīra tayā mad pravarti ātma svarūpa anusandhānena sarvāṇi karmāṇi mayā eva kriyamāṇāni iti mayi parama puruṣe saṃnyasya tāni ca kevalam mad ārādhanāni iti kṛtvā tad phale nirāśīḥ tataḥ eva tatra karmaṇi mamatā rahitaḥ bhūtvā vigata jvaraḥ yuddha ādikam kuruṣva svakīyena ātmanā kartrā svakīyaiḥ ca upakaraṇaiḥ su ārādhana eka prayojanāya parama puruṣaḥ sarva śeṣī sarva īśvaraḥ svayam eva sva karmāṇi kārayati iti anusandhāya karma ḥ mamatā rahitaḥ prācīnena anādi kāla pravṛtta anantapāpa sañcayena katham aham bhaviṣyāmi iti evaṃbhūta antar jvara vinirmuktaḥ parama puruṣa eva karmabhiḥ ārādhitaḥ bandhān mocayiṣyati iti sukhena karma yogam eva kuruṣv iti arthaḥ tam īśvarāṇām paramam maheśvaram tam daivatānām paramam ca daivatam  patim viśvasya  patim patīnām  ityādi śruti siddhim hi sarva īśvara tvam sarva śeṣi tvam ca īśvara tvam niyantṛ tvam śeṣi tvam pati tvam ayam eva sākṣāt upaniṣad sāra bhūtaḥ artha iti āha ye mānavāḥ śāstra adhikāriṇaḥ ayam eva śāstra artha iti etad me matam niścitya tathā anutiṣṭhanti ye ca ananutiṣṭhantaḥ api asmin śāstra arthe śraddadhānā bhavanti ye ca aśraddadhānā api evam śāstra arthaḥ na saṃbhavati iti na abhyasūyanti asmin mahā guṇe śāstra arthe doṣam anāviṣkurvantaḥ bhavanti iti arthaḥ te sarve bandha hetubhiḥ anādi kāla ārabdhaiḥ sarvaiḥ karmabhiḥ mucyante te api iti api śabdāt eṣām pṛthak karaṇam idānīm ananutiṣṭhantaḥ api asmin śāstra arthe śraddadhānā anabhyasūyavaḥ ca śraddhayā ca anasūyayā ca kṣīṇa pāpāḥ acireṇa imam eva śāstra artham anuṣṭhāya mucyanta iti arthaḥ bhagavat abhimatam aupaniṣadam artham ananutiṣṭhatām aśraddadhānānām abhyasūyatām ca doṣam āha ye tu etad sarvam ātma vastu mad śarīra tayā mad ādhāram mad śeṣa bhūtam mad eka pravartyam iti me matam na anutiṣṭhanti na evam anusandhāya sarvāṇi karmāṇi kurvate ye ca na śraddadhate ye ca abhyasūyantaḥ vartante tān sarveṣu jñāneṣu viśeṣeṇa mūḍhān tataḥ eva naṣṭān acetasaḥ viddhi cetaḥ kāryam hi vastu yāthātmya niścayaḥ tad abhāvāt acetasaḥ viparīta jñānāḥ sarvatra vimūḍhāḥ ca evam prakṛti saṃsargiṇa ḥ tad guṇa udreka kṛtam kartṛ tvam tad ca parama puruṣa āyattam iti anusandhāya karma yoga yogyena jñāna yoga yogyena ca karma yogasya suśaka tvāt apramāda tvāt antargata ātma jñāna tayā nirapekṣa tvāt itarasya duśśaka tvāt sa pramāda tvāt śarīra dhāraṇa ādi artha tayā karma apekṣa tvāt karma yoga eva kartavyaḥ vyapadeśyasya tu viśeṣataḥ sa eva kartavyaḥ iti ca uktam ataḥ param adhyāya śeṣeṇa jñāna yogasya duśśaka tayā sa pramādatā ucyate prakṛti viviktam īdṛśam ātma svarūpam tad eva sarvadā anusandhā iyam iti ca śāstrāṇi pratipādayanti iti jñānavān api svasyāḥ prakṛteḥ prācīna vāsanāya aḥ sadṛśam prākṛta viṣayeṣu eva ceṣṭate kutaḥ prakṛtim yānti bhūtāni acit saṃsṛṣṭā jantavaḥ anādi kāla pravṛtta vāsanām eva anuyānti tāni vāsanā anuyāyīni bhūtāni śāstra kṛtaḥ nigrahaḥ kim kariṣyati prakṛti anuyāyi tva prakāram āha śrotra ādi jñāna indriyasya arthe śabda ādau vāc ādi karmendriyasya ca arthe vacana ādau prācīna vāsanā janita tad anububhūṣā rūpaḥ yaḥ rāgaḥ avarjanīyaḥ vyavasthitaḥ tad anubhave pratihate ca āvarjanīyaḥ yaḥ dveṣaḥ vyavasthitaḥ tau  evam jñāna yogāya yatamānam niyamita sarva indriyam sva vaśe kṛtvā prasahya sva kāryeṣu saṃyojayataḥ tataḥ ca ayam ātma svarūpa anubhava vimukhaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati jñāna yoga ārambheṇa rāga dveṣa vaśam āgamya na vinaśyet tau hi rāga dveṣau asya durjayau śatrū jñāna abhyāsam vārayataḥ ataḥ suśaka tayā svadharma bhūtaḥ karma yogaḥ viguṇaḥ api apramāda garbhaḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya duśśaka tayā para dharma bhūtāj jñāna yogāt sa guṇāt api kiṃcid kālam anuṣṭhitāt sa pramādāt chreyān svena eva upādātum yogyatayā svadharma bhūte karma yoge vartamānasya ekasmin janmani aprāpta phala tayā nidhanam api śreyaḥ anantarāya hata tayā ananta ra janmani api avyākula karma yoga ārambha saṃbhavāt prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya svena eva upādātum aśakya tayā para dharma bhūtaḥ jñāna yogaḥ pramāda garbha tayā bhaya āvahaḥ atha ayam jñāna yogāya pravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ svayam viṣayān anubhavitum anicchan  api kena prayuktaḥ viṣaya anubhava rūpam pāpam balān niyojita iva carati asya udbhava abhibhava rūpeṇa vartamāna guṇa maya prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya jñānāya ārabdhasya rajaḥ guṇa samudbhavaḥ prācīnavāsanā janitaḥ śabda ādi viṣayaḥ kāmaḥ mahā aśanaḥ śatruḥ viṣayeṣu enam ākarṣati eṣa eva pratihata gatiḥ pratihati hetu bhūta cetanān prati krodha rūpeṇa pariṇataḥ mahā pāpmā para hiṃsā ādiṣu pravartayati enam rajaḥ guṇa samudbhavam sahajam jñāna yoga virodhinam vairiṇam viddhi yathā dhūmena vahniḥ āvriyate yathā ādarśaḥ malena yathā ca ulbena āvṛtaḥ garbhaḥ tathā tena kāmena idam jantu jātam āvṛtam āvaraṇa prakāram āha asya jantoḥ jñāninaḥ jñāna svabhāvasya ātma viṣayam jñānam etena kāmakāreṇa viṣaya vyāmoha jananena nitya vairiṇā āvṛtam duṣpūreṇa prāpti anarha viṣayeṇa analena ca paryāpti rahitena kaiḥ upakaraṇaiḥ ayam kāma ātmānam adhiṣṭhiti iti atra āha adhitiṣṭhati ebhiḥ ayam kāma ātmānam iti indriyāṇi manaḥ buddhiḥ asya adhiṣṭhānam etaiḥ indriya manaḥ buddhibhiḥ kāmaḥ adhiṣṭhāna bhūtaiḥ viṣaya pravaṇaiḥ dehinam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭam jñānam āvṛtya vimohayati vividham mohayati ātma jñāna vimukham viṣaya anubhava param karoti iti arthaḥ yasmāt sarva indriya vyāpāra uparati rūpe jñāna yoge pravṛttasya ayam kāmarūpaḥ śatruḥ viṣaya abhimukhya karaṇena ātmani vaimukhyam karoti tasmāt prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa tayā indriya vyāpāra pravaṇaḥ tvam ādau mokṣa upāya ārambha samaya eva indriya vyāpāra rūpe karma yoge indriyāṇi niyamya enam jñāna vijñāna nāśanam ātma svarūpa viṣayasya jñānasya tad viveka viṣayasya ca nāśanam pāpmānam kāmarūpam vairiṇam prajahi nāśaya jñāna virodhiṣu pradhānam āha jñāna virodhe pradhānāni indriyāṇi āhuḥ yata indriyeṣu viṣaya vyāpṛteṣu ātmani jñānam na pravartate indriyebhyaḥ param manaḥ indriyeṣu uparateṣu api manasi viṣaya pravaṇe ātma jñānam na saṃbhavati manasaḥ tu parā buddhiḥ manasi vṛtti antara vimukhe api viparīta adhyavasāya pravṛttau satyām jñānam na pravartate sarveṣu buddhi paryanteṣu uparateṣu api icchā aparyāyaḥ kāmaḥ rajassamudbhavaḥ vartate ced sa eva etāni indriya ādīni api sva viṣaye vartayitvā ātma jñānam niruṇaddhi tad idam ucyate yaḥ buddheḥ para ḥ tu saḥ iti buddheḥ api yaḥ para ḥ sa kāma iti arthaḥ evam buddheḥ api param kāmam jñāna yoga virodhinam vairiṇam buddhvā ātmānam manaḥ ātmanā buddhyā karma yoge avasthāpya enam kāmarūpam durāsadam śatrum jahi nāśaya iti tṛtīye adhyāye prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya mumukṣoḥ sahasā jñāna yoge anadhikārāt karma yoga eva kāryaḥ jñāna yoga adhikāriṇaḥ api akartṛ tva anusandhāna pūrvaka karma yoga eva śreyān iti sa hetukam uktam śiṣṭa tayā vyapadeśyasya tu viśeṣataḥ karma yoga eva kārya iti ca uktam caturthena idānīm asya eva karma yogasya nikhila jagat uddharaṇāya manvantara ādau  eva upadiṣṭa tayā kartavyatām draḍhayitvā antargata jñāna tayā asya eva jñāna yoga ākara tām pradarśya karma yoga svarūpam tad bhedāḥ karma yoge jñāna aṃśasya eva prādhānyam ca ucyate prasaṅga āt ca bhagavat avatārayāthātmyam ucyate śrī bhagavān uvāca yaḥ ayam tava uditaḥ yogaḥ sa kevalam yuddha protsāhanāya idānīm udita iti na mantavyam manvantara ādau  eva nikhila jagat uddharaṇāya parama puruṣa artha lakṣaṇa mokṣa sādhana tayā imam yogam aham eva vivasvate proktavān vivasvān  ca manave manuḥ ikṣu akave iti evam saṃpradāya paramparayā prāptam imam yogam pūrve rājarṣayaḥ aviduḥ sa mahatā kālena tad tad śrotṛ buddhi māndyāt vinaṣṭa prāyaḥ abhūt sa eva ayam askhalita svarūpaḥ purātanaḥ yogaḥ sakhyena atimātra bhaktyā ca mām eva prapannāya te mayā proktaḥ sa parikaraḥ sa vistaram ukta iti arthaḥ mad anyena kena api jñātum vaktum ca aśakyam yata idam vedānta uditam uttamam rahasyam jñānam asmin prasaṅge bhagavat avatārayāthātmyam yathāvaj jñātum arjuna uvāca kāla saṅkhyayā avaram asmad janma sama kālam hi bhavataḥ janma vivasvataḥ ca janma kāla saṅkhyayā param aṣṭāviṃśati caturyuga saṅkhyā saṅkhyātam tvam eva ādau proktavān iti katham etad asaṃbhāvanīyam yathārtham jānīyām nanu janma antareṇa api vaktum śakyam janma antara kṛtasya mahatām smṛtiḥ ca yujyata iti na atra kaścid virodhaḥ na ca asau vaktāram enam vasudeva tanayam sarveśvaram na jānāti yata evam vakṣyati param brahma param dhāma pavitram paramam bhavān puruṣam śāśvatam divyam ādidevam ajam vibhum āhuḥ tvām ṛṣayaḥ sarve devarṣiḥ nārada ḥ tathā asitaḥ devalaḥ vyāsaḥ svayam ca eva bravīṣi me iti yudhiṣṭhira rājasūya ādiṣu bhīṣma ādibhyaḥ ca asakṛt śrutam kṛṣṇa eva hi lokānām utpattiḥ api ca apyayaḥ kṛṣṇasya hi kṛte bhūtam idam viśvam carācaram iti evamādiṣu kṛṣṇasya hi kṛte iti kṛṣṇasya śeṣa bhūtam idam kṛtsnam jagad iti arthaḥ atra ucyate jānāti eva ayam bhagavantam vasudeva sūnam pārthaḥ jānataḥ api ajānata iva pṛcchataḥ ayam āśayaḥ nikhila heya pratyanīka kalyāṇa ekatānasya sarva īśvarasya sarvajñasya satya saṅkalpasya avāpta samasta kāmasya karma para vaśa deva manuṣya ādi sajātīyam janma kim indrajāla ādi van mithyā uta satyam satya tve ca katham janma prakāraḥ kim ātmakaḥ ayam dehaḥ kaḥ ca janma hetuḥ kadā ca janma kim artham ca janma iti parihāra prakāreṇa praśna arthaḥ vijñāyate anena janmanaḥ satya tvam uktam bahūni me vyatītāni janmāni iti vacanāt tava ca iti dṛṣṭānta tayā upādāna āt ca avatāra prakāram deha yāthātmyam janma hetum ca āha ajatvā avyaya tva sarva īśvara tva ādi sarvam pārameśvaram prakāram ajahad eva svām prakṛtim adhiṣṭhāya ātma māyayā saṃbhavāmi prakṛtiḥ svabhāvaḥ svam eva svabhāvam adhiṣṭhāya svena eva rūpeṇa sva icchayā saṃbhavāmi iti arthaḥ sva svarūpam hiāditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt  kṣayantam asya rajasaḥ parāke  ya eṣaḥ antarāditye hiraṇya mayaḥ puruṣaḥ  tasmin  ayam puruṣaḥ manaḥ mayaḥ amṛtaḥ hiraṇmayaḥ  sarve nimeṣā jajñire vidyutaḥ puruṣāt adhi  bhā ru upaḥ satya saṅkalpa ākāśa ātmā sarva kāmā sarva kāma ḥ sarva gandha ḥ sarva rasaḥ  mā āhāra janam vāsaḥ ityādi śruti siddham ātma māyayā ātmīyayā māyayā māyā vayunam jñānam iti jñāna paryāyaḥ atra māyā śabdaḥ tathā ca abhiyukta prayogaḥ māyayā satatam vetti prāṇinām ca śubha aśubham iti ātmīyena jñānena ātma saṅkalpena iti arthaḥ ataḥ apahata pāpma tva ādi samasta kalyāṇa guṇa ātmaka tvam sarvam aiśam svabhāvam ajahat svam eva rūpam deva manuṣya ādi sajātīya saṃsthānam kurvan ātma saṅkalpena deva ādi rūpaḥ saṃbhavāmi tad idam āha ajāyamānaḥ bahudhā vijāyate iti śrutiḥ itara puruṣa sādhāraṇam janma akurvan deva ādi rūpeṇa sva saṅkalpena ukta prakriyayā jāyata iti arthaḥ bahūni me vyatītāni janmāni tava ca arjuna tāni aham veda sarvāṇi  tad ā ātmānam sṛjāmi aham  janma karma ca me divyam evam yaḥ vetti tattvataḥ iti pūrva apara avirodhāt ca janma kālam āha na kāla niyamaḥ asmad saṃbhavasya yadā yadā hi dharmasya veda uditasya cāturvarṇya cāturāśramya vyavasthayā avasthitasya kartavyayasya glāniḥ bhavati yadā yadā ca tad viparyayasya adharmasya abhyutthānam tadā aham eva sva saṅkalpena ukta prakāreṇa ātmānam sṛjāmi janmanaḥ prayojanam āha sādhavaḥ ukta lakṣaṇa dharma śīlāḥ vaiṣṇava agra īsarā mad samāśrayaṇe pravṛttā mad nāma karma svarūpāṇām vāc manasā agocaratayā mad darśanena vinā sva ātma dhāraṇa poṣaṇa ādi km alabhamānāḥ kṣaṇa mātra kālam kalpa sahasram manvānāḥ pratiśithila sarva gātrā bhaveyuḥ iti mad sva rūpa ceṣṭita avalokanālāpa ādi dānena teṣām paritrāṇāya tad viparītānām vināśāya ca kṣīṇasya vaidikasya dharmasya mad ārādhana rūpasya ārādhya svarūpa pradarśanena sthāpanāya ca deva manuṣya ādi rūpeṇa yuge yuge saṃbhavāmi kṛta tretā ādi yuga viśeṣa niyamaḥ api na asti iti arthaḥ evam karma mūla heya triguṇa prakṛti saṃsarga rūpa janma rahitasya sarvesvara tva sāru ajñi satya saṅkalpa tva ādi samasta kalyāṇa guṇa upetasya sādhu paritrāṇa mad samāśrayaṇa eka prayojanam divyam aprākṛtam mada sādhāraṇam mama janma ceṣṭitam ca tattvataḥ yaḥ vetti sa vartamānam deham parityajya punarjanma na eti mām eva prāpnoti madīya divya janma ceṣṭita yāthātmya vijñānena vidhvasta samastamad samāśryaṇa virodhi pāpaḥ asmin  eva janmani yathā udita prakāreṇa mām āśritya mad eka priyaḥ mad eka cittaḥ mām eva prāpnoti tad āha madīya janma karma tattva jñāna ākhyena tapasā pūtā bahava evam saṃvṛttāḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ tasya dhīrāḥ parijānanti yonim iti dhīrāḥ dhīmatām agresarā evam tasya janma prakāram jānanti iti arthaḥ na kevalam deva manuṣya ādi rūpeṇa avatīrya mad samāśrayaṇa apekṣāṇām paritrāṇam karomi api tu ye mad samāśrayaṇa apekṣā yathā yena prakāreṇa sva apekṣa anurūpam mām saṃkalpya prapadyante samāśrayante tān prati tathā eva tad manīṣita prakāreṇa bhajāmi mām darśayāmi kim atra bahunā sarve manuṣyāḥ mad anuvartana eka manorathā mama vartma mad svabhāvam sarvam yoginām vāc manasā agocaram api svakīyāiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇaiḥ sarvaśaḥ svāpekṣitaiḥ sarva prakāraiḥ anubhūya anuvartnte idānīm prāsaṅgikam parisamāpya prakṛtasya karma yogasya jñāna ākāra tā prakāram vaktum tathāvidha karma yoga adhikāriṇaḥ durlabha tvam āha sarva eva puruṣāḥ karmaṇām phalam kāṅkṣamāṇāḥ indra ādi devatā mātram yajante ārādhayanti na tu kaścid anabhisaṃhita phalaḥ indra ādi devatā ātma bhūtam sarva yajñānām bhoktāram mām yajate kuta etad yataḥ kṣiprasmin  eva mānuṣe loke karma jā putra paśu annādi siddhiḥ bhavati manuṣya loka śabdaḥ svarga ādīnām api pradarśana arthaḥ sarvam eva laukikāḥ puruṣā akṣīṇa anādi kāla pravṛtta ananta pāpa saṃcaya tayā avivekinaḥ kṣipra phala ākāṅkṣiṇaḥ putra paśu annādya svarga ādi artha tayā sarvāṇi karmāṇi indra ādi devatā ārādhana mātrāṇi kurvate na tu kaścid saṃsāra udvigna hṛdayaḥ mumukṣuḥ ukta lakṣaṇam karma yogam mad ārādhana bhūtam ārabhata iti arthaḥ yathā ukta karma yoga ārambha virodhi pāpa kṣaya hetum āha cāturvarṇya pramukham brahma ādi stamba paryantam kṛtsnam jagat sattva ādi guṇa vibhāgena tad anuguṇa śama ādi karma vibhāgena ca vibhaktam mayā sṛṣṭam sṛṣṭi grahaṇam pradarśana artham mayā eva rakṣyante mayā eva ca upasaṃhriyate tasya vicitra sṛṣti ādeḥ kartāram api akartāram mām viddhi katham iti atra āha yata imāni vicitra sṛṣṭi ādīni karmāṇi mām na limpanti na mām saṃbadhnanti na mad prayuktāni tāni deva manuṣya ādi vaicitryāṇi sṛjyānām puṇya pāpa rūpa karma viśeṣa prayuktāni iti arthaḥ ataḥ prāpta aprāpta vivekena vicitra sṛṣṭi ādeḥ na aham kartā yataḥ ca sṛṣṭāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ sṛṣṭi labdha karaṇa kalebarāḥ sṛṣṭi labdham bhogya jātam phala saṅga ādi hetu sva karma anuguṇam bhuṅjate sṛṣṭyāt karma phale ca teṣām eva spṛhā iti ne me spṛhā tathā āha sūtra kāraḥ vaiṣamyanaiḥ ghṛṇye na sa apekṣa tvāt iti tathā ca bhagavān parāśaraḥ nimitta mātram eva asau sṛjyānām sarga karmaṇi pradhāna kāraṇībhūtā yataḥ vai sṛjya śaktayaḥ nimitta mātram muktvā idam na anyat kiṃcid apekṣate nīyate tapatām śreṣṭha sva śaktyā vastu vastu tām  iti sṛjyānām deva ādīnām kṣetrajñānām sṛṣṭeḥ kāraṇa mātram eva ayam parama puruṣaḥ deva ādi vaicitrye tu pradhāna kāraṇam sṛjya bhūta kṣetrajñānām prācīnakarma śaktaya eva ataḥ nimitta mātram muktvā sṛṣṭeḥ kartāram parama puruṣam muktvā idam kṣetrajña vastu deva ādi vicitra bhāve na anyat apekṣate sva gata prācīnakarma śaktyā eva hi deva ādi vastu bhāvam nīyata iti arthaḥ evam uktena prakāreṇa sṛṣti ādeḥ kartāram api akartāram sṛṣṭi ādi karma phala saṅga rahitam ca yaḥ mām abhijānāti sa karma yoga ārambha virodhibhiḥ phala saṅga ādi hetubhiḥ prācīna karmabhiḥ na saṃbadhyate mucyata iti arthaḥ evam mām jñātvā vimukta pāpaiḥ pūrvaiḥ api mumukṣubhiḥ ukta lakṣaṇam karma kṛtam tasmāt tvam ukta prakāra mad viṣaya jñāna vidhūta pāpaḥ pūrvaiḥ vivasvat manu ādibhiḥ kṛtam pūrvataram purātanam tadānīm eva mayā uktam vakṣyamāṇa ākāram karva eva kuru vakṣyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ durjñāna tām āha mumukṣuṇā anuṣṭheyam karma kiṃrūpam akarma ca kim akarma iti kartuḥ ātmanaḥ yāthātmya jñānam ucyate anuṣṭheyam karma tad antargatam jñānam ca kiṃrūpam iti ubhayatra kavayaḥ vidvāṃsaḥ api mohitāḥ yathāvan na jānanti evam antargata jñānam yad karma tad te pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā anuṣṭhāya aśubhāt saṃsāra bandhān mokṣyase kartavya karma jñānam hi anuṣṭhāna phalam kutaḥ asya durjñāna tā iti āha yasmān mokṣa sādhana bhūte karma svarūpe boddhavyam asti vikarmaṇi ca nitya naimittika kāmya rūpeṇa tad sādhana dravya arjana ādi ākāreṇa ca vividha tā āpannam karma vikarma akarmaṇi jñāne ca boddhavyam asti gahanā durvijñānā mumukṣoḥ karmaṇaḥ gatiḥ vikarmaṇi boddhavyam nitya naimittika kāmya dravya arjana ādau karmaṇi phala bheda kṛtam vaividhyam parityajya mokṣa eka phala tayā eka śāstra artha tva anusandhānam tad etad  vyavasāya ātmikā buddhiḥ ekā iti atra eva uktam iti na iha prapañcyate karma akarmaṇoḥ boddhavyam āha akarma śabdena atra karma itarāt prastutam ātma jñānam ucyate karmaṇi kriyamāṇa eva ātma jñānam yaḥ paśyet akarmaṇi ca ātma jñāne vartamāna eva yaḥ karma paśyet kim uktam bhavati kriyamāṇam eva karma ātma yāthātmya anusandhānena jñāna ākāram yaḥ paśyet tad ca jñānam karma yoga antara gata tayā karma ākāram yaḥ paśyet iti uktam bhavati kriyamāṇe hi karmaṇi kartṛ bhūta ātma yāthātmya anusandhāne sati tad ubhayam saṃpannam bhavati evam ātma yāthātmya anusandhāna antargarbham karma yaḥ paśyet sa buddhimān kṛtsna śāstra artha vid manuṣyeṣu sa yuktaḥ mokṣāya arhaḥ sa eva kṛtsna karma kṛt kṛtsna śāstra artha kṛt pratyakṣeṇa kriyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ jñana ākāra tā katham upapadyata iti atra āha yasya mumukṣoḥ sarve dravya arjana ādi laukika karma pūrvaka nitya naimittika kāmya rūpa karma samārambhāḥ kāma arjitāḥ phala saṅga rahitāḥ saṅkalpa varjitāḥ ca prakṛtyā tad guṇaiḥ ca ātmānam ekīkṛtya anusandhānam saṅkalpaḥ prakṛti viyukta ātma svarūpa anusandhāna yukta tayā tad rahitāḥ tam evam karma kurvāṇam paṇḍitam karma antargata ātma yāthātmya jñāna agninā dagdha prācīna karmāṇam āhuḥ tattva jñāḥ ataḥ karmaṇaḥ jñāna ākāra tvam upapadyate etad eva vivṛṇoti karma phala saṅgam tyaktvā nitya tṛptaḥ nitye sva ātmni eva tṛptaḥ nirāśrayaḥ asthira prakṛtau āśraya buddhi rahitaḥ yaḥ karmāṇi karoti sa karmaṇi ābhimukhyena pravṛttaḥ api na eva kiṃcid karma karoti karma apadeśena jñāna abhyāsam eva karoti iti arthaḥ punar api karmaṇaḥ jñāna ākāra tā eva viśodhyate nirāśīḥ nirgata phala abhisandhiḥ yata citta ātmā yata citta manāḥ tyakta sarva parigrahaḥ ātma eka prayojana tayā prakṛti prākṛta vastuni mamatā rahitaḥ yāvat jīvam kevalam śārīram eva karma kurvan kilbiṣam saṃsāram na āpnoti jñāna niṣṭhā vyavadhāna rahita kevala karma yogena evaṃrūpeṇa ātmānam paśyati iti arthaḥ yadṛcchā upanata śarīra dhāraṇa hetu vastu santuṣṭaḥ dvandva atītaḥ yāvat sādhana samāptya varjanīya śīta uṣṇa ādi sahaḥ vimatsaraḥ aniṣṭa upanipāta hetu bhūta sva karma nirūpaṇena pareṣu vigata matsaraḥ samaḥ siddhau  asiddau ca yuddha ādi karmasu jaya ādi siddhi asiddhyoḥ sama cittaḥ karma eva kṛtvā api jñāna niṣṭhām vinā api na nibadhyate na saṃsāram pratipadyate ātma viṣaya jñāna avasthita manaḥ tvena nirgata taditara saṅgasya tataḥ eva nikhila parigraha vinirmuktasya ukta lakṣaṇa yajña ādi karma nirvṛttaye vartamānasya puruṣasya bandha hetu bhūtam prācīnam karma samagram pravilīyate niśśeṣam kṣīyate prakṛti viyukta ātma svarūpa anusandhāna yukta tayā karmaṇaḥ jñāna ākāra tvam uktam idānīm sarvasya sa parikarasya karmaṇaḥ para brahma bhūta parama puruṣa ātmaka tva anusandhāna yukta tayā jñāna ākāra tvam āha brahma arpaṇam iti havir viśeṣyate arpyate anena iti arpaṇam sruc ādi tad brahma kārya tvāt brahma brahma yasya haviṣaḥ arpaṇam tad brahma arpaṇam brahma haviḥ brahma arpaṇam haviḥ svayam ca brahma bhūtam brahma agnau brahma bhūte agnau brahmaṇā kartrā hutam iti sarvam karma brahma ātmaka tayā brahma mayam iti yaḥ samādhatte sa brahma karma samādhiḥ tena brahma karma samādhinā brahmā eva gantavyam brahma ātmaka tayā brahma bhūtam ātma svarūpam gantavyam mumukṣuṇā kriyamāṇam karma para brahma ātmakam eva iti anusandhāna yukta tayā jñāna ākāram sākṣāt ātma avalokana sādhanam na jñāna niṣṭhāvi adhānena iti arthaḥ evam karmaṇaḥ jñāna ākāra tām pratipādya karma yoga bhedān āha bhhu daivam deva arcana rūpam yajñam apare karma yoginaḥ paryupāsate sevante tatra eva niṣṭhām kurvanti iti arthaḥ apare brahma agnau yajñam yajñena eva upajuhvati atra yajña śabdaḥ haviḥ sruc ādi yajña sādhane vartate brahma arpaṇam brahma haviḥ iti nyāyena yāga homayoḥ niṣṭhām kurvanti bhhu anye śrotra ādīnām indriyāṇām saṃyamane prayatante anye yoginaḥ indriyāṇām śabda ādi pravaṇa tā nivāraṇe prayatante bhhu anye jñāna dīpite manassaṃyana yoga agnau sarvāṇi indriya karmāṇi prāṇa karmāṇi ca juhvati manasa indriya prāṇa karma prvaṇa tā nivāraṇe prayatanta iti arthaḥ bhhu kecid karma yoginaḥ dravya yajñāḥ nyāyataḥ dravyāṇi upādāya devatā arcane prayatante kecid ca dāneṣu kecid ca yāgeṣu kecid ca homeṣu ete sarve dravya yajñāḥ kecid tapaḥ yajñāḥ kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa upavāsa ādiṣu niṣṭhām kurvanti yoga yajñāḥ ca apare puṇya tīrtha puṇya sthāna prāptiṣu niṣṭhām kurvanti iha yoga śabdaḥ karma niṣṭha abheda prakaraṇāt tad viṣayaḥ kecid svādhyāya abhyāsa parāḥ kecid tad artha jñāna abhyāsa parāḥ yatayaḥ yatana śīlāḥ saṃśita vratāḥ dṛḍha saṅkalpāḥ bhhu apare karma yoginaḥ prāṇāyāmeṣu niṣṭhām kurvanti te ca trividhāḥ pūraka recaka kumbhaka bhedena apāne juhvati prāṇam iti pūrakaḥ prāṇe apānam iti recakaḥ prāṇa apāna gatī ruddhvā prāṇān prāṇeṣu juhvati iti kumbhakaḥ prāṇāyāma pareṣu triṣu api anuṣajyate niyata āhārā iti bhhu daiva yajña prabhṛti prāṇāyāma paryanteṣu karma yoga bhedeṣu sva samīhiteṣu pravṛttā ete sarve saha yajñaiḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā iti abhihita mahā yajña pūrvaka nitya naimittika karma rūpa yajña vidaḥ tad niṣṭhāḥ tataḥ eva kṣapita kalmaṣāḥ yajña śiṣṭa amṛtena śarīra dhāraṇam kurvanta eva karma yoga vyāpṛtāḥ sanātanam brahma yānti bhhu ayajñasya mahāyajña ādi pūrvaka nitya maimittika karma rahitasya na ayam lokaḥ na prākṛta lokaḥ prākṛta loka saṃbandhi dharma artha kāma ākhyaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ na sidhyati kuta itaḥ anyaḥ mokṣa ākhyaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ parama puruṣa artha tayā mokṣasya prastuta tvāt tad itara puruṣa arthaḥ ayam lokaḥ iti nirdiśyate sa hi prākṛtaḥ bhhu evam hi bahu prakārāḥ karma yogāḥ brahmaṇaḥ mukhe vitatāḥ ātma yāthātmya avāpti sādhana tayā sthitāḥ tān ukta lakṣaṇān ukta bhedān karma yogān sarvān karma jān viddhi aharahar anuṣṭhīyamāna nitya naimittika karma jān viddhi evam jñātvā yathā ukta prakāreṇa anuṣṭhāya mokṣyase antargata jñāna tayā karmaṇaḥ jñāna ākāra tvam uktam tatra antargata jñāne karmaṇi jñāna aṃśasya eva prādhānyam āha bhhu ubhaya ākāre karmaṇi dravya mayād aṃśāj jñāna maya aṃśaḥ śreyān sarvasya karmaṇaḥ tad itarasya ca akhilasya upādeyasya jñāne parisamāpteḥ tad eva sarvaiḥ sādhanaiḥ prāpya bhūtam jñānam karma antargata tvena abhyasyate tad eva abhyasyamānam krameṇa prāpya daśām pratipadyate bhhu tad atma viṣayam jñānam avināśi tu tad viddhi iti ārabhya eṣā te abhihitā iti antena mayā upadiṣṭam tad yukta karmaṇi vartamāna tvam vipāka anuguṇam kāle kāle praṇipāta paripraśna sevā ādibhiḥ viśada ākāram jñānibhyaḥ viddhi sākṣātkṛtātma svarūpā aḥ tu jñāninaḥ praṇipāta ādibhyaḥ sevitāḥ jñāna bubhutsayā paritaḥ pṛcchataḥ tava āśayam ālakṣya jñānam upadekṣyanti ātma yāthātmya viṣayasya jñānasya sākṣātkāra rūpasya lakṣaṇam āha bhhu yaj jñānam jñātvā punar evam deva ādi ātma abhimāna rūpam tad kṛtam mamatā adi āspadam ca moham na yāsyasi yena ca deva manuṣya ādi ākāreṇa anusanhitāni sarvāṇi bhūtāni sva ātmani eva drakṣyasi yataḥ tava anyeṣām ca bhūtānām prakṛti viyuktānām jñāna eka ākāra tayā sāmyam prakṛti saṃsarga doṣa vinirmuktam ātma rūpam sarvam samam iti ca vakṣyate nirdoṣam hi samam brahma tasmāt brahmaṇi te sthitāḥ iti athaḥ mayi sarva bhūtāni aśeṣeṇa drakṣyasi mad svarūpa sāmyāt pariśuddhasya sarvasya ātma vastunaḥ idam jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ iti hi vakṣyate tathā tadā vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti evamādiṣu nāma rūpa vinirmuktasya ātma vastunaḥ para svarūpa sāmyam avagamyate ataḥ prakṛti vinirmuktam sarvam ātma vastu parasparam samam sarva īśvareṇa ca samam bhhu yadi api sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ pāpa kṛttamaḥ asi sarvam pūrva arjitam vṛjina rūpam samudram ātma viṣaya jñāna rūpa plavena eva saṃtariṣyasi bhhu samyak pravṛddhaḥ agniḥ indhana sañcayam iva ātmayāthātmya jñāna rūpaḥ agniḥ jīvātma gatam anādi kāla pravṛtta ananta karma sañcayam bhasmīkaroti bhhu yasmāt ātma jñānena sadṛśam pavitram śuddhi karam iha jagati vastu antaram na vidyate tasmāt ātma jñānam sarva pāpam nāśayati iti arthaḥ tad tathāvidham jñānam yathā upadeśam aharahar anuṣṭhīyamāna jñāna ākāra karma yoga
