saṃsiddhaḥ kālena sva ātmani svayam eva labhate tad eva vispaṣṭam āha bhhu evam upadeśa aj jñānam labdhvā ca upadiṣṭa jñāna vṛddhau śraddhāvān tad paraḥ tatra eva niyata manāḥ tad itara viṣayāt saṃyata indriyaḥ acireṇa kālena ukta lakṣaṇa vipāka daśā āpannam jñānam labhate tathāvidham jñānam labdhvā parām śāntim acireṇa adhigacchati param nirvāṇam āpnoti bhhu ajñaḥ evam upadeśa labdha jñāna rahitaḥ upadiṣṭa jñāna vṛddhi upāye ca aśraddhadhānaḥ atvaramāṇaḥ upadiṣṭe ca jñāne saṃśaya ātmā saṃśaya manāḥ vinaśyati vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati asmin  upadiṣṭe ātmayāthātmya viṣaye jñāne saṃśaya ātmanaḥ ayam api prākṛtaḥ lokaḥ na asti na ca paraḥ dharma artha kāma rūpa puruṣa arthāḥ ca na sidhyanti kutaḥ mokṣa iti arthaḥ śāstrīya karma siddhi rūpa tvāt sarveṣām puruṣa arthānām śāstrīya karma janya siddheḥ ca deha atirikta ātma niścaya pūrvaka tvāt ataḥ sukha lava bhāgi tvam ātmani saṃśaya ātmanaḥ na saṃbhavati bhhu yathā upadiṣṭa yogena saṃnyasta karmāṇam jñāna ākāra tā āpanna karmāṇam yathā upadiṣṭena ca ātma jñānena ātmani saṃcchinna saṃśayam ātmavantam manasvinam upadiṣṭa arthe dṛḍha avasthita manasam bandha hetu bhūta prācīna ananta karmāṇi na nibadhnanti bhhu tasmāt anādya jñāna saṃbhūtam hṛd stham ātma viṣayam saṃśayam mayā upadiṣṭena ātma jñāna asinā chittvā mayā upadiṣṭam karma yogam ātiṣṭha tad artham uttiṣṭha bhārata iti caturthe adhyāye karma yogasya jñāna ākāra tā pūrvaka svarūpa bhedaḥ jñāna aṃśasya ca prādhānyam uktam jñāna yoga adhikāriṇaḥ api karma yogasya antargata ātma jñāna tvāt apramāda tvāt sukara tvān nirapekṣa tvāt ca jyāyaḥ tvam tṛtīya eva uktam idānīm karma yogasya ātma prāpti sādhana tve jñāna niṣṭhāya āḥ śaighryam karma yoga antargata ākarṭrtvā anusandhāna prakāram ca pratipādya tad mūlam jñānam ca viśodhyate karmaṇām saṃnyāsam jñāna yogam punar karma yogam ca śaṃsasi etad uktam bhavati dvitīye adhyāye mumukṣoḥ prathamam karma yoga eva kāryaḥ karma yogena mṛdita antaḥkaraṇa kaṣāyasya jñāna yogena ātma darśanam kāryam iti pratipādya punar tṛtīya caturthayoḥ jñāna yoga adhikāra daśāpannasya api karma niṣṭhā eva jyāyasī sā eva jñāna niṣṭhā niḥ apekṣā ātma prāptau sādhanam iti karma niṣṭhām praśaṃśasi iti tatra etayoḥ jñāna yoga karma yogayoḥ ātma prāpti sādhana bhāve yad ekam saukārya c chaighryāt ca śreyaḥ śreṣṭham iti su niścitam tad me brūhi bhhu saṃnyāsaḥ jñāna yogaḥ karma yogaḥ ca jñāna yoga śaktasya api ubhau nirapekṣau niśśreyasa karau tayoḥ tu karma saṃnyāsā j jñāna yogāt karma yoga eva viśiṣyate kuta iti atra āha bhhu yaḥ karma yogī tad antargata ātma anubhava tṛpta ḥ tad vyatiriktam kim api na kāṅkṣati tataḥ eva kim api na dveṣṭi tataḥ eva dvandva sahaḥ ca sa nitya saṃnyāsī nitya jñāna niṣṭha iti jñeyaḥ sa hi sukara karma yoga niṣṭhatayā sukham bandhāt pramucyate jñāna yoga karma yogayoḥ ātma prāpti sādhana bhāve anyonyanaiḥ apekṣyam āha bhhu jñāna yoga karma yogau phala bhedāt pṛthak bhūtau ye pravadanti te bālāḥ aniṣpanna jñānāḥ na paṇḍitāḥ akṛtsna vidaḥ karma yogaḥ jñāna yogam eva sādhayati jñāna yoga ḥ tu eka ātma avalokanam sādhayati iti tayoḥ phala bhedena pṛthaktvam vadantaḥ na paṇḍitā iti arthaḥ ubhayoḥ ātma avalokana eka phalayoḥ eka phala tvena ekam api āsthita ḥ tad eva phalam labhate etad eva vivṛṇoti bhhu sāṃkhyaiḥ jñāna niṣṭhaiḥ yad atma avalokana rūpam phalam prāpyate tad eva karma yoga niṣṭhaiḥ api prāpyate evam eka phala tvena ekam vaikalpikam sāṃkhyam yogam ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati sa eva paṇḍita iti arthaḥ iyān viśeṣa iti āhā bhhu saṃnyāsaḥ jñāna yoga ḥ tu ayogataḥ karma yogāt rte prāptum aśakyaḥ yoga yuktaḥ karma yoga yuktaḥ svayam eva muniḥ ātma manana śīlaḥ sukhena karma yogam sādhayitvā na cireṇa alpena eva kālena brahma adhigacchati ātmānam prāpnoti jñāna yoga yukta ḥ tu mahatā duḥkhena jñāna yogam sādhayati duḥkha sādhya tvāt ātmānam cireṇa prāpnoti iti arthaḥ bhhu karma yoga yukta ḥ tu śāstrīye parama puruṣa ārādhana rūpe viśuddhe karmaṇi vartamānaḥ tena viśuddha manāḥ vijita ātmā svābhyaste te karmaṇi vyāpṛta manaḥ tvena sukhena vijita manāḥ tataḥ eva jitendiyaḥ kartuḥ ātmanaḥ yāthātmya anusandhān aniṣṭhatayā sarva bhūta ātma bhūta ātmā sarveṣām deva ādi bhūtānām ātma bhūta ātmā yasya asau sarva bhūta ātma bhūta ātmā ātmayāthātmyam anusandhānasya hi deva ādīnām svasya ca eka ākāra ātmā deva ādi bhedānām prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣa rūpa tayā ātma ākāratva asaṃbhavāt prakṛti viyuktaḥ sarvatra deva ādi deheṣu jñāna eka ākāra tayā samāna ākāra iti nirdoṣam hi samam brahma iti anantaram eva vakṣyate sa evaṃbhūtaḥ karma kurvan  api anātmani ātma abhimānena na lipyate na saṃbadhyate ataḥ acireṇa ātmānam prāpnoti iti arthaḥ yataḥ saukaryāt chaighryāt ca karma yoga eva śreyān ataḥ tad apekṣitam śṛṇu bhhu bhhu evam ātma tattva vid śrotra ādīni jñāna indriyāṇi vāc ādīni ca karmendriyāṇi praṇāḥ ca sva viṣayeṣu vartanta iti dhārayan anusandhānaḥ na aham kiṃcid karomi iti manyeta jñāna eka svabhāvasya mama karma mūla indriya prāṇa saṃbandha kṛtam īdṛśam kartṛ tvam na svarūpa prayuktam iti manyeta iti arthaḥ bhhu brahma śabdena prakṛtiḥ iha ucyate mama yoniḥ mahat brahma iti hi vakṣyate indriyāṇām prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣa rūpa tvena indriya ākāreṇa avasthitāyām prakṛtau paśyan chṛṇvan ityādi ukta prakāreṇa karmāṇi ādhāya phala saṅgam tyaktvā na eva kiṃcid karomi iti yaḥ karmāṇi karoti sa prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa tayā vartamānaḥ api prakṛti ātma abhimāna rūpeṇa bandha hetunā pāpena na lipyate padma patram iva ambhasā yathā padma patram ambhasā saṃsṛṣṭam api na lipyate tathā na lipyata iti arthaḥ bhhu kāya manaḥ buddhi indriya sādhyam karma svarga ādi phala saṅgam tyaktvā yogina ātma viśuddhaye kuranti ātma gata prācīna karma bandha vināśāya kurvanti iti arthaḥ bhhu bhhu asya deva tiryak manuṣya sthāvara ātmanā prakṛti saṃsargeṇa vartamānasya lokasya deva ādi asādhāraṇam kartṛ tvam tad tad asādhāraṇāni karmāṇi tad tad karma janya deva ādi phala saṃyogam ca ayam prabhuḥ akarma vaśyaḥ svābhāvika svarūpeṇa avasthita ātmā na sṛjati na utpādayati kaḥ tarhi svabhāvaḥ tu pravartate svabhāvaḥ prakṛti vāsanā anādi kāla pravṛtta pūrva pūrva karma janita deva ādi ākāra prakṛti saṃsarga kṛta tad tad ātma abhimāna janita vāsanā akṛtam īdṛśam kartṛ tva ādikam sarvam na svarūpa prayuktam iti arthaḥ bhhu kasyacid sva saṃbandhi tayā abhimatasya putra ādeḥ pāpam duḥkham na ādatte na apanudati kasyacid pratikūla tayā abhimatasya sukṛtam sukham ca na ādatte na apanudati yataḥ ayam vibhuḥ na kvācid kaḥ na deva ādi deha ādyasā dhāraṇa deśaḥ ata eva na kasyacid saṃbandhī na kasyacid pratikūlaḥ ca sarvam idam vāsanā kṛtam evaṃsvabhāvasya katham iyam viparīta vāsanā utpadyate ajñānena āvṛtam jñānam jñāna virodhinā pūrva pūrva karmaṇā sva phala anubhava yogya tvāya asya jñānam āvṛtam saṃkucitam tena jñāna āvaraṇa rūpeṇa karmaṇā deva ādi deha saṃyoga ḥ tad tad ātma abhimāna rūpa moha ḥ ca jāyate tataḥ ca tathāvidha ātmā abhimāna vāsanā tad ucita karma vāsanā ca vāsanātaḥ viparīta ātmā abhimānaḥ karma ārambhaḥ ca upapadyate sarvam jñāna plavena eva vṛjinam saṃtariṣyati  jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā  na hi jñānena sadṛśam pavitram iti pūrva uktam sva kāle saṃgamayati bhhu evam vartamāneṣu sarveṣu ātmasu yeṣām ātmanām ukta lakṣaṇena ātma yāthātmya upadeśa janitena ātma viṣayeṇa aharahar abhyāsa ādheya atiśayena niratiśaya pavitreṇa jñānena tad jñāna āvaraṇam anādi kāla pravṛtta ananta karma saṃcaya rūpam ajñānam nāśitam teṣām tad svābhāvikam param jñānam aparimitam asaṃkucitam ādityavat  sarvam yathā avasthitam prakāśayati teṣām iti vinaṣṭa ajñānānām bahutva abhimānāt ātma svarūpa bahu tvam na tu eva aham jātu na asam iti upakrama avagatam atra spaṣṭataram uktam na ca idam bahu tvam upādhikṛtam vinaṣṭa ajñānānām upādhi gandha abhāvāt teṣām āditya vaj jñānam iti vyatireka nirdeśa āt jñānasya svarūpa anubandhi dharma tvam uktam āditya dṛṣṭāntena ca jñātṛ jñānayoḥ prabhā prabhāvatoḥ iva avasthānam ca tataḥ eva saṃsāra daśāyām jñānasya karmaṇā saṃkocaḥ mokṣa daśāyām vikāsaḥ ca upapannaḥ bhhu tad buddhayaḥ tathāvidhātma darśana adhyavasāyāḥ tad ā ātmānaḥ tad viṣaya manasaḥ tad niṣṭhāḥ tad abhyāsa niratāḥ tad parāyaṇāḥ tad eva parama prayojanam iti manvānāḥ evam abhyasyamānena jñānena nirdhūta prācīna kalmaṣāḥ tathāvidham ātmanam apunarāvṛttim gacchanti yad avasthād ātmanaḥ punarāvṛttiḥ na vidyate sa ātmā apunarāvṛttiḥ svena rūpeṇa avasthitam ātmānam gacchanti iti arthaḥ bhhu vidyā vinaya saṃpanne kevala brāhmaṇe gaḥ hasti śvaśva paca ādiṣu atyanta viṣama ākāra tayā pratīyamāneṣu ātmasu paṇḍitāḥ ātma yāthātmya vidaḥ jñāna eka ākāra tayā sarvatra sama darśinaḥ viṣama ākāra ḥ tu prakṛteḥ na ātmanaḥ ātmā tu sarvatra jñāna eka ākāra tayā sama iti paśyanti iti arthaḥ iha eva taiḥ jitaḥ svargaḥ yeṣām sāmye sthitam manaḥ nirdoṣam hi samam brahma tasmāt brahmaṇi te sthitāḥ iha eva sādhana anuṣṭhāna daśāyām eva taiḥ sargaḥ jitaḥ saṃsāraḥ jitaḥ yeṣām ukta rītyā sarveṣu ātmasu sāmye sthitam manaḥ nirdoṣam hi samam brahma prakṛti saṃsarga doṣa viyukta tayā samam ātma vastu hi bramha ātma sāmye sthitāḥ ced brahmaṇi sthitā eva te brahmaṇi sthitiḥ eva hi sṃsāra jayaḥ ātmasu jñāna eka ākāra tayā sāmyam eva anusandhānā muktā eva iti arthaḥ yena prakāreṇa avathitasya karma yoginaḥ sama darśana rūpaḥ jñana vipākaḥ bhavati tam prakāram upadiśati yādṛśa deha sthasya yad avasthasya prācīna karma vāsanayā yad priyam bhavati yad ca apriyam tad ubhayam prāpya harṣa udvegau na kuryāt katham sthira buddhiḥ sthire ātmani buddhiḥ yasya saḥ sthira buddhiḥ asaṃmūḍhaḥ asthieṇa śarīreṇa sthiram ātmānam ekīkṛtya mohaḥ saṃmohaḥ tad rahitaḥ tad ca katham brahma vid brahmaṇi sthitaḥ upadeśena brahma vid san tasmin brahmaṇi abhyāsa yuktaḥ etad uktam bhavati tattva vidām upadeśena ātma yāthātmya vid bhūtvā tatra eva yatamānaḥ deha ātmā abhimānam parityajya sthira rūpa ātma avalokana priya anubhave vyavasthitaḥ asthire prākṛte priya apriye prāpya harṣa udevegau na kuryāt iti evam uktena prakāreṇa bāhya sparśeṣu ātma vyatirikta viṣaya anubhaveṣu asakta ātmā asakta manāḥ antarātmani eva yaḥ sukham vindati labhate sa prakṛti abhyāsam vihāya brahma yoga yukta ātmā brahma abhyāsa yukta manāḥ brahma anubhava rūpam akṣayam sukham prāpnoti viṣaya indriya sparśa jāḥ ye bhogāḥ duḥkha yonayaḥ te duḥkha udarkāḥ ādi antavantaḥ alpa kāla vartinaḥ hi upalabhyante na teṣu tad yāthātmya vid ramate śarīravimokṣaṇāt prāk ih eva sādhana anuṣṭhāna daśā ayam eva ātma anubhava prītyā kāma krodha udbhavam vegam soḍhum niroddhum yaḥ śaknoti sa yuktaḥ ātma anubhavāya arhaḥ sa eva śarīra vimokṣa uttara kālam ātma anubhava eka sukha ḥ saṃpatsyate yaḥ bāhya viṣaya anubhavam sarvam vihāya antassukhaḥ ātma anubhava eka sukhaḥ antara ārāmaḥ ātmā eka udyānaḥ sva guṇaiḥ ātmā eva sukha vardhakaḥ yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tathā antar jyotiḥ ātma eka jñānaḥ yaḥ vartate sa brahma bhūtaḥ yogī brahma nirvāṇam ātma anubhava sukham prāpnoti cchinna dvaidhāḥ śīta uṣṇa ādi dvandvaiḥ vimuktāḥ yata ātmānaḥ ātmani eva niyamita manasaḥ sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ ātmavat  sarveṣām bhūtānām hiteṣu eva niratāḥ ṛṣayaḥ draṣṭāraḥ ātma avalokana parāḥ ya evambhūtāḥ te kṣīṇa aśeṣa ātma prāpti virodhi kalmaṣāḥ brahma nirvāṇam labhante kāma krodhviyuktānām yatīnām yatana śīlānām yata cetasām niyamita manasām vijita ātmanām vijita manasām brahma nirvāṇam abhitaḥ vartate evaṃbhūtānām hasta stham brahma nirvāṇam iti arthaḥ yata indriya manaḥ buddhiḥ muniḥ mokṣa parāyaṇaḥ vigata icchā bhaya krodhaḥ yaḥ sadā mukta eva saḥ bāhyān viṣaya sparśān bahiḥ kṛtvā bāhya indriya vyāpāram sarvam upasaṃhṛtya yoga yogya āsane ṛjukāya upaviśya cakṣuṣī bhruvoḥ antare nāsā agre vinyasya nāsā abhyantara cāriṇau prāṇa apānau samau kṛtvā ucchvāsa niśvāsau sama gatī kṛtvā ātma avalokanāt anyatra pravṛtti anarha indriya manaḥ buddhiḥ tataḥ eva vigata icchā bhaya krodhaḥ mokṣa parāyaṇaḥ mokṣa eka prayojanaḥ muniḥ ātma avalokana śīlaḥ yaḥ saḥ sadā mukta eva sādhya daśāyām iva sādhana daśāyām api mukta eva iti arthaḥ yajña tapasām bhoktāram sarva loka maheśvaram sarva bhūtānām suhṛdam mām jñātvā śāntim ṛcchati karma yoga karaṇa eva sukham ṛcchati sarva loka maheśvaram sarveṣām loka īśvarāṇām api īśvaram tam īśvarāṇām paramam maheśvaram iti hi śrūyate mām sarva loka maheśvaram sarva suhṛdam jñātvā mad ārādhana rūpaḥ karma yoga iti sukhena tatra pravartata iti arthaḥ suhṛda ārādhanāya hi sarve pravartante uktaḥ karma yogaḥ sa parikaraḥ idānīm jñāna yoga karma yoga sādhya ātma avalokana rūpa yoga abhyāsa vidhiḥ ucyate tatra karma yogasya nirapekṣa yoga sādhana tvam draḍhayitum jñāna ākāraḥ karma yogaḥ yoga śiraskaḥ anūdyate karma phalam svarga ādikam anāśritaḥ kāryam karma anuṣṭhānam eva kāryam sarva ātmanā asmad suhṛd bhūta parama puruṣa ārādhana rūpa tayā karma eva mama prayojanam na tad sādhyam kiṃcid iti yaḥ karma karoti sa saṃnyāsī ca jñāna yoga niṣṭhaḥ ca yogī ca karma yoga niṣṭhaḥ ca ātma avalokana rūpa yoga sādhana bhūta ubhaya niṣṭha iti arthaḥ na niragniḥ na ca akriyaḥ na codita yajña ādi karmasu apravṛttaḥ na ca kevala jñāna niṣṭhaḥ tasya hi jña na niṣṭhā eva karma yoga niṣṭhasya tu ubhayam asti iti abhiprāyaḥ yam saṃnyāsa iti jñāna yoga iti ātma yāthātmya jñānam iti prāhuḥ tam karma yogam eva viddhi tad upapādayati na hi asaṃnyasta saṃkalpaḥ yogī bhavati kaścana ātma yāthātmya anusandhānena anātmani prakṛtau ātma saṅkalpaḥ saṃnyastaḥ parityaktaḥ yena sa saṃnyasta saṅkalpaḥ anevaṃbhūtaḥ asaṃnyasta saṅkalpaḥ na hi ukteṣu karma yogiṣu anevaṃbhūtaḥ kaścana karma yogī bhavati yasya sarve samārambhāḥ kāma saṅkalpa varjitāḥ iti hi uktam yogam ātma avalokanam prāptum icchā ūḥ mumukṣoḥ karma yoga eva kāraṇam ucyate tasya eva yoga ārūḍhasya pratiṣṭhita yogasya eva śamaḥ karma nivṛttiḥ kāraṇam ucyate yāvat ātma avalokana rūpa mokṣa avāpti karma kāryam iti arthaḥ yadā ayam yogī tu ātma eka anubhava svabhāvatayā indriya artheṣu ātma vyatirikta prākṛta viṣayeṣu tad saṃbandhiṣu ca karmasu na anuṣajjate na saṅgam arhati tadā hi sarva saṅkalpa samnyāsī yoga ārūḍha iti ucyate tasmāt ārurukṣoḥ viṣaya anubhava arha tayā tad ananuṣaṅga abhyāsa rūpaḥ karma yoga eva yoga niṣpatti kāraṇam ataḥ viṣayān anuṣaṅga abhyāsa rūpam karma yogam eva ārurukṣuḥ kuryāt ātmanā manasā viṣayān anuṣaktena ātmānam uddharet tad viparītena manasā ātmānam na avasādayet ātmā eva mana eva hi ātmanaḥ bandhuḥ tad eva ātmanaḥ ripuḥ yena puruṣeṇa svena eva sva manaḥ viṣayebhyaḥ jitam tad manaḥ tasya bandhuḥ anātmanaḥ ajita manasaḥ svakīyam eva manaḥ svasya śatruvat śatru tve varteta sva niśśreyasa viparīte varteta iti arthaḥ yathā uktam bhagavatā parāśareṇa api mana eva manuṣyāṇām kāraṇam bandha mokṣayoḥ bandhāya viṣaya āsaṅgi muktyā eva nirviṣayam manaḥ śīta uṣṇa sukha duḥkheṣu māna avamānayoḥ ca jita ātmanaḥ jita manasaḥ vikāra rahita manasaḥ praśāntasya manasi paramātmā samāhitaḥ samyak āhitaḥ sva rūpeṇa avasthitaḥ pratyagātmā atra paramātmā iti ucyate tasya eva prakṛta tvāt tasya api pūrva pūrva avasthā apekṣayā paramātma tvāt ātmā param samāhita iti vā anvayaḥ jñāna vijñāna tṛpta ātmā ātma svarūpa viṣayeṇa jñānena tasya ca prakṛti visajātīya ākāra viṣayeṇa jñānena ca tṛpta manāḥ kūṭasthaḥ deva ādi avasthāsu anuvartamāna sarva sādhāraṇa jñāna eka ākāra ātmani sthitaḥ tataḥ eva vijita indriyaḥ sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanaḥ prakṛti vivikta svarūpa niṣṭhatayā prākṛta vastu viśeṣeṣu bhogya tva abhāvāl loṣṭa aśma kāñcaneṣu sama prayojanaḥ yaḥ karma yogī sa yukta iti ucyate ātma avalokana rūpa yoga abhyāsa arha iti ucyate vayaḥ viśeṣa anaṅgīkāreṇa sva hita eṣiṇaḥ suhṛdaḥ savayasaḥ hita eṣiṇaḥ mitrāṇi arayaḥ nimittataḥ anartha icchavaḥ ubhaya hetu abhāvāt ubhaya rahitā udāsīnāḥ janmata eva ubhaya rahitā madhyasthāḥ janmata eva anicchā icchavaḥ dveṣyāḥ janmata eva hita eṣiṇaḥ bandhavaḥ sādhavaḥ dharma śīlāḥ pāpāḥ pāpa śīlāḥ ātma eka prayojana tayā suhṛd mitra ādibhiḥ prayojana abhāvāt virodha abhāvāt ca teṣu sama buddhiḥ yoga abhyāsa arha tve viśiṣyate yogī ukta prakāra karma yoga niṣṭhaḥ satatam aharahar yoga kāle ātmānam yuñjīta ātmānam yuktam kurvīta sva darśana niṣṭham kurvīta iti arthaḥ rahasi jana varjite niśśabde deśe sthitaḥ ekākī tatra api na sa dvitīyaḥ yata citta ātmā yata citta manaskaḥ nirāśīḥ ātma vyatirikte kṛtsne vastuni nirapekṣaḥ aparigrahaḥ tad vyatirikte kasmiṃścid api mamatā rahitaḥ tatra ekāgram manaḥ kṛtvā yata citta indriya kriyaḥ upaviśya āsane yuñjyāt yogam ātma viśuddhaye śucau deśe aśucibhiḥ puruṣaiḥ anadhiṣṭhite aparigṛhīte ca aśucibhiḥ vastubhiḥ aspṛṣṭe ca pavitra bhūte deśe dārva ādi nirmitam na ati ucchritam na ati nīcam cela ajina kuśa uttaram āsanam pratiṣṭhāpya tasmin manaḥ prasāda kare sa apāśraye upaviśya yoga ekāgram manaḥ kṛtvā yata citta indriya kriyaḥ sarva ātmanā upasaṃhṛta citta indriya kriyaḥ ātma viśuddhaye bandha nivṛttaye yogam yuñjyāt atma avalokanam kurvīta praśānta ātmā vigata bhīḥ brahmacāri vrate sthitaḥ manaḥ saṃyamya mad cittaḥ yukta āsīta mad paraḥ kāya śiraḥ grīvam samam acalam sa apāśraya tayā sthiram dhārayan diśaḥ ca anavaloakayan sva nāsikā agram saṃprekṣya praśānta ātmā atyanta nirvṛta manāḥ vigata bhīr brahmacarya yuktaḥ manaḥ saṃyamya mad cittaḥ yuktaḥ avahitaḥ mad para āsīta mām eva cintyan āsīta evam mayi parasmin brahmaṇi puruṣottame manasaḥ śubha āśraye sadā ātmānam manaḥ yuñjan niyata mānasaḥ mad sparśavitrīkṛta mānasatayā niścala mānasaḥ mām eva cintayan mad saṃsthām nirvāṇa paramām śāntim adhigacchati nirvāṇa kāṣṭhā rūpām mad saṃsthām mayi saṃsthitām śāntim adhigacchati yukta āhāra vihārasya yukta ceṣṭasya karmasu yukta svapna avabodhasya yogaḥ bhavati duḥkha hā ati aśana anaśane yoga virodhinī ati vihāra avihārau ca tathā atimātra svapna jāgarye tathā ca ati āyāsānāyāsau mita āhāra vihārasya mita āyāsasya mita svapna avabodhasya sakala duḥkha hā bandha nāśanaḥ yogaḥ saṃpannaḥ bhavati yadā prayojana viṣayam cittam ātmani eva viniyatam viśeṣeṇa niyatam niratiśaya prayojana tayā tatra eva niyatam niścalam avatiṣṭhate tadā sarva kāmebhyaḥ nisspṛhaḥ san yukta iti ucyate yoga arha iti ucyate nivāta sthaḥ dīpaḥ yathā na iṅgate na calati acalaḥ sa prabhaḥ tiṣṭhati yata cittasya nivṛtta sakala itara manaḥ vṛtteḥ yoginaḥ ātmani yogam yuñjataḥ ātma svarūpasya sopamā nivāta stha tayā niścala saprabhadīpavan nivṛtta sakala manaḥ vṛtti tayā niścalaḥ jñāna prabha ātmā tiṣṭhaī iti arthaḥ yatra uparamate cittam niruddham yoga sevayā yatra ca eva ātmanā ātmānam paśyan ātmani tuṣyati yam labdhvā ca aparam lābham manyate na adhikam tataḥ yasmin sthitaḥ na duḥkhena guruṇā api vicālyate tam vidyāt duḥkha saṃyoga viyogam yoga saṃjñitam sa niścayena yoktavyaḥ yogaḥ anirviṇṇa cetasā yoga sevayā hetunā sarvatra niruddham cittam yatra yoge uparamate atiśayita sukham idam iti ramate yatra ca yoge ātmanā manasā ātmānam paśyan anya nirapekṣam ātmani eva tuṣyati yad tad atīndriyam ātma buddhi eka grāhyam ātyantikam sukham yatra ca yoge vetti anubhavati yatra ca yoge sthitaḥ sukha atirekeṇa tattvataḥ tad bhāvān na calati yam yogam labdhvā yogāt virataḥ tam eva kāṅkṣamāṇaḥ na aparam lābham tataḥ adhikam manyate yasmin  ca yoge sthitaḥ virataḥ api guṇavat putra viyoga ādinā guruṇā api duḥkhena na vicālyate tam duḥkha saṃyoga viyogam duḥkha saṃyoga pratyanīka ākāram yoga śabda abhidheyam vidyāt sa evaṃrūpaḥ yoga iti ārambha daśāyām niścayena anirviṇṇa cetasā hṛṣṭa cetasā yogaḥ yoktavyaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ uparamet buddhyā dhṛti gṛhītayā ātma saṃstham manaḥ kṛtvā na kiṃcid api cintayet sparśa jāḥ saṅkalpa jāḥ ca iti dvividhāḥ kāmāḥ sparśa jāḥ śīta uṣṇa ādayaḥ saṅkalpa jāḥ putra kṣetra ādayaḥ tatra saṅkalpa prabhavāḥ sva rūpeṇa eva tyaktum śakyāḥ tān sarvān manasā eva tad anvaya anusandhānena tyaktvā sparśa jeṣu avarjanīyeṣu tad nimitta harṣa udvegau tyaktvā samantataḥ sarvasmāt viṣayāt sarvam indriya grāmam viniyamya śanaiḥ śanaiḥ dhṛti gṛhītayā viveka viṣayayā buddhyā sarvasmāt ātma vyatiriktāt uparamya ātma saṃstham manaḥ kṛtvā na kiñcid api cintayet cala svabhāva tayā ātmani asthiram manaḥ yataḥ yataḥ viṣaya prāvaṇya hetoḥ bahiḥ niścarati tataḥ tataḥ yatnena manaḥ niyamya ātmani eva atiśayita sukha bhāvanayā vaśam nayet praśānta manasam ātmani niścala manasam ātmani asta manasam tad eva hetoḥ dagdha aśeṣa kalmaṣam tataḥ eva śānta rajasam vinaṣṭa rajaḥ guṇam tataḥ eva brahma bhūtam sva svarūpeṇa avasthitam enam yoginam ātma svarūpa anubhava rūpam uttamam sukham upaiti hi iti hetau uttama sukha rūpa tvāt ātma svarūpasya iti arthaḥ evam ukta prakāreṇa ātmānam yuñjan tena eva vigata prācīna samasta kalmaṣaḥ brahma saṃsparśam brahma anubhava rūpam sukham atyantam aparimitam sukhena anāyāsena sadā aśunute sva ātmanaḥ pareṣām ca bhūtānām prakṛti viyukta svarūpāṇām jñāna eka ākāra tayā sāmyāt vaiṣamyasya ca prakṛti gata tvāt yoga yukta ātmā prakṛti viyukteṣu ātmasu sarvatra jñāna eka ākāra tayā sama darśanaḥ sarva bhūta stham sva ātmānam sarva bhūtāni ca sva ātmani īkṣate sarva bhūta samāna ākāram sva ātmānam sva ātma samāna ākārāṇi ca sarva bhūtāni paśyati iti arthaḥ ekasmin ātmani dṛṣṭe sarvasya ātma vastunaḥ tad sāmyāt sarvam ātma vastu dṛṣṭam bhavati iti arthaḥ sarvatra sama darśanaḥ iti vacanāt  yaḥ ayam yoga ḥ tvayā proktaḥ sāmyena iti anubhāṣaṇa āt ca nirdoṣam hi samam brahma iti vacanāt ca tataḥ api vipāka daśa āpannaḥ mama sādharmyam upāgataḥ nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti ucyamānam sarvasya ātma vastunaḥ vidhūta puṇya pāpasya sva rūpeṇa avasthitasya mad sāmyam paśyan yaḥ sarvatra ātma vastuni mām paśyati sarvam ātma vastu ca mayi paśyati anyonya sāmyāt anyatara darśanena anyatara d api īdṛśam iti paśyati tasya sva ātma svarūpam paśyataḥ aham tad sāmyān na praṇaśyāmi na adarśanam upayāmi mama api mām paśyataḥ mad sāmyāt sva ātmānam mad samam avalokayan sa na adarśanam upayāti yoga daśāyām sarva bhūta sthitam mām asaṃkucita jñāna eka ākāra tayā eka tvam āsthitaḥ prākṛta bheda parityāgena su dṛḍham yaḥ bhajate sa yogī vyutthāna kāle api yathā tathā vartamānaḥ sva ātmānam sarva bhūtāni ca paśyan mayi vartate mām eva paśyati sva ātmani sarva bhūteṣu ca sarvadā mad sāmyam eva paśyati iti arthaḥ sva ātmanaḥ ca anyeṣām ca ātmanām asaṃkucita jñāna eka ākāratayā upamyena sva ātmani ca anyeṣu ca sarvatra vartamānam putra janma ādi rūpam sukham tad maraṇa ādi rūpam ca duḥkham asaṃbandha sāmyāt samam yaḥ paśyati para putra janma maraṇa ādi samam sva putra janma maraṇa ādikam yaḥ paśyati iti arthaḥ sa yogī paramaḥ mataḥ yoga kāṣṭhām gataḥ mataḥ yaḥ ayam deva manuṣya ādi bhedena jīveśvara bhedena ca atyata bhinnatayā etā antam kālam anubhūteṣu sarveṣu ātmasu jñāna eka ākāra tayā paraspara sāmyena akarma vaśya tayā ca īśvara sāmyena sarvatra sama darśana rūpaḥ yoga ḥ tvayā proktaḥ etasya yogasya sthirām sthitim na paśyāmi manasaḥ cañcala tvāt tathā anavarata abhyasta viṣayeṣu api svata eva cañcalam puruṣeṇa ekatra avasthāpayitum aśakyam manaḥ puruṣam balāt pramathya dṛḍham anyatra carati tasya sva abhyasta viṣayeṣu api cañcala svabhāvasya manasaḥ tad viparīta ākāra ātmani sthāpayitum nigraham pratikūla gateḥ mahā vātasya vyajana ādinā eva su duṣkaram aham manye manaḥ nigraha upāyaḥ vaktavya iti abhiprāyaḥ asaṃyata ātmanā yogaḥ duṣprāpa iti me matiḥ vaśya ātmanā tu yatatā śakyaḥ avāptum upāyataḥ cala svabhāva tayā manaḥ durnigraham eva iti atra na saṃśayaḥ tathā api ātmanaḥ guṇa ākaratva abhyāsa janita ābhimukhyena ātma vyatirikteṣu doṣa ākara tva janita vaitṛṣṇyena ca kathaṃcid gṛhyate asaṃyata ātmanā ajita manasā mahatā api balena yogaḥ duṣprāpa ea upāyataḥ tu vaśya ātmanā pūrva uktena mad ārādhana rūpeṇa antargata jñānena karmaṇā jita manasā yatamānena ayam eva sama darśana rūpaḥ yogaḥ avāptum śakyaḥ kaccit na ubhaya vibhraṣṭa ḥ chinna abhram iva naśyati apratiṣṭhaḥ mahā bāhaḥ vimūḍhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ pathi etam me saṃśayam kṛṣṇa cchetum arhasy aśeṣataḥ tvad anyaḥ saṃśayasya asya cchettā na hi upapadyate śraddhayā yoge pravṛttaḥ dṛḍhatara abhyāsa rūpa yatana vaikalyena yoga saṃsiddhim aprāpya yogāt calita mānasaḥ kām gatim gacchati ubhaya vibhraṣṭaḥ ayam cchinna abhram iva kaccit na naśyati yathā megha śakalaḥ pūrvasmāt bṛhataḥ meghāc chinnaḥ param bṛhantam megham aprāpya madhye vinaṣṭaḥ bhavati tathā eva kaccit na naśyati katham ubhaya vibhraṣṭa tā apratiṣṭhaḥ vimūḍhaḥ brahmaṇaḥ pathi iti yathā avasthitam svarga ādi sādhana bhūtam karma phala abhisandhi rahitasya asya puruṣasya sva phala sādhana tvena pratiṣṭhā na bhavati iti apratiṣṭhaḥ prakrānte brahmaṇaḥ pathi vimūḍhaḥ tasmāt pathaḥ pracyutaḥ ataḥ ubhaya vibhraṣṭa tayā kim ayam naśyati eva uta na naśyati tam enam saṃśayam aśeṣataḥ chettum arhasi svataḥ pratyakṣeṇa yugapad sarvam sadā paśyataḥ tvad taḥ anyaḥ saṃśayasya asya chettā na hi upapadyate śraddhayā yoge prakrāntasya tasmāt pracyutasya iha ca amutra ca vināśaḥ na vidyate prākṛta svarga ādi bhoga anubhave brahma anubhave ca abhilaṣitān avāpti rūpaḥ pratyavāya ākhyā aniṣṭa avāpti rūpa ḥ ca vināśaḥ na vidyata iti arthaḥ na hi niratiśaya kalyāṇa rūpa yoga kṛt kaścid kāla traye api durgatim gacchati yad jātīya bhoga abhikāṅkṣayā yogāt pracyutaḥ ayam ati puṇya kṛtām prāpyān lokān prāpya tad jātīyān ati kalyāṇān bhogān yoga māhātmyāt eva bhuñjānaḥ yāvat tad bhoga tṛṣṇā avasānam śaśvatīḥ samāḥ tatra uṣitvā tasmin bhoge vitṛṣṇaḥ śucīnām śrīmatām yoga upakrama yogyānām kule yoga upakrame bhraṣṭaḥ yoga māhātmya at jāyate paripakva yogaḥ calita ḥ ced yoginām dhīmatām yogam kurvatām svayam eva yoga upadeśa kṣamāṇām mahatām kule bhavati tad etad ubhayavidham yoga yogyānām yoginām ca kule janma loke prākṛtānām durlabhataram etad tu yoga māhātmya kṛtam pūrva abhyāsena tena eva hriyate hi avaśaḥ api saḥ tatra janmani paurvadaihikam tam eva yoga viṣayam buddhi saṃyogam labhate tataḥ supta prabuddhavat  bhūyaḥ saṃsiddhau yatate yathā na antarāyahataḥ bhavati tathā yatate tena pūrva abhyāsena pūrveṇa yoga viṣyeṇa abhyāsena saḥ yoga bhraṣṭaḥ hi avaśaḥ api yoga eva hriyate prasiddham hi etad yoga māhātmyam iti arthaḥ apravṛtta yogaḥ yoge jijñāsuḥ api tataḥ calita mānasaḥ punar api tām eva jijñāsām prāpya karma yoga ādikam yogam anuṣṭhāya śabdabrahma ativartate śabdabrahma deva manuṣya pṛthivī antarikṣa svarga ādi śabda abhilāpa yogyam brahma prakṛtiḥ prakṛti bandhāt vimuktaḥ deva manuṣya ādi śabda abhilāpa anarham jñāna ānanda ekatānam ātmānam prāpnoti iti arthaḥ yata evam yoga māhātmyam tataḥ aneka janma arjita puṇya sañcayaiḥ saṃśuddha kilbiṣaḥ saṃsiddhiḥ saṃjātaḥ prayatnāt yatamānaḥ tu yogī calitaḥ api punar parām gatim yāti eva kevala tapobhiḥ yaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ sādhyate ātma jñāna vyatiriktaiḥ jñāna aiḥ ca yaḥ yaḥ ca kevalaiḥ aśvamedha ādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ tebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ adhika puruṣa artha sādhana tvāt yogasya tapasvibhyaḥ jñānibhyaḥ karmibhyaḥ ca adhikaḥ yogī tasmāt yogī bhava arjuna yoginām iti pañcamī arthe ṣaṣṭhī sarva bhūta stham ātmānam  ityādinā caturvidhā yoginaḥ pratipāditāḥ teṣu anantargata tvāt vakṣyamāṇasya yoginaḥ na nirdhāraṇe ṣaṣṭhī saṃbhavati api sarveṣām iti sarva śabda nirdiṣṭāḥ tapasvi prabhṛtayaḥ tatra api uktena nyāyena pañcamī arthaḥ grahītavyaḥ yogibhyaḥ api sarvebhyaḥ vakṣyamāṇaḥ yogī yuktatamaḥ tad apekṣayā avara tve tapasvi prabhṛtīnām yoginām ca na kaścid viśeṣa iti arthaḥ meru apekṣayā sarṣapāṇām iva yadi api sarṣapeṣu anyonya nyūna adhika bhāvaḥ vidyate tathā api meru apekṣayā avara tu nirdeśaḥ samānaḥ mad priya tva atirekena ananya dhāraṇa svabhāvatayā mad gatena antarātmanā manasā śraddhāvān atyartha mad priya tvena kṣaṇa mātra viśleṣa asaha tayā mad prāpti pravṛttau tvarāvān yaḥ mām bhajate mām vicitra ananta bhogya bhoktṛ varga bhoga upakaraṇa bhoga sthāna paripūrṇa nikhila jagat udaya vibhava laya līlam aspṛṣṭa aśeṣa doṣān avadhika atiśaya jñāna balāi śvarya vīrya śakti tejaḥ prabhṛti asaṅkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa nidhim sva abhimata anurūpa eka rūpa acintya divya adbhuta nitya niravadya niratiśayāujjvalya saundarya saugandhya saukumārya lāvaṇya yauvana ādi ananta guṇa nidhi divy vāc manasā aparicchedya svarūpa svabhāvam apārakāruṇya sauśīlya vātsalya udārya mahā udadhim anālocita viśeṣa aśeṣa loka śaraṇyam praṇata ārti haram āśrita vātsalya eka jaladhim akhilam anujanayana viṣaya tām gatam ajahatsva svabhāvam vasudeva gṛhe avatīrṇam anavadhika atiśaya tejasā nikhilam jagad bhāsayantam ātma kāntyā viśvam āpyāyayantam bhajate sevate upāsta iti arthaḥ sa me yuktatamaḥ mataḥ sa sarvebhyaḥ śreṣṭatamaḥ iti sarvam sarvadā yathā avasthitam svata eva sākṣātkurvan aham manye mayi ābhimukhyena asakta manāḥ mad priya tva atirekeṇa mad sva rūpeṇa guṇaiḥ ca ceṣṭitena mad vibhūtyā viśleṣe sati tad kṣaṇāt eva viśīryamāṇa svarūpa tayā mayi sugāḍham baddha manāḥ tathā mada śrayaḥ svayam ca mayā vinā viśīryamāṇa tayā mad āśrayaḥ mad eka ādhāraḥ mad yogam yuñjan yoktum pravṛttaḥ yoga viṣaya bhūtam mām asaṃśayam nissaṃśayam samagram sakalam yathā jñāsyasi yna jñānena uktena jñāsyasi tad jñānam avahita manāḥ tvam śṛṇu aham te mad viṣayam idam jñānam vijñānena saha aśeṣataḥ vakṣayāmi vijñānan vivikta ākāra viṣayam jñānam yathā aham mad vyatiriktāt samasta cit acit vastu jātān nikhila heya pratyanīka tayā nānā vidhāna vadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa ananta mahā vibhūti tayā ca viviktaḥ tena vivikta viṣaya jñānena saha mad sva rūpa viṣaya jñānam vakṣyāmi kim bahunā yad jñānam jñātvā mayi punar anyaj jñātavyam na avaśiṣyate manuṣyāḥ śāstra adhikāra yogyāḥ teṣām sahasreṣu kaścid eva siddhi paryantam yatate siddhi paryantam yatamānānām sahasreṣu kaścid eva mām viditvā matta ḥ siddhaye yatate mad vidān sahasreṣu kaścid eva tattvataḥ yathā avasthitam mām vetti na kaścid iti abhiprāyaḥ sa mahātmā su durlabhaḥ  mām tu veda na kaścana iti hi vakṣyate asya vicitra ananta bhogya bhoga upakaraṇa bhoga sthāna rūpeṇa avasthitasya jagataḥ prakṛtiḥ iyam gandha ādi guṇaka pṛthi vyap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa ādi rūpeṇa manaḥ prabhṛti indriya rūpeṇa mahat ahaṃkāra rūpeṇa ca aṣṭadhā bhinnā madīya iti viddhi iyam mama aparā prakṛtiḥ itaḥ tu anyām itaḥ acetanāyāḥ cetana bhogya bhūtāyāḥ prakṛteḥ visajātīya ākārām jīva bhūtām parām tasyāḥ bhoktṛ tvena pradhāna bhūtām cetana rūpām madīyām prakṛtim viddhi yayā idam acetanam kṛtsnam jagad dhāryate etad cetanā cetana samaṣṭi rūpa madīya prakṛti dvaya yonīni brahma ādi stamba paryantāni uccāvaca bhāvena avasthitāni cit acit miśrāṇi madīyāni sarvāṇi bhūtāni iti upadhāraya madīya prakṛti dvaya yonīni hi tāni madīyāni eva tathā prakṛti dvaya yoni tvena kṛtsnasya jagataḥ tayoḥ dvayoḥ api mad yoni tvena madīya tvena ca kṛtsnasya jagataḥ aham eva prabhavaḥ aham eva ca pralayaḥ aham eva ca śeṣī iti upadhāraya tayoḥ cit acit samaṣṭi bhūtayoḥ prakṛti puruṣayoḥ api parama puruṣa yoni tvam śruti smṛti siddham mahān avyakte līyate avyaktam akṣare līyate akṣaram tamasi līyate tamaḥ pare deva ekībhavati  viṣṇoḥ svarūpāt paratodite dve rūpe prdhānam puruṣaḥ ca vipra  prakṛtiḥ yā mayā ākhyātā vyakta avyakta svarūpiṇī puruṣaḥ ca api ubhau  etau līyate parama ātmani paramātmā ca sarveṣām ādhāraḥ parameśvaraḥ viṣṇu nāmā sa vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate sarvam idam cit acit vastu jātam kārya avastham kāraṇa avastham ca mad śarīra bhūtam sūtre maṇi gaṇavat atma tayā avasthite mayi protam āśritam yasya pṛthivī śarīram  yasya ātmā śarīram  eṣa sarva bhūta antarātma apahata pāpmā divyaḥ deva ekaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ iti ātma śarīra bhāvena avasthānam ca jagat brahmaṇoḥ antaryāmi brāhmaṇa ādiṣu siddham puṇyaḥ gandhaḥ pṛthivyām ca tejaḥ ca asmi vibhāvasau jīvanam sarva bhūteṣu tapaḥ ca asmi tapasviṣu bījam mām sarva bhūtānām viddhi pārtha sanātanam buddhiḥ buddhimatām asmi tejaḥ tejasvinām aham balam balavantān ca aham kāma rāga vivarjitam dharma aviruddhaḥ bhūteṣu kāmaḥ asmi bharata ṛṣabha ete sarve vilakṣaṇā bhāvā matta eva utpannāḥ mad śeṣa bhūtāḥ mad śarīra tayā mayi eva avasthitāḥ ataḥ tad tad prakāraḥ aham eva āvathitaḥ kim viśiṣya abhidhīyate sāttvikā rājasāḥ tāmasāḥ ca jagati deha tvena indriya tvena bhogya tvena tad tad dhtetutvena ca avasthitā ye bhavāḥ tān sarvān matta eva utpannān viddhi te mad śarīra tayā mayi eva avasthitā iti ca na tu aham teṣu na aham kadācid api tad āyatta sthitiḥ anyatra ātma āyatta sthiti tve api śarīrasya śarīreṇa ātmanaḥ sthitau  api upakāraḥ vidyate mama tu taiḥ na kaścid tathāvidha upakāraḥ kevala līlā eva prayojanam iti arthaḥ tad evam cetana acetana ātmakam kṛtsnam jagan madīyam kāle kāle matta eva utpadyate mayi ca pralīyate mayi eva avasthitam mad śarīra bhūtam mad ātmakam ca iti aham eva kāraṇa avasthāyām kāryau athāyām ca sarva śarīra tayā sarva prakāraḥ avasthitaḥ ataḥ kāraṇa tvena śeṣi tvena ca jñāna ādi asaṅkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa aiḥ ca aham eva sarvaiḥ prakāraiḥ parataraḥ mattaḥ anyat kena api kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇena parataram na vidyate evaṃbhūtam mām tribhyaḥ sāttvika rājasa tāmasa guṇa mayebhyaḥ bhāvebhyaḥ param mada sādhāraṇaiḥ kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇaiḥ tad tad bhogya tā prakāraiḥ ca param utkṛṣṭatamam avyayam sadā eka rūpam api taiḥ eva tribhiḥ guṇa mayaiḥ nihīnataraiḥ kṣaṇa dhvaṃsibhiḥ pūrva karma anuguṇa deha indriya bhogya tvena avasthitaiḥ padārthaiḥ mohitam deva tiryak manuṣya sthāvara ātmanā avasthitam sarvam idam jagan na abhijānāti cd mām eva satya saṅkalpam parama kāruṇikam anālocita viśeṣa aśeṣa loka śaraṇyam ye śaraṇam prapadyante te etām madīyām guṇa mayīm māyām taranti māyām utsṛjya mām eva upāsata iti arthaḥ duṣkṛtinaḥ pāpa karmāṇaḥ mām na prapadyate duṣkṛta tāratamyena te caturvidhā bhavanti mūḍhāḥ nara adhamāḥ māyayā apahṛta jñānāḥ āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ iti mūḍhāḥ viparīta jñānāḥ pūrva ukta prakāreṇa bhagavat śeṣa tā eka rasam ātmānam bhogya jātam ca su śeṣa tayā manyamānāḥ nara adhamāḥ sāmānyena jñāte api mad svarūpe madaunmukhyān arhāḥ māyayā apahṛta jñānāḥ mad viṣayam mad aiśvarya viṣayam ca jñānam yeṣām tad asaṃbhāvanā pādinībhiḥ kūṭa yuktibhiḥ apahṛtam te tathā uktāḥ āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ mad viṣayam mad aiśvarya viṣayam ca jñānam su dṛḍham upapannam yeṣām dvaiṣāya eva bhavati te āsuram bhāvam āśritāḥ uttarottarāḥ pāpiṣṭhatamāḥ sukṛtinaḥ puṇya karmāṇaḥ mām śaraṇam upagamya mām eva bhajante te ca sukṛta tāratamyena caturvidhāḥ sukṛta garīyaḥ tu ena pratipatti vaiśeṣyāt uttarottarā adhikatamā bhavanti ārtaḥ pratiṣṭhā hīnaḥ bhraṣṭāiśvaryaḥ punar tad prāpti kāmaḥ artha arthī aprāptāiśvarya tayā aiśvarya kāmaḥ tayoḥ mukha bheda mātram aiśvarya viṣaya tayā aikyāt eka eva adhikāraḥ jijñāsuḥ prakṛti viyukta ātma svarūpa avāpti icchuḥ jñānam eva asya svarūpam iti jijñāsuḥ iti uktam jñānī ca itaḥ tu anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām ityādinā abhihita bhagavat śeṣa tā ekarasa ātma svarūpa vid prakṛti viyukta kevala ātmani aparyavasyan bhagavantam prepsuḥ bhagavantam eva parama prāpyam manvānaḥ teṣām jñānī viśiṣyate kutaḥ nitya yukta eka bhaktiḥ iti ca jñāninaḥ hi mad eka prāpyasya mayā yogaḥ nityaḥ itarayoḥ tu yāvat sva abhilaṣita prāpti mayā yogaḥ tathā jñāninaḥ mayi ekasmin  eva bhaktiḥ itarayoḥ tu sva abhilaṣite tad sādhana tvena mayi ca ataḥ sa eva viśiṣyate kiñ ca priyaḥ hi jñāninaḥ atyartham aham artha śabdaḥ abhidheya vacanaḥ jñāninaḥ aham yathā priyaḥ tathā mayā sarvajñena sarva śaktinā api abhidhātum na śakyata iti arthaḥ priya tvasya iyattā ra hita tvāt yathā jñāninām agresarasya prahlādasya sa tu āsakta matiḥ kṛṣṇe daśyamānaḥ mahā uragaiḥ na viveda ātmanaḥ gātram tad smṛtyā āhlāda saṃsthitaḥ iti tathā eva saḥ api mama priyaḥ sarva eva ete mām eva upāsata iti udārāḥ vadānyāḥ ye mattaḥ yad kiṃcid api gṛhṇanti te hi mama sarva sva dāyinaḥ jñānī tu ātmā eva me matam tad āyatta dhāraṇaḥ aham iti manye kasmāt evam yasmāt ayam mayā vinā ātma dhāraṇā saṃbhāvanayā mām eva anuttamam prāpyam āsthitaḥ ataḥ tena vinā mama api ātma dhāraṇam na saṃbhavati tataḥ mama ātmā hi saḥ na alpa saṃkhyā saṅkhyātānām puṇya janmanām phalam idam yad mad śeṣa tā ekarasa ātma yāthātmya jñāna pūrvakam mad prapadanam api tu bahūnām janmanām puṇya janmanām ante avasāne vāsudeva śeṣa tā eka rasaḥ aham tad āyatta svarūpa sthiti pravṛttiḥ ca sa ca asaṅkhyeyaiḥ kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇaiḥ parataraḥ iti jñānavān bhūtvā vāsudeva eva mama parama prāpyam prāpakam ca anyat api yad manoratha vartim sa eva mama tad sarvam iti mām prapadyate mām upāste sa mahātmā mahāmanāḥ su durlabhaḥ durlabha taraḥ loke vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti asya ayam eva arthaḥ priyaḥ hi jñāninaḥ atyartham aham  āsthitaḥ sa hi yukta ātmā mām eva anuttamām gatim iti prakramāt jñānavānḥ ca ayam ukta lakṣaṇa eva asya eva pūrva ukta jñāni tvāt bhūmiḥ āpaḥ iti ārabhya ahaṅkāra iti iyam me bhinnā prakṛtiḥ aṣṭadhā aparā iyam itaḥ tu anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām jīva bhūtām iti hi cetana acetana prakṛti dvayasya parama puruṣa śeṣa tā eka rasa tā uktā aham kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ tathā mattaḥ parataram na anyat kiñcid asti dhanañjaya iti ārabhya ye ca eva sāttvikā bhāvā rājasāḥ tāmasāḥ ca ye matta eva iti tān viddhi na tu aham teṣu te mayi sarva eva hi laukikāḥ puruṣāḥ svayā prakṛtyā pāpa vāsanayā guṇa maya bhāva viṣayayā niyatāḥ nitya anvitāḥ taiḥ taiḥ sva vāsanā anurūpaiḥ guṇa mayaiḥ eva kāmaiḥ icchā viṣaya bhūtaiḥ hṛtamad sva rūpa viṣaya jñānāḥ tad tad kāma siddhi artham anya devatāḥ mad vyatiriktāḥ kevala indra ādi devatāḥ tam tam niyamam āsthāya tad tad devatā viśeṣa mātra prīṇa nāsā dhāraṇam niyamam āsthyāya prapadyante tā eva āśritya arcayante tā api devatā madīyāḥ tanavaḥ ya āditye tiṣṭhan yam ādityaḥ na veda yasya ādityaḥ śarīram ityādi śrutibhiḥ pratipāditāḥ madīyāḥ tanava iti ajānan  api yaḥ yaḥ yām yām madīyām āditya ādikām tanum bhaktaḥ śraddhayā arcitum icchati tasya tasya ajānataḥ api mad tanu viṣayā eṣā śraddhā iti anusandhāya tām eva acalām nirvighnām vidadhāmi aham sa tayā nirvighnayā śraddhayā yukta ḥ tasya indra ādeḥ ārādhanam pratīhate tataḥ mad tanubhūta indra ādi devatā ārādhanāt tān eva hi sva abhilaṣitān kāmān mayā eva vihitān labhate yadi api ārādhana kāleārādhya indrāt ayaḥ madīyāḥ tanavaḥ tataḥ eva tad arcanam ca mad ārādhanam iti na jānāti tathā api tasya vastunaḥ mad ārādhana tvāt ārādhaka abhilaṣitam aham eva vidadhāmi teṣām alpa medhasām alpabuddhīnām indra ādi mātra yājinām tad ārādhana phalam alpam antavat ca bhavati kutaḥ devān devayajaḥ yānti yata indra ādīn devān tad yājinaḥ yānti indra ādayaḥ api hi paricchinna bhogāḥ parimita kāla vartinaḥ ca tataḥ tad sāyujyam prāptāḥ taiḥ saha pracyavante mad bhaktā api teṣām eva karmaṇām mad ārādhana rūpa tām jñātvā paricchinna phala saṅgam tyaktvā mad prīṇa na eka prayojanāḥ mām prāpnuvanti na ca punar nivartante mām upetya tu kaunteya punar janma na vidyate iti hi vakṣyate sarvaiḥ karmabhiḥ ārādhyaḥ aham sarva īśvaraḥ vāc manasā aparicchedya svarūpa svabhāvaḥ parama kāruṇyāt aśritya vātsalī āt ca sarva samāśrayaṇīya tvāya ajahatsvabhāva eva vasudeva sūnuḥ avarīrṇa iti mama evam param bhāvam avyayam anuttamam ajānantaḥ prākṛta rāja sūnu samānam itaḥ pūrvam anabhivyaktam idānīm karma vaśāj janma viśeṣam prāpya vyaktim āpannam prāptam mām buddhayaḥ manyante ataḥ mām na āśrayante na karmabhiḥ ārādhayanti ca kṣetrajñā sā dhāraṇa manuṣya tva ādi saṃsthāna yoga ākhya māyayā samāvṛtaḥ aham na sarvasya prakāśaḥ mayi manuṣya tva ādi saṃsthāna darśana mātreṇa mūḍhaḥ ayam lokaḥ mām ativāyu indra karmāṇam ati sūrya agni tejasam upalabhyamānam api ajam avyayam nikhila jagat eka kāraṇam sarveśvaram mām sarva samāśrayaṇīya tvāya manuṣya tva saṃsthānam āsthitam na abhijānāti atītāni vartamānāni anāgatāni ca sarvāṇi bhūtāni aham veda jānāmi mām tu veda na kaścana mayā anusaṃdhīyamāneṣu kāla traya vartiṣu bhūteṣu mām evaṃvidham vāsudevam sarva samāśrayṇīya tvāya avatīrṇam viditvā mām eva samāśrayan na kaścid upalabhyata iti arthaḥ ataḥ jñānī su durlabha eva icchā dveṣābhyām samutthitena śīta uṣṇa ādi dvandva ākhyena mohena sarva bhūtāni sarge janma kāla eva saṃmoham yānti etad uktam bhavati guṇa mayeṣu sukha duḥkha ādi dvandveṣu pūrva pūrva janmani yad viṣayau icchā dveṣau abhyastau tad vāsanayā punar api janma kāla eva tad eva dvandva ākhyam icchā dveṣa viṣaya tvena samutthitam bhūtānām mohanam bhavati tena mohena sarva bhūtāni saṃmoham yānti tad viṣaya icchā dveṣa svabhāvāni bhavanti na mad samśleṣa viyoga sukha duḥkha svabhāvāni jñānī tu mad saṃśleṣa viyoga eka sukha duḥkha svabhāvaḥ na tad svabhāvam kim api bhūtam jāyate iti yeṣām tu aneka janma arjitena utkṛṣṭa puṇya saṃcayena guṇa maya dvandveccchā dveṣa hetu bhūtam mada aunmukhya virodhi ca anādi kāla pravṛttam pāpam anta gatam kṣīṇam te pūrva uktena sukṛta tāratamyena mām śaraṇam anuprapadya guṇa mayān mohāt vinirmuktāḥ jarā maraṇa mokṣāya mahate ca aiśvaryāya mad prāptaye ca dṛḍha vratāḥ dṛḍha saṅkalpāḥ mām eva bhajante jarā maraṇa mokṣāya prakṛti viyukta ātma svarūpa darśanāya mām āśritya ye yatante te tad brahma viduḥ adhyātmam tu kṛtsnam viduḥ karma ca akhilam viduḥ atra ya iti punar nirdeśāt pūrva nirdiṣṭa vyaḥ anye adhikāriṇaḥ jñāyante sa adhibhūtam sa adhidaivam mām aiśvarya arthinaḥ ye viduḥ iti etad anuvāda sarūpam api aprāpta artha tvāt vidhāyakam eva tathā sa adhiyajñam iti api trayāṇām adhikāriṇām aviśeṣeṇa vidhīyate artha svabhāvyāt trayāṇām hi nitya naimittika rūpa mahā yajña ādi anuṣṭhānam avarjanīyam te ca prayāṇa kāle api sva prāpya anuguṇam mām viduḥ te ca iti cakārāt pūrve jarā maraṇa mokṣāya yatamānāḥ ca prayāṇa kāle viduḥ iti samuccīyante anena jñāninaḥ api artha svābhāvyāt sa adhiyajñam mām viduḥ prayāṇa kāle api sva prāpya anuguṇam mām viduḥ iti uktam bhavati adhiyajñaḥ katham kaḥ atra dehe asmin madhusūdanam prayāṇa kāle ca katham jñeyaḥ asi niyata ātmabhiḥ jarā maraṇa mokṣāya bhagavantam āśritya yatamānānām jñātavyatayā uktam tad brahma adhyātmam ca kim iti vaktavyam aiśvarya arthīnām jñātavyam adhibhūtam adhidaivam ca kim trayāṇām jñātavyaḥ adhiyajña śabda nirdiṣṭa ḥ ca kaḥ tasya ca adhiyajña bhāvaḥ katham prayāṇa kāle ca ebhiḥ tribhiḥ niyata ātmabhiḥ katham jñeyaḥ asi tad brahma iti nirdiṣṭam paramam akṣaram na kṣarati iti akṣaram kṣetrajña samaṣṭi rūpam tathā ca śrutiḥ avyaktam akṣare līyate akṣaram tamasi līyate iti ādikā paramam akṣaram prakṛti vinirmuktam ātma svarūpam svabhāvaḥ adhyātmam ucyate svabhāvaḥ prakṛtiḥ anātma bhūtam ātmani saṃbadhyamānam bhūta sūkṣma tad vāsanā ādikam pañca agnividyāyām jñātavya tayā uditam tad ubhayam prāpyatayā tyājya tayā ca mumukṣubhiḥ jñātavyam bhūta bhāva udbhava karaḥ visargaḥ karma saṃjñitaḥ bhūta bhāvaḥ manuṣya ādi bhāvaḥ tad udbhava karaḥ yaḥ visargaḥ pañcamyām āhutau  āpaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ bhavanti iti śruti siddhaḥ yoṣit saṃbandha jaḥ sa karma saṃjñitaḥ tad ca akhilam sa anubandham udvejanīya tayā pariharaṇīya tayā ca mumukṣubhiḥ jñātavyam pariharaṇīya tayā ca anantaram eva vakṣyate yad icchantaḥ brahmacaryam caranti iti aiśvarya arthinām jñātavyatayā nirdiṣṭam adhibhūtam kṣaraḥ bhāvaḥ viyat ā ādi bhūteṣu vartamānaḥ tad pariṇāma viśeṣaḥ kṣaraṇa svabhāvaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ śabda sparśa ādi ḥ sa asrayaḥ vilakṣaṇāḥ sa āśrayāḥ śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāḥ aiśvarya arthibhiḥ prāpya aḥ taiḥ anusandheyāḥ puruṣaḥ ca adhidaivatam adhidaivata śabda nirdiṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ adhidaivatam devatā upari vartamānaḥ indra prajāpati prabhṛti kṛtsna daivata upari vartamānaḥ indra prajāpati prabhṛtīnām bhogya jāta d vilakṣaṇa śabda ādeḥ bhoktā puruṣaḥ sā ca bhoktṛtvā avasthā aiśvarya arthibhiḥ prāpyatayā anusandheyā adhiyajñaḥ aham eva adhiyajñaḥ yajñaiḥ ārādhya tayā vartamānaḥ atra indra ādau mama deha bhūte ātma tayā avasthitaḥ aham eva yajñaiḥ ārādhya iti mahāyajña ādi nitya naimittika anuṣṭhāna velāyām trayāṇām adhikāriṇām anusandheyam etad idam api trayāṇām sādhāraṇam antakāle ca mām eva smaran kalevaram tyaktvā yaḥ prayāti sa mad bhāvam yāti mama yaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ tam yāti tadānīm yathā mām anusandhatte tathāvidha ākāraḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ yathā ādi bharata ādayaḥ tadānīm smaryamāṇa mṛga sajātīya ākārāt saṃbhūtāḥ ante antakāle yam yam vā api bhāvam smaran kalebaram tyajati tam tam bhāvam eva maraṇa anantaram eti antima pratyayaḥ ca pūrva bhāvita viṣaya eva jāyate yasmāt pūrva kāla abhyasta viṣaya eva antya pratyayaḥ jāyate tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu āprayāṇāt ahar ahar mām anusmara aharahar anusmṛti karam yuddha ādikam varṇa āśrama anubandhi śruti smṛti coditam nitya naimittikam ca karma kuru evam upāyena mayi arpita manaḥ buddhiḥ anta kale ca mām eva smaran yathā abhilaṣita prakāram mām prāpsyasi na atra saṃśayaḥ aharahar abhyāsa yogābhyām yukta tayā na anya gāminā cetasā antakāle paramam puruṣam divyam mām vakṣyamāṇa prakāram cintayan mām eva yāti ādi bharata mṛga tva prāptivat  aiśvarya viśiṣṭa tayā mad samāna ākāraḥ bhavati abhyāsaḥ nitya naimittikā viruddheṣu sarveṣu kāleṣu manasā upāsya saṃśīlanam yoga ḥ tu aharahar yoga kāle anuṣṭhīyamānam yathā ukta lakṣaṇam upāsanam prayāṇa kāle manasā acalena bhaktyā yuktaḥ yoga balena ca eva bhruvoḥ madhye prāṇam āveśya samyak sa tam param puruṣam upaiti divyam kavim sarvajñan purāṇam purātanam anuśāsitāram viśvasya praśāsitāram aṇoḥ aṇīyāṃsam jīvāt api sūkṣmataram sarvasya dhātāram sarvasya sraṣṭāram acintya rūpam sakala itara visajātīya svarūpam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastād aprākṛta svāsa ādhāraṇa divya rūpam tam evaṃbhūtam aharahar abhyasyamāna bhakti yukta yoga balena ārūḍha saṃskāra tayā acalena manasā prayāṇa kāle bhruvoḥ madhye prāṇam āveśya saṃsthāpya tatra bhū madhye divyam puruṣam yaḥ anusmaret sa tam eva upaiti tad bhāvam yāti tad samānāi śvaryaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ yad akṣaram asthūla tva ādi guṇakam veda vidaḥ vadanti vīta rāgāḥ ca yatayaḥ yad akṣaram viśanti yad akṣaram prāptum icchantaḥ brahmacaryam caranti tad padam saṃgraheṇa te pravakṣye padyate gamyate cetasā iti padam tad nikhila vedānta vedyam mad svarūpam akṣaram yathā upāsyam tathā saṃkṣepeṇa pravakṣyāmi iti arthaḥ om iti eka akṣaram brahma vyāharan mām anusmaran yaḥ prayāti tyajan deham sa yāti paramām gatim sarvāṇi śrotra ādīni indriyāṇi jñāna dvāra bhūtāni saṃyamya sva vyāpārebhyaḥ vinivartya hṛdaya kamala niviṣṭe mayi akṣare manaḥ nirudhya yoga ākhyām dhāraṇām āsthitaḥ mayi eva niścalām sthitim āsthitaḥ om iti eka akṣaram brahma mad vācakam vyāharan vācyam mām anusmaran ātmanaḥ prāṇam mūrdhni ādhāya deham tyajan yaḥ prayāti sa yāti paramām gatim prakṛti viyuktam mad samāna ākāram apunarāvṛttim ātmānam prāpnoti iti arthaḥ yaḥ sa sarveṣu bhūteṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyati nityaśaḥ mām udyoga prabhṛti satatam sarvakālam ananya cetāḥ yaḥ smarati atyartha mad priya tvena mad smṛtyā vinā ātma dhāraṇam alabhamānaḥ niratiśaya priyām smṛtim yaḥ karoti tasya nitya yuktasya nitya yogam kāṅkṣamāṇasya yoginaḥ aham sulabhaḥ aham eva prāpyaḥ na mad bhāva aiśvarya ādikaḥ su prāpaḥ ca tad viyogam asahamānaḥ aham eva tam vṛṇe yam eva eṣa vṛṇute tena labhyaḥ iti hi śrūyate mad prāpti anuguṇa upāsana vipākam tad virodhi nirasanam atyartha mad priya tva ādikam ca aham eva dadāmi iti arthaḥ vakṣyate ca teṣām satata yuktānām bhajatām prīti pūrvakam dadāmi buddhi yogam tam yena mām upāyānti te mām prāpya punar nikhila duḥkha ālayam aśāśvatam asthiram janma na prāpnuvanti yata ete mahātmānaḥ mahāmanasaḥ yathā avasthita mad sva rūpa jñānānā atyartha mad priya tvena mayā vinā ātma dhāraṇam alabhamānā mayi āskta manasaḥ mad āśrayā mām upāsya parama saṃsiddhi rūpam mām prāptāḥ brahma loka paryantāḥ brahmāṇḍa udara vartinaḥ sarve lokā bhogāi śvarya ālayāḥ punarāvartinaḥ vināśinaḥ ata aiśvarya gatim prāptānām prāpya sthāna vināśāt vināśi tvam avarjanīyam mām sarvajñam satya saṅkalpam nikhila jagat utpatti sthiti laya līlam parama kāruṇikam sadā eka rūpam prāptānām vināśa prasaṅga abhāvāt teṣām punarjanma na vidyate avyaktāt vyaktayaḥ sarvāḥ prabhavanti ahar āgame rātri āgame pralīyante tatra eva avyakta saṃjñake bhūta grāmaḥ sa eva ayam bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyate rātri āgame avaśaḥ pārtha prabhavati ahar āgame ye manuṣya ādi caturmukha antānām mad saṅkalpa kṛta ahorātra vyavasthā vidaḥ janāḥ te brahmaṇaḥ caturmukhasya yad ahar tad caturyuga sahasra avasānam viduḥ rātriṃ ca tathārūpām tatra brahmaṇaḥ aharāgama samaye trailokya antar vartinyaḥ deha indriya bhogya bhoga sthāna rūpā vyakta ḥ caturmukha deha avasthād avyaktāt prabhavanti tatra eva avyakta avasthā viśeṣe caturmukha dehe rātri āgama samaye pralīyante sa eva ayam karma vaśyaḥ bhūta grāmaḥ aharāgame bhūtvā bhutvā rātri āgame pralīyate punar api ahar āgame prabhavati tathā varṣata avasāna rūpa yuga sahasra ante brahma loka paryantā lokāḥ brahmā ca pṛthivī apsu pralīyate āpaḥ tejasi līyante ityādi krameṇa avyakta akṣara tamaḥ paryantam mayi eva pralīyante evam mad vyatiriktasya kṛtsnasya kāla vyavasthayā matta utpatteḥ mayi pralayāt ca utpatti vināśa yogi tvam avarjanīyam iti aiśvarya gatim prāptānām punarāvṛttiḥ aparihāryā mām upetānām tu na punarāvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ avyaktaḥ akṣara iti ukta ḥ tam āhuḥ paramām gatim yam prāpya na nivartante tad dhāma paramam mama tasmāt avyaktāt acetana prakṛti rūpāt puruṣa artha tayā paraḥ utkṛṣṭaḥ bhāvaḥ anyaḥ jñāna eka ākāra tayā tasmāt visajātīyaḥ avyaktaḥ kenacid pramāṇena na vyajyata iti avyaktaḥ sva saṃvedya svāsādhāraṇa ākāra iti arthaḥ sanātanaḥ utpatti vināśān arha tayā nityaḥ yaḥ sarveṣu viyat ā ādi bhūteṣu sa kāraṇeṣu sa kāryeṣu vinaśyatsu tatra tatra sthitaḥ api na vinaśyati saḥ avyaktaḥ akṣara iti uktaḥ ye tu akṣaram anirdeśyam avyaktam paryupāsate  kūṭasthaḥ akṣara ucyate ityādiṣu tam veda vidaḥ paramām gatim āhuḥ ayam eva yaḥ prayāti tyajan deham sa yāti paramām gatim iti atra parama gati śabda nirdiṣṭaḥ akṣaraḥ prakṛti saṃsarga viyukta sva svarūpeṇa avasthita ātmā iti arthaḥ yam evaṃbhūtam sva rūpeṇa avasthitam prāpya na nivartante tad mama paramam dhāma param niyamana sthānam acetana prakṛtiḥ ekam niyamana sthānam tad saṃsṛṣṭa rūpā jīva prakṛtiḥ dvitīyam niyamana sthānam acit saṃsarga viyuktam sva rūeṇa avathitam mukta svarūpam paramam niyamana sthānam iti arthaḥ tad ca apunarāvṛtti rūpam atha vā prakāśa vācī dhāma śabdaḥ prakāśaḥ ca iha jñānam abhipretam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭāt parichinna jñāna rūpāt ātmanaḥ aparicchinna jñāna rūpa tayā mukta svarūpam param dhāma mattaḥ parataram na anyat kiñcid asti dhanaṃjaya mayi sarvam idam protam sūtre maṇi gaṇā iva agniḥ jyotiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsā uttarāyaṇam tatra prayātā gacchanti brahma brahma vidaḥ janāḥ atra kāla śabdaḥ mārgasya ahar prabhṛti saṃvatarānta kāla abhimāni devatā bhūyaḥ tayā mārga upalakṣaṇa arthaḥ yasmin mārge prayātā yoginaḥ anāvṛttim puṇya karmāṇaḥ ca āvṛttim yānti tam mārgam vakṣyāmi iti arthaḥ agniḥ jyotiḥ ahar śuklaḥ ṣaṣ māsā uttarāyaṇam iti saṃvatsara ādīnām pradarśanam etad ca dhūma ādi mārga stha pitṛ loka ādeḥ pradarśanam atra yogi śabdaḥ puṇya karma saṃbandhi viṣayaḥ śuklā gatiḥ arciḥ ādikā kṛṣṇā ca dhūma ādikā śukla yāna āvṛttim yāti kṛṣṇayā tu punar āvartate ete śukla kṛṣṇe gatī jñāninām vividhānām puṇya karmaṇām ca śrutau śāśvate mate tad ya ittham viduḥ ye ca ime araṇye śraddhā tapa iti upāsate te arciṣam abhisaṃbhavanti  atha ya ime grāma iṣṭāpūrte dattam iti upāsate te dhūmam abhisaṃbhavanti iti etau mārgau jānan yogī prayāṇa kāle kaścana na muhyati api tu svena eva deva yānena pathā yāti tasmāt aharahar cira ādi gati cintana ākhya yoga yuktaḥ bhava ṛc yaju ssāma atharva rūpa veda abhyāsa yajña tapaḥ dāna prabhṛtiṣu sarveṣu puṇyeṣu yad phalam nirdiṣṭam idam adhyāya dvaya uditam bhagavat māhātmyam viditvā tad sarvam atyeti etad vedana sukha atirekeṇa tad sarvam tṛṇavan manyate yogī jñānī ca bhūtvā jñāninaḥ prāpyam param ādyam sthānam upaiti idam tu guhyatamam bhakti rūpam upāsana ākhyam jñānam vijñāna sahitam upāsana gata viśeṣa jñāna sahitam anasūyave te pravakṣyāmi mad viṣayam sakala itara visajātīyam aparimita prakāram māhātmyam śrutvā evam eva saṃbhavati iti manu ānāya te pravakṣyāmi iti arthaḥ yaj jñānam anuṣṭhāna paryantam jñātvā mad prāpti virodhinaḥ sarvasmāt aśubhān mokṣyase rāja vidyā vidyānām rājā rāja guhyam guhyānām rājā rājñām vidyā iti vā rāja vidyā rājānaḥ hi vistīrṇa agādhya manasaḥ mahāmanasām iyam vidyā iti arthaḥ mahāmanasa eva hi gopanīya gopana kuśalā iti teṣām eva guhyam idam uttamam pavitram mad prāpti virodhi aśeṣa kalmaṣa apaham pratyakṣa avagamam avagamyata iti avagamaḥ viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa bhūtaḥ avagamaḥ viṣayaḥ yasya jñānasya tad pratyakṣa avagamam bhakti rūpeṇa upāsanena upāsyamānaḥ aham tādānīm eva upāsituḥ pratyakṣatām upagataḥ bhavāmi iti arthaḥ atha api dharmyam dharmāt anapetam dharma tvam hi niśśreyasa sādhana tvam sva rūpeṇa eva atyartha priya tvena tadānīm eva mad darśana āpādana tayā ca svayam niśśreyasa rūpam api niratiśaya niśśreyasa rūpa ātyantika mad prāpti sādhanam iti arthaḥ ata eva su sukham kartum su sukha upādānam atyartha priya tvena upādeyam avyayam akṣayam mad prāptim sādhayitvā api svayam na kṣīyate evaṃrūpam upāsanam kurvataḥ mad pradāne kṛte api kiṃcid kṛtam mayā asya iti me pratibhāti iti arthaḥ asya upāsana ākhyasya dharmasya niratiśaya priyamadviṣaya tayā svayam niratiśaya priya rūpasya parama niśśreyasa rūpa mad prāpti sādhanasya avyayasya upādāna yogya daśāyām prāpya aśraddadhānāḥ viśvāsa pūrvaka tvarā rahitāḥ puruṣāḥ mām aprāpya mṛtyu rūpe saṃsāra vartmani nitarām vartante ahaḥ mahat idam āścaryam iti arthaḥ na ca mad sthāni bhūtāni paśya me yogam aiśvaram bhūta bhṛt na ca bhūta sthaḥ mama ātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥ idam cetana acetana ātmakam kṛtsnam jagad avyakta mūrtinā aprakāśita svarūpeṇa mayā antaryāmiṇā tatam asya jagataḥ dhāraṇa artham niyamana artham ca śeṣi tvena vyāptam iti arthaḥ yathā antaryāmi brāhmaṇe yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan yam pṛthivī na veda  ya ātmani tiṣṭhan yam ātmā na veda iti cetana acetana vastu jātaiḥ adṛṣṭeṇa antaryāmiṇā tatra tatra vyāptiḥ uktā tataḥ mad sthāni sarva bhūtāni sarvāṇi bhūtāni mayi antaryāmiṇi sthitāni tatra eva brāhmaṇe yasya pṛthivī śarīram yaḥ pṛthivīm antaraḥ yamayati yasya ātmā śarīram ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati iti śarīra tvena niyāmya tva pratipādanāt tadāyatte sthiti niyamane pratipādite śeṣi tvam ca na ca aham teṣu avasthitaḥ aham tu na tad āyatta sthitiḥ mad sthitau taiḥ na kaścid upakāra iti athaḥ na ca mad sthāni bhūtāni na ghaṭa ādīnām jala ādeḥ iva mama dhāraka tvam katham mad saṅkalpena paśya mama aiśvaram yogam anyatra kutracid asaṃbhāvanīyam mada sādhāraṇam āścaryam yogam paśya kaḥ asau yoga bhūta bhṛt na ca bhūta sthaḥ mama ātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām bhartā aham na ca taiḥ kaścid api mama upakāraḥ mama ātmā eva bhūtabhāvanaḥ mama manaḥ mayaḥ saṅkalpa eva bhūtānām bhāvayitā dhārayitā niyantā ca yathā ākaśe anālambane mahān vayuḥ sthitaḥ sarvatra gacchati sa tu vāyuḥ nirālambanaḥ mad āyatta sthitiḥ iti avaśya abhyupagamanīyaḥ evam eva sarvāṇi bhūtāni taiḥ adṛṣṭe mayi sthitāni mayā eva dhṛtāni iti upadhāraya yathā āhuḥ veda vidaḥ megha udayaḥ sāgara sannivṛttiḥ indoḥ vibhāgaḥ sphuritāni vāyoḥ vidyut vibhaṅgaḥ gatiḥ uṣṇa raśmeḥ viṣṇoḥ vicitrāḥ prabhavanti māyāḥ iti viṣṇoḥ ananya sādhāraṇāni mahā āścaryāṇi iti arthaḥ śrutiḥ api etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ  bhīṣā asmāt vātaḥ pavate bhīṣodeti sūryaḥ bhīṣā asmāt agniḥ ca indraḥ ca iti ādikā sthāvara jaṅgama ātmakāni sarvāṇi bhūtāni māmikām mad śarīra bhūtām prakṛtim tamaḥ śabda vācyām nāma rūpa vibhāgān arhām kalpa kṣaye catur mukha avasāna samaye mad saṅkalpāt yānti tāni eva bhūtāni kalpa ādau punar visṛjyāmi aham yathā āha manuḥāsīt idam tamaḥ bhūtam saḥ abhidhyāya śarīrāt svāt iti śrutiḥ api yasya avyaktam śarīram  avyaktam akṣare līyate akṣaram tamasi līyate iti ādikā tam āsīt tamasā gūḍham agre praketam iti ca svakīyām vicitra pariṇāminīm prakṛtim avaṣṭabhya aṣṭadhā pariṇāmyy imam caturvidham deva tiryak manuṣya sthāvara ātmakam bhūta grāmam madīyāyā mohinyā guṇa mayyāḥ prakṛteḥ vaśād avaśam punar punar kāle kāle visṛjāmi na ca tāni viṣama sṛṣṭi ādīni karmāṇi mām nibadhnanti mayi nairghṛṇya ādikam na apādayanti yataḥ kṣetrajñānām pūrva kṛtāni eva karmāṇi deva ādi viṣama bhāva hetavaḥ aham tu tatra vaiṣamye asaktaḥ tatra udāsīnavat  āsīnaḥ yathā āha sūtra kāraḥ vaiṣamyanaiḥ ghṛṇye na sa apekṣa tvāt na karma avibhāgāt iti ced nānā ādi tvāt iti tasmāt kṣetrajña karma anuguṇam madīyā prakṛtiḥ satya saṅkalpena mayā adhyakṣeṇa īkṣitā sacarācaram jagat sūyate anena kṣetrajña karma anuguṇam adīkṣaṇena hetunā jagat parivartata iti mad svāmyam satya saṅkalpa tvam nairghṛṇya ādi doṣa rahita tvam iti evam ādikam mama vasudeva sūnoḥ aiśvaram yogam paśya yathā āha śrutiḥ asmān māyī sṛjate viśvam etad tasmin  ca anyaḥ māyayā sanniruddhaḥ māyām tu prakṛtim vidyān māyinam tu mha īśvaram evam mām bhūta maheśvaram sarvajñam satya saṅkalpam nikhila jagat eka kāraṇam parama kāruṇika tayā sarva samāśrayaṇīya tvāya mānuṣīm tanum āśritam sva kṛtaiḥ pāpa karmabhiḥ mūḍhā avajānanti prākṛta manuṣya samam manyante bhūta maheśvarasya mama āpāraka aruṇya udārya sauśīlya vātsalya nibandhanam manuṣya tva samāśrayaṇa lakṣaṇam imam param bhāvam ajānantaḥ manuṣya tva samāśrayaṇa mātreṇa mām itarasa jātīyam matvā tiraskurvanti iti arthaḥ mama manuṣya tve parama kāruṇī ādi paratvati rodhāna karīm rākṣasīm āsurīm ca mohinīm prakṛtim āśritāḥ mogha āśāḥ moghvān chitāḥ niṣphalavān chitāḥ moghkarmāṇaḥ mogha ārambhāḥ mogha jñānāḥ sarveṣu madīyeṣu carācareṣu artheṣu viparīta jñāna tayā niṣphala jñānāḥ vicetasaḥ tathā sarvatra vigata yāthātmya jñānāḥ mām sarveśvaram itara samam matvā mayi ca yad kartum icchanti yad uddiśya ārambhān kurvate tad sarvam mogham bhavati iti arthaḥ ye tu sva kṛtaiḥ puṇya sañcayaiḥ mām śaraṇam upagamya vidhvasta samasta pāpa bandhā daivīm prakṛtim āśritā mahātmānaḥ te bhūtādim avyayam vāc manasā agocara nāma karma svarūpam parama kāruṇika tayā sādhu paritrāṇāya manuṣya tvena avatīrṇam mām jñātvā ananya manasaḥ mām bhajante mad priya tva atirekeṇa mad bhajanena vinā manasaḥ ca ātmanaḥ ca bāhya karaṇānām ca dhāraṇam alabhamānā mad bhajana eka prayojanā bhajante atyartha mad priya tvena mad kīrtanayatana namaskāraiḥ vinā kṣaṇāṇu mātre api ātma dhāraṇam alabhamānāḥ mad guṇa viśeṣa vācīni mad nāmāni smṛtvā pulaka āñcita sarva aṅgāḥ harṣa gadgada kaṇṭhāḥ nārāyaṇa kṛṣṇa vāset eva iti evam ādīni satatam kīrtayantaḥ tathā eva yatantaḥ mad karmasu arcana ādikeṣu tad upakāreṣu bhavana nandana vana karaṇa ādikeṣu ca dṛḍha saṅkalpā yatamānāḥ bhakti bhārau anamita manaḥ buddhi abhimāna pada dvaya kara dvaya śirobhiḥ aṣṭāṅgaiḥ acintita pāṃsu kardama śarkarā ādike dharā tale daṇḍavat  praṇipatantaḥ satatam mām nitya yuktāḥ nitya yogam kāṅkṣamāṇā ātma antam mad dāsya vyavasāyinaḥ upāsate anye api mahātmanaḥ pūrva uktaiḥ kīrtana ādibhiḥ jñāna ākhyena yajñena ca yajantaḥ mām upāsate katham bahudhā pṛthaktvena jagat ākāreṇa viśvatomukham viśva prakāram avasthitam mām eka tvena upāsate etad uktam bhavati bhagavān vāsudeva eva nāma rūpa vibhāgān arha ati sūkṣma cit acit vastu śarīra ḥ san satya saṅkalpaḥ vividha vibhakta nāma rūpa sthūla cit acit vastu śarīraḥ syām iti saṃkalpya sa eka eva deva tiryak manuṣya sthāvara ākhya vicitra jagat śarīraḥ avatiṣṭhata iti anusaṃdadhānāḥ ca mām upāsate iti aham kratuḥ aham jyotiṣṭoma ādikaḥ kratuḥ aham eva mahāyajñaḥ aham eva pitṛ gaṇa puṣṭi dā svadhā auṣadham haviḥ ca aham eva aham eva ca mantraḥ aham eva ca ājyam pradarśana artham idam soma ādikam ca havir aham eva iti arthaḥ aham āhavanīya ādikaḥ agniḥ homaḥ ca aham eva asya sthāvara jaṅgama ātmakasya jagataḥ tatra tatra pitṛ tvena mātṛ tvena dhātṛ tvena pitāmaha tvena ca vartamānaḥ aham eva atra dhātṛ śabdaḥ mātā pitṛ vyatirikte utpatti prayojake cetana viśeṣe vartate yad kiñcid veda vedyam pavitram pāvanam tad aham eva vedakaḥ ca veda bīja bhūtaḥ praṇavaḥ aham eva ṛc sāma yajuḥ ātmakaḥ vedaḥ ca aham eva gamyata iti gatiḥ tatra tatra prāpya sthānam iti arthaḥ bhartā dhārayitā prabhuḥ śāsitā sākṣī sākṣāt dṛṣṭā nivāsaḥ vāsasthānam veśma ādi śaraṇam iṣṭasya prāpaka tayā aniṣṭasya nivāraṇa tayā ca samāśrayaṇīyaḥ cetanaḥ śaraṇam sa ca aham eva su kṛt dhita eṣī prabhava pralaya sthānam yasya kasyacid yatra kutracid utpatti pralayayoḥ yad sthānam tad aham eva nidhānam nidhīyata iti nidhānam utpādyam upasaṃhāryam ca aham eva iti arthaḥ avyayam bījam tatra tatra vyaya rahitam yad kāraṇam tad aham eva agni āt ityādi rūpeṇa aham eva tapāmi grīṣma ādau  aham eva varṣam nigṛhṇāmi tathā varṣāsu ca aham eva utsṛjāmi amṛtam ca eva mṛtyuḥ ca yena jīvati lokaḥ yena ca mriyate tad ubhayam aham eva kim atra bahunā uktena sat asat ca aham eva sat yad vartate asad yad atītam anāgatam ca sarva avasthā avasthita cit acit vastu śarīra tayā tad tad prakāraḥ aham eva avasthita iti arthaḥ evam bahudhā pṛthaktvena vibhakta nāma rūpa avasthita kṛtsna jagat śarīra tayā tad prakāraḥ aham eva avasthita iti eka tva jñānena ananu saṃdadhānāḥ ca mām upāsate te tam bhuktvā svarga lokam viśālam kṣīṇe puṇye martya lokam viśanti evam trayī dharmam anuprapannāḥ gatāgatam kāma kāmā labhante ṛc yajussāma rūpāḥ tisraḥ vidyāḥ tri vidyam kevalam tri vidya niṣṭhāḥ traividyāḥ na tu trayī anta niṣṭhāḥ trayī anta niṣṭhā hi mahātmanaḥ pūrva ukta prakāreṇa nikhila veda vedyam mām eva jñātvā atimātramad bhakti kārita kīrtana ādibhiḥ jñāna yajñena ca mad eka prāpyā mām eva upāsate traividyāḥ tu veda pratipādya kevala indra ādi yāga śiṣṭa somān pibantaḥ pūta pāpāḥ svarga ādi prāpti virodhi pāpāt pūtāḥ taiḥ kevala indra ādi devatyatayā anusaṃhitaiḥ yajñaiḥ vastu taḥ tad rūpam mām iṣṭvā tathā avasthitam mām ajānantaḥ svarga gatim prārthayante te puṇyam duḥkha asaṃbhinnam sura indra lokam prāpya tatra tatra divyān deva bhogān aśnanti te tam viśālam svarga lokam bhuktvā tad anubhava hetu bhūte puṇye kṣīṇe punar api martya lokam viśanti evam trayī anta siddha jñāna vidhurāḥ kāmya svarga ādi kāmāḥ kevalam trayī dharmam anuprapannāḥ gatāgatam labhante alpa asthira svarga ādīn anubhūya punar punar nivartanta iti arthaḥ ananyāḥ ananya prayojanāḥ mad cintanena vinā ātma dhāraṇa alābhān mad cintana eka prayojanāḥ mām cintayantaḥ ye mahātmānaḥ janāḥ paryupāsate sarva kalyānṇa guṇa anvitam sarva vibhūti yuktam mām parita upāsate anyūnam upāsate teṣām nitya abhiyuktānām mayi nitya abhiyogam kāṅkṣamāṇānām aham mad prāpti lakṣaṇam yogam apunarāvṛtti rūpam kṣemam ca vahāmi ye tu indra ādi devatā bhaktāḥ kevala trayī niṣṭhāḥ śraddhayā anvitāḥ indra ādīn yajante te api pūrva uktena nyāyena sarvasya mad śarīra tayā mad ātmaka tvena indra ādi śabdānām ca mad vāci tvāt vastu taḥ mām eva yajante api tu avidhi pūrvakam yajante indra ādīnām devatānām karamsvārādhya tayā anvayam yathā vedānta vākyāni catur hotāraḥ yatra saṃpadam gacchanti deaiḥ ityādīni vidadhati na tad pūrvakam yajante vedānta vākya jātam hi parama puruṣa śarīra tayā avasthitānām indra ādīnām ārādhya tvam vidadhat atma bhūtasya parama puruṣasya eva sākṣāt ārādhya tvam vidadhāti catur hotāraḥ agnihotra darśa pūrṇamāsa ādīni karmāṇi yatra paramātmani ātma tayā avasthite sati eva tad śarīra bhūta indra ādi devaiḥ saṃpadam gacchanti indra ādi devānām ārādhanāni etāni karmāṇī ti imām saṃpadam gacchanti iti arthaḥ prabhuḥ eva ca tatra tatra phala pradātā ca aham eva iti arthaḥ vrata śabdaḥ saṅklpa vācī devavratāḥ darśa pūrṇamāsa ādibhiḥ karmabhiḥ indra ādīn yajāmahe iti indra ādi yajana saṅkalpā ye te indra ādīn devān yānti ye ca pitṛ yajña ādibhiḥ pitñn yajāmahe iti pitṛ yajana saṅkalpāḥ te pitñn yānti ye ca yakṣara kaṣaḥ piśāca ādīni bhūtāni yajāmahe iti bhūta yajana saṅkalpāḥ te bhūtāni yānti ye te taiḥ eva yajñaiḥ deva pitṛ bhūta śarīrakam paramātmānam bhagavantam vāsudevam yajāmahe iti mām yajante te madya ajinaḥ mām eva yānti deva ādi vratāḥ deva ādīn prāpya taiḥ saha parimitam bhogam bhuktvā teṣām vinaśa kāle taiḥ saha vinaṣṭā bhavanti mad ya ajina ḥ tu mām anādi nidhanam sarvajñam satya saṅkalpam anavadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa mahā udadhim anavadhika atiśaya ānandam prāpya na punar nivartanta iti arthaḥ sarva sulabham patram vā puṣpam vā phalam vā toyam vā yaḥ bhaktyā me prayacchati atyartha mad priya tvena tad pradānena vinā ātma dhāraṇam alabhamāna tayā tad eka prayojanaḥ yaḥ me patra ādikam dadāti tasya prayata ātmanaḥ tad pradāna eka prayojana tva rūpa śuddhi yukta manasaḥ tad tathāvidha bhakti upahṛtam aham sarva īśvaraḥ nikhila jagat udaya vibhava laya līlā avāpta samasta kāmaḥ satya saṅkalpaḥ anavadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇaḥ svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya ānanda sva anubhave vartamānaḥ api manoratha patha dūra varti priyam prāpya eva aśnāmi yathā uktam mokṣa dharme yāḥ kriyāḥ saṃprayuktā aḥ syuḥ ekānta gata buddhibhiḥ tāḥ sarvāḥ śirasā devaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vai svayam iti yad deha yātrā aśeṣa bhūtam laukikam karma karoṣi yad ca deha dhāraṇāya aśnāsi yad ca vaidikam homa dāna tapaḥ prabhṛti nitya naimittikam karma karoṣi tad sarvam mad arpaṇam kuruṣva arpyata iti arpaṇam sarvasya laukikasya vaidikasya ca karmaṇaḥ kartṛ tvam bhoktṛ tvam ārādhya tvam ca yathā mayi samarpitam bhavati tathā kuru etad uktam bhavati yāga dāna ādiṣu ārādhya tayā pratīyamānānām deva ādīnām karma kartuḥ bhoktuḥ tava ca madīyatayā mad saṅkalpa āyatta svarūpa sthiti pravṛtti tayā ca mayi eva parama śeṣiṇi parama kartari tvām ca kartāram bhoktāram ārādhakam ārādhyam ca devatā jātam ārādhanam ca kriyā jātam sarvam samarpaya tava mad niyāmyatā pūrva kama cheṣa tā eka rasa tām ārādhya ādeḥ ca etad svabhāva garbhatām atyartha prīti yuktaḥ anusaṃdhatsva iti evam saṃnyāsa ākhya yoga yukta manāḥ ātmānam mad śeṣa tāmat niyāmyata eka rasam karma ca sarvam mad ārādhanam anusaṃdadhānaḥ laukikam vaidikam ca karma kurvan śubha aśubha phalaiḥ anantaiḥ prācīna karma ākhyaiḥ bandhanaiḥ mad prāpti virodhibhiḥ sarvaiḥ mokṣyase taiḥ vimuktaḥ mām eva upaiṣyasi deva tiryak manuṣya sthāvara ātmanā avasthiteṣu jātitaḥ ca ākārataḥ svabhāvataḥ jñānataḥ ca atyanta utkṛṣṭa apakṛṣṭa rūpeṇa vartamāneṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu samāśrayaṇīya tve samaḥ aham ayam jāti ākāra svabhāva jñāna ādibhiḥ nirkṛṣṭa iti samāśrayaṇe na me dveṣyaḥ asti udvejanīya tayā na tyājyaḥ asti tathā samāśrita tva atirekeṇa jāti ādibhiḥ atyanta utkṛṣṭaḥ ayam iti tad vyukta tayā samāśrayaṇe na kaścid priyaḥ asti na saṃgrāhyaḥ asti api tu atyartha mad priya tvena mad bhajanena vinā ātma dhāraṇa alābhān mad bhajana eka prayojanā ye mām bhajante te jāti ādibhiḥ utkṛṣṭā apakṛṣṭā vā mad samāna guṇavat yathāsukham mayi eva vartante aham api teṣu mad utkṛṣṭeṣu iva varte tatra tatra jāti viśeṣe jātānām yaḥ samācāra upādeyaḥ pariharaṇīyaḥ ca tasmāt ativṛttaḥ api ukta prakāreṇa mām ananya bhāj bhajana eka prayojanaḥ bhajate ced sādhuḥ eva saḥ vaiṣṇava agresara eva saḥ mantavyaḥ bahu mantavyaḥ pūrva uktaiḥ sama iti arthaḥ kuta etad samyak vyavasitaḥ hi saḥ yataḥ asya vyavasāyaḥ su samīcīnaḥ bhagavān nikhila jagat eka kāraṇa bhūtaḥ param brahma nārāyaṇaḥ carācara patiḥ asmad svāmī mama guruḥ mama suhṛd mama paramam bhogyam iti sarvaiḥ duṣprāpaḥ ayam vyavasāya ḥ tena kṛtaḥ tad kāryam ca ananya prayojanam nirantaram bhajanam tasya asti ataḥ sādhuḥ eva bahu mantavyaḥ asmin vyavasāye tad kārye ca ukta prakāra bhajane saṃpanne sati tasya ācāra vyatikramaḥ su alpa vaikalyam iti na tāvatā anādaraṇīyaḥ api tu bahu mantavya eva iti arthaḥ mad priya tva kāritān anya prayojana madbhajanena vidhūta pāpa tayā eva sa mūla unmūlita rajaḥ tamaḥ guṇaḥ kṣipram dharma ātmā bhavati kṣipram eva virodhiḥ ahita saparikara mat bhajana ekamanā bhavati evaṃrūpa bhajanam eva hi dharmasya asya parantapa iti upakrame dharma śabda uditam śaśvat śāntim nigacchati śaśvatīm apunarāvartinīm mad prāpti virodhi ācāra nivṛttim gacchati kaunteya tvam eva asmin  arthe pratijñām kuru mad bhaktau  upakrāntaḥ virodhi ācāra miśraḥ api na naśyati api tu mad bhakti māhātmyena sarvam virodhi jātam nāśayitvā śāśvatīm virodhi nivṛttim adhigamya kṣipram paripūrṇa bhaktiḥ bhavati iti kim punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayaḥ tathā anityam asukham lokam imam prāpya bhajasva mām striyaḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca pāpa yona yaḥ api mām vyapāśritya parām gatim yānti kim punar puṇya yona yaḥ brāhmaṇā rājarṣayaḥ ca mad bhaktim āsthitāḥ ataḥ tvam rājarṣiḥ asthiram tāpa traya abhihata tayā asukham ca imam lokam prāpya vartamānaḥ mām bhajasva mad manā bhava mayi sarva īśvara īśvare nikhila heya pratyanīka kalyāṇa ekatāne sarvajñe satya saṅkalpe nikhila jagat eka kāraṇe parasmin brahmaṇi puruṣottame puṇḍarī ka dalā amala āyata akṣe svaccha nīla jīmūta saṅkāśe yugapad udita dinakara sahasra sadṛśa tejasi lāvaṇya amṛta mahā udadhau udāra pīvara catur bāhau ati ujjvala pīta ambare amala kirīṭa makara kuṇḍala hāra keyūra kaṭaka bhūṣite apāraka aruṇya sauśīlya saundarya mādhurya gāmbhīryā u dārya vātsalya jaladhau anālocita viśeṣa aśeṣa loka śaraṇye sarva svāmini taila dhārāvat avicchedena niviṣṭa manā bhava tad eva viśinaṣṭi mad bhaktaḥ atyartha mad priya tvena yuktaḥ mad manā bhava iti arthaḥ punar pi viśinaṣṭi mad yājī anavadhika atiśaya priyamadanubhava kārita madya jana paraḥ bhava yajanam nāma paripūrṇa śeṣa vṛttiḥ aupacārika sāṃsparśika abhyavahārikā ādi sakala bhoga pradāna rūpaḥ hi yāgaḥ yathā mad anubhava janita nirvadhikā atiśaya prīti kārita madya jana paraḥ bhavasi tathā mad manā bhava iti uktam bhavati punar api tad eva viśinaṣṭi mām namaskuru anavadhika atiśaya priyamadanubhava kāritā atyartha priya aśeṣa śeṣa vṛttau aparyavasyan mayi antarātmani atimātra prahvībhāva vyavasāyam kuru mad parāyaṇaḥ aham eva param ayanam yasya asau mad parāyaṇaḥ mayā vinā ātma dhāraṇa asaṃbhāvanayā mad āśraya iti arthaḥ evam ātmānam yuktvā mad parāyaṇaḥ evam anavadhika atiśaya prītyā mad anubhava samartham manaḥ prāpya mām eva eṣyasi ātma śabdaḥ hi atra manaḥ viṣayaḥ evaṃrūpeṇa manasā mām dhyātvā mām anubhūya mām iṣṭvā mām namaskṛtya mad parāyaṇaḥ mām eva prāpsyasi iti arthaḥ tad evam laukikāni śarīra dhāraṇa arthāni vaidikāni ca nitya naimittikāni karmāṇi mad prītaye mad śeṣa tā eka rasaḥ mayā eva kārita iti kurvan satatam mad kīrtanayatana namaskāra ādikān prītyā kurvāṇaḥ mad niyāmyam nikhila jagan mad śeṣa tā eka rasam iti ca anusandhānaḥ atyartha priya madguṇa gaṇam ca anusandhāya āharahar ukta lakṣaṇam idam upāsanam upādadānaḥ mām eva prāpsyasi mama māhātmyam śrutvā prīyamāṇāya te mad bhakti utpatti vivṛddhi rūpa hita kāmanayā bhūyaḥ mad māhātmya prapañca viṣayam eva paramam vacaḥ yad vakṣyāmi tad avahita manāḥ śṛṇu sura gaṇā mahā ṛṣayaḥ ca atīndriya artha darśinaḥ adhikatara jñānā api me prabhavam prabhāvam na viduḥ mama nāmakarma svarūpa svabhāva ādikam na jānanti yataḥ teṣām devānām mahā ṛṣīṇām ca sarvaśaḥ aham ādiḥ teṣām svarūpasya jñāna śakti ādeḥ ca aham ādiḥ teṣām deva tvam ahā ṛṣi tva ādi hetu bhūta puṇya anuguṇam mayā dattam jñānam parimitam ataḥ te parimita jñānā mad svarūpa ādikam yathāvan na jānanti na jāyata iti ajaḥ anena vikāridravyād acetanāt tad saṃsṛṣṭāt saṃsāri cetanā c ca visajātīya tvam uktam saṃsāri cetanasya hi karma kṛta ācid saṃsargaḥ janma anādim iti anena padena ādimataḥ ajān mukta ātmanaḥ visajātīya tvam uktam mukta ātmanaḥ hi aja tvam ādimat tasya heya saṃbandhasya pūrva vṛtta tvāt tad arhatā asti ataḥ anādim iti anena tad anarhatayā tad pratyanīka tā ucyate niravadyam ityādi śrutyā ca evam heya saṃbandha pratyanīka svarūpa tayā tad anarham mām loka maheśvaram loka īśvarāṇām api īśvaram martyeṣu asaṃmūḍhaḥ yaḥ vetti itarasa jātīyatayā ekīkṛtya mohaḥ saṃmohaḥ tad rahitaḥ asaṃmūḍhaḥ sa mad bhakti utpatti virodhibhiḥ sarvaiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate etad uktam bhavati loke manuṣyāṇām rājā itara manuṣya sajātīyaḥ kenacid karmaṇā tad ādhipatyam prāptaḥ tathā devānām adhipatiḥ api tathā aṇḍa adhipatiḥ api itara saṃsāri sajātīyaḥ tasya api bhāvanā traya antargata tvāt yaḥ brahmāṇam vidadhāti iti śruteḥ ca tathā anye api ye kecana aṇima ādi aiśvaryam prāptāḥ ayam tu loka maheśvaraḥ kārya kāraṇa avasthād acetanāt baddhān muktā c ca cetanāt iśitavyāt sarvasmān nikhila heya pratyanīkāna vadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa eka tāna tayā niyamana eka svabhāva tayā ca visajātīya iti ītrasa jātīyatā moha rahitaḥ yaḥ mām vetti sa sarvaiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate iti ahiṃsā sama tā tuṣṭhi ḥ tapaḥ dānam yaśaḥ ayaśaḥ bhavanti bhāvā bhūtānām matta eva pṛthagvidhāḥ buddhiḥ manasaḥ nirūpaṇa sāmarthyam jñānam cit acit vastu viśeṣa viṣayaḥ niścayaḥ asaṃmohaḥ pūrva gṛhītād rajata ādeḥ visajātīye śuktikā ādi vastuni sajātīyatā buddhi nivṛttiḥ kṣamā manaḥ vikāra hetau sati api avikṛta manaḥ tvam satyam yathā dṛṣṭa viṣayam bhūta hita rūpam vacanam tad anuguṇā manaḥ vṛttiḥ iha abhipretā manaḥ vṛtti prakaraṇāt damaḥ bāhya karaṇānām anartha viṣayebhyaḥ niyamanam śamaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya tathā niyamanam sukham ātma anukūla anubhavaḥ duḥkham pratikūla anubhavaḥ bhavaḥ bhavanam anukūla anubhava hetukam manasaḥ bhavanam abhāvaḥ pratikūla anubhava hetu kaḥ manasaḥ avasādaḥ bhayam āgāminaḥ duḥkhasya hetu darśana jam duḥkham tad nivṛttiḥ abhayam ahiṃsā para duḥkha ahetu tvam sama tā ātmani sukṛtsu vipakṣeṣu ca artha anarthayoḥ samam ati tvam tuṣṭiḥ sarveṣu ātmasu dṛṣṭeṣu toṣa svabhāva tvam tapaḥ śāstrīyaḥ bhoga saṅkoca rūpaḥ kāya kleśaḥ dānam svakīya bhogyānam parasmai pratipādanam yaśaḥ guṇavattā prathā ayaśaḥ nairguṇya prathā etad ca ubhayam tad anuguṇa manaḥ vṛtti dvayam mantavyam tad prakaraṇāt tapaḥ dāne ca tathā evam ādyāḥ sarveṣām bhūtānām bhāvāḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti hetavaḥ manaḥ vṛttayaḥ matta eva mad saṅkalpa āyattā bhavanti pūrve sapta mahā ṛṣayaḥ atīta manvantare ye bhṛgu ādayaḥ sapta mahā ṛṣa yaḥ nitya sṛṣṭi pravartanāya brahmaṇaḥ mana ssaṃbhavāḥ nitya sthiti pravartanāya ye ca sārvaṇikā nāma catvāraḥ manavaḥ sthitāḥ yeṣām santāna maye loke jātā imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ pratikṣaṇam āpralayāt apatyānām utpādakāḥ pālakāḥ ca bhavanti te bhṛgu ādayaḥ manavaḥ ca mad bhāvāḥ mama yaḥ bhāvaḥ sa eva yeṣām bhāvaḥ te mad bhāvāḥ mad mate sthitāḥ mad saṅkalpā nuvartina iti arthaḥ vibhūtiḥ aiśvaryam etām sarvasya mad āyatta utpatti sthiti pravṛttitā rūpām vibhūtim mama heya pratyanīka kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa rūpam yogam ca yaḥ tattvataḥ vetti saḥ avikampena aprakampyena bhakti yogena yujyate na atra saṃśayaḥ mad vibhūti viṣayam kalyāṇa guṇa viṣayam ca jñānam bhakti yoga vardhanam iti svayam eva drakṣyasi iti abhiprāyaḥ aham sarvasya vicitra cit acit prapañcasya prabhavaḥ utpatti kāraṇam sarvam matta eva pravartate iti idam mama svābhāvikam niraṃkuśāi śvaryam sauśīlya saundarya vātsalyādi kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa yogam ca matvā budhā jñāninaḥ bhāva samanvitāḥ mām sarva kalyāṇa guṇa anvitam bhajante bhāvaḥ manaḥ vṛtti viśeṣaḥ mayi spṛhayā alavaḥ mām bhajanta iti arthaḥ mad cittāḥ mayi niviṣṭa manasaḥ mad gata prāṇāḥ mad gata jīvitāḥ mayā vinā ātma dhāraṇam alabhamānā iti arthaḥ svaiḥ svaiḥ anubhūtān madīyān guṇān parasparam bodhayantaḥ madīyāni divyāni ramaṇīyāni karmāṇi ca kathayantaḥ tuṣyanti ca ramanti ca vaktāraḥ tad vacanena ananya prayojanena tuṣyanti śrotāraḥ ca tad śravaṇena anavadhika atiśaya priyeṇa ramante teṣām satata yuktānām mayi satata yogam āśaṃsamānānām mām bhajamānānām aham tam eva buddhi yogam vipāka daśa āpannam prīti pūrvakam dadāmi yena te mām upayānti teṣām eva anugraha artham aham ātma bhāva sthaḥ teṣām manaḥ vṛttau viṣaya tayā avasthitaḥ madīyān kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇān  ca āviṣkurvan mad viṣaya jñāna ākhyena bhāsvatā dīpena jñāna virodhi prācīna karma rūpa ajñāna jam mad vyatirikta pūrva abhyasta viṣaya prāvaṇya rūpam tamaḥ nāśayāmi ab puruṣam śāśvatam divyam ādidevam ajam vibhum ṛṣayaḥ ca sarve parāvara tattva yāthātmya vidaḥ tvām eva śāśvatam divyam puruṣam ādidevam ajam vibhum āhuḥ tathā eva devarṣiḥ nāradaḥ asitaḥ devalaḥ vyāsaḥ ca ye ca deva vidaḥ vipraḥ ye ca adhyātma vidaḥ janāḥ te vadanti mahātmānam kṛṣṇam dharmam sanātanam ataḥ sarvam etad yathā avasthita vastu kathanam manye na praśaṃsā ādi abhiprāyam yad mām prati ananya sādhāraṇam anavadhika atiśayam svābhāvikam tava aiśvaryam kalyāṇa guṇa ānantyam ca vadasi ataḥ bhagavan niratiśaya jñāna śakti balāi śvarya vīrya tejasām nidhe te vyaktim vyañjana prakāram na hi parimita jñānā devāḥ dānavāḥ ca viduḥ he puruṣottama ātmanā ātmānam tvām svayam eva svena jñānena eva vettha bhūta bhāvana sarveṣām bhūtānām utpādayitaḥ bhūteśa sarveṣām niyantaḥ devadeva daivatānām api parama daivata yathā manuṣya mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpa ādīn saundarya sauśīlya ādi kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇaiḥ daivatāni atītya vartante tathā tāni sarvāṇi daivatāni api taiḥ taiḥ guṇaiḥ atītya vartamāna jagatpate jagatsvāmin divyāḥ tvad asādha araṇyaḥ vibhūtayaḥ yāḥ tāḥ tvam eva aśeṣeṇa vaktum arhasi tvam eva vyañjaya iti arthaḥ yābhiḥ anantābhiḥ vibhūtibhiḥ yaiḥ niyamana viśeṣaiḥ yuktaḥ imān lokān tvam niyantṛ tvena vyāpya tiṣṭhasi aham yogī bhakti yoga niṣṭhaḥ san bhaktyā tvām sadā paricintayan cintayitum pravṛttaḥ cintanīyam tvām paripūrṇa aiśvaryā ādi kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇam katham vidyām pūrva ukta buddhi jñāna ādi bhāva vyatirikteṣu keṣu keṣu ca bhāveṣu mayā niyantṛ tvena cintyaḥ asi aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate iti saṃkṣepeṇa uktam tava sraṣṭṛ tva ādi yogam vibhūtim niyamanam ca bhūyaḥ vistareṇa kathaya tvayā ucyamānam tvad māhātmya amṛtam śṛṇvataḥ me tṛptiḥ na asti hi mama atṛptiḥ tvayā eva viditā iti abhiprāyaḥ he kuru śreṣṭha madīyāḥ kalyāṇīḥ vibhūtīḥ prādhānyataḥ te kathayiṣyāmi prādhanya śabdena utkarṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ purodhasām ca mukhyam mām iti hi vakṣyate jagati utkṛṣṭāḥ kāścana vibhūtīḥ vakṣyāmi vistareṇa vaktum śrotum ca na śakyate tāsām ānantyāt vibhūti tvam nāma niyāmya tvam sarveṣām bhūtānām buddhi ādayaḥ pṛthagvidhā bhāvā matta eva bhavanti iti uktvā etām vibhūtim yogam ca mama yaḥ vetti tattvataḥ iti pratipādanāt tathā tatra yoga śabda nirdiṣṭam sraṣṭṛ tva ādikam vibhuti śabda nirdiṣṭam tad pravartya tvam iti hi uktam punar ca aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate iti matvā bhajante mām budhā bhāva samanvitāḥ iti sarveṣām bhūtānām mama śarīra bhūtānām āśaye hṛdaye aham ātma tayā avasthitaḥ ātmā hi nāma śarīrasya sarva ātmanā ādhāraḥ niyantā śeṣī ca tathā vakṣyate sarvasya ca aham hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ matta ḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam ca  īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan sarva bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā dvādaśa saṃkhyā saṃkhyātānām ādityānām dvādaśaḥ ya utkṛṣṭaḥ viṣṇuḥ nāma ādityaḥ saḥ aham jyotiṣām jagati prakāśakānām yaḥ aṃśumān raviḥ āditya gaṇaḥ saḥ aham marutām utkṛṣṭaḥ marīciḥ yaḥ saḥ aham asmi nakṣatrāṇām aham śaśī na iyam nirdhāraṇe ṣaṣṭhī bhūtānām asmi cetanā itivat  nakṣatrāṇām patiḥ yaḥ candraḥ saḥ aham asmi vedānām ṛc yajuḥ sāma ātharvaṇām ya utkṛṣṭaḥ sāmavedaḥ saḥ aham devānām indraḥ aham asmi ekādaśānām indriyāṇām yad utkṛṣṭam mana indriyam tad aham asmi iyam api na nirdhāraṇe bhūtānām cetanāvatām yā cetanā saḥ aham asmi rudrāṇām ekādaśānām śaṅkaraḥ aham asmi yakṣa rakṣasām vaiśravaṇaḥ aham vasūnām aṣṭānām pāvakaḥ aham śikhariṇām śikhara śobhinām parvatānām madhye meruḥ aham purodhasām utkṛṣṭaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ yaḥ saḥ aham asmi senānīnām senāpatīnām skandaḥ aham asmi sarasām sāgaraḥ aham asmi mahā ṛṣīṇām marīci ādīnām bhṛguḥ aham artha abhidhāyinaḥ śabdā giraḥ tāsām ekam akṣaram praṇavaḥ aham asmi yajñānām utkṛṣṭaḥ japa yajñaḥ asmi pūrva mātrāṇām himavān aham uccaiśśravasam aśvānām viddhi mām amṛta udbhavam airāvatam gaja indrāṇām narāṇām ca narādhipam āyudhānām aham vajram dhenūnām asmi kāmadhuk prajanaḥ ca asmi kandarpaḥ sarpāṇām asmi vāsukiḥ ananta ḥ ca asmi nāgānām varuṇaḥ yādasām aham pitñṇām aryamā ca asmi yamaḥ saṃyamatām aham vṛkṣāṇām pūjyaḥ aśvatthaḥ aham deva rṣīṇam nāradaḥ aham kāmadhuk divyā surabhiḥ janana hetuḥ kandarpaḥ ca aham asmi sarpāḥ ekāśirasaḥ nāgāḥ bahu śirasaḥ yādāṃsi jala vāsinaḥ teṣām varuṇaḥ aham daṇḍayatām vaivasvataḥ aham anartha prepsutayā gaṇayatām madhye kālaḥ mṛtyuḥ aham pavatām gamana svabhāvānām pavanaḥ aham śastrabhṛtām rāmaḥ aham śastrabhṛt tvam atra vibhūtiḥ artha antara abhāvāt āditya ādayaḥ ca kṣetrajñā ātma tvena avasthitasya bhagavataḥ śarīra tayā dharma bhūtā iti śastrabhṛt tva sthānīyāḥ sṛjyanta iti sargāḥ teṣām ādiḥ kāraṇam sarvadā sṛjyamānānām sarveṣām prāṇinām tatra tatra sraṣṭāraḥ aham eva iti arthaḥ tathā antar sarvadā saṃhriyamāṇānām tatra tatra saṃhartāraḥ api aham eva tathā ca madhyam pālanam sarvadā pālyamānānām pālayitāraḥ ca aham eva iti arthaḥ jalpa vitaṇḍa ādi kurvatām tattva nirṇayāya pravṛttaḥ vādaḥ yaḥ saḥ aham akṣarāṇām madhye akāraḥ vai sarvā vāc  iti śruti siddhiḥ sarva varṇānām prakṛtiḥ akāraḥ aham sāmāsikaḥ samāsa samūhaḥ tasya madhye dvandva samāsaḥ aham sa hi ubhaya padārtha pradhāna tvena utkṛṣṭaḥ kalā muhūrta ādi mayaḥ akṣayaḥ kālaḥ aham eva sarvasya sraṣṭā hiraṇyagarbhaḥ caturmukhaḥ aham sarva prāṇa haraḥ mṛtyuḥ ca aham utpatsyamānānām udbhava ākhyam karma ca aham śrīḥ aham kīrtiḥ ca aham vāc ca aham smṛtiḥ ca aham medhā ca aham dhṛtiḥ ca aham kṣamā ca aham sāmnām bṛhatsāma aham chandasām gāyatrī aham kusuma ākaraḥ vasantaḥ chalam kurvatām chala āspadeṣu akṣa ādi lakṣaṇam dyutam aham jetñṇām jayaḥ asmi vyavasāyinām vyavasāyaḥ asmi sattvavatām sattvam aham sattvam mahāmanaḥ tvam vasudeva sūnu tvam atra vibhūtiḥ artha antara abhāvāt eva pāṇḍavānām dhanañjayaḥ arjunaḥ aham munayaḥ mananena ātma yāthātmya darśinaḥ teṣām vyāsaḥ aham kavayaḥ vipaścitaḥ niyama atikramaṇe daṇḍam kurvatām daṇḍaḥ aham vijigīṣūṇām jaya upāya bhūtā nītiḥ asmi guhyānām saṃbandhiṣu gaḥ pāneṣu maunam asmi jñānavatām jñānam ca aham sarva bhūtānām sarva avasthā avasthitānām tad tad avasthā bīja bhūtam pratīyamānam apratīyamānam ca yad tad aham eva bhūta jātam mayā ātma tayā avasthitena vinā yad syāt na tad asti aham ātmā guḍākeśa sarva bhūta āśaya sthitaḥ iti prakramāt  na tad asti vinā yad syāt mayā bhūtam carācaram iti atra api ātma tayā avasthānam eva vivakṣitam sarvam vastu jātam sarva avastham mayā ātma bhūtena yuktam syāt iti arthaḥ anena sarvasya asya sāmānādhikaraṇya nirdeśasya ātmatayā avasthitiḥ eva hetuḥ iti prakaṭitam mama divyānām kalyāṇīnām vibhūtīnām antaḥ na asti eṣa tu vibhūteḥ vistaraḥ mayā kaiścid upādhibhiḥ saṃkṣepataḥ
