proktaḥ yad yad vibhūtimat iśitavya saṃpannam bhūta jātam śrīmat kāntimat dhana dhānya samṛddham vā ūrjitam kalyāṇa ārambheṣu udyuktam tad tad mama tejaḥ aṃśa saṃbhavam iti avagaccha tejaḥ para abhibhavana sāmarthyam mama acintya śakteḥ niyamana śakti eka deśa saṃbhavati iti arthaḥ bahunā etena ucyamānena jñānena kim prayojanam idam cit acit ātmakam kṛtsnam jagat kārya avastham kāraṇa avastham sthūlam sūkṣmam ca svarūpa sadbhāve sthitau pravṛtti bhede ca yathā mad saṅkalpam na ativarteta tathā mama mahimnaḥ ayuta ayuta aṃśena viṣṭabhya aham avasthitaḥ yathā uktam bhagavatā parāśareṇa yasya ayuta ayuta aṃśa aṃśe viśva śaktiḥ iyam sthitā iti deha ātmā abhimāna rūpa mohena mohitasya mama anugraha eka prayojanāya paramam guhyam paramam rahasyam adhyātma saṃjñitam ātmani vaktavyam vacaḥ na tu eva aham jātu na asam ityādi tasmāt yogī bhava arjuna iti etad antam yad tvayā uktam tena ayam mama ātma viṣayaḥ mohaḥ sarvaḥ vigataḥ dūrataḥ nirastaḥ saptama prabhṛti daśama paryante tvad vyatiriktānām sarveṣām bhūtānām tvattaḥ paramātmanaḥ bhava apyayau utpatti pralayau vistaraśaḥ mayā śrutau hi kamala patra akṣa tava avyayam nityam sarva cetana acetana vastu śeṣi tvam jñāna bala ādi kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇaiḥ tava eva paratara tvam sarva ādhāra tvam cintita nimiṣita ādi sarva pravṛttiṣu tava eva pravartayitṛ tvam ityādi aparimitam māhātmyam ca śrutam hi śabdaḥ vakṣyamāṇa didṛkṣādyotana arthaḥ he parameśvara evam etad iti avadhṛtam yathā atha tvam ātmānam bravīṣi puruṣottama āśrita vātsalya jaladhe tava aiśvaram tvad asādhāraṇam sarvasya praśāsitṛ tve pālayitṛ tve sraṣṭṛ tve saṃhartṛ tve bhartṛ tve kalyāṇa guṇa ākara tve paratara tve sakala itara visajātīya tve avasthitam rūpam draṣṭum sākṣātkartum icchāmi tad sarvasya sraṣṭṛ sarvasya praśāsitṛ sarvasya ādhāra bhūtam tvad rūpam mayā draṣṭum śakyam iti yadi manyase tataḥ yogeśvara yogaḥ jñāna ādi kalyāṇa guṇa yogaḥ paśya me yogam aiśvaram iti hi vakṣyate tvad vyatiriktasya kasya api asaṃbhāvitānām jñāna balāi śvarya vīrya śakti tejasām nidhe ātmānam tvām avyayam me darśaya avyayam iti kriyā viśeṣaṇam tvām sakalam me darśaya iti arthaḥ paśya me sarva āśrayāṇi rūpāṇi atha śataśaḥ sahasraśaḥ ca nānāvidhāni nānā prakārāṇi divyāni aprākṛtāni nānā varṇa ākṛtīni śukla kṛṣṇa ādi nānāvarṇāni nānā ākārāṇi ca paśya mama ekasmin rūpe paśya ādityān dvādaśa vasūn aṣṭau rudrān ekādaśa aśvinau dvau maruta ḥ ca ekonapañcāśatam pradarśana artham idam iha jagati pratyakṣa dṛṣṭāni śāstra dṛṣṭāni ca yāni vastūni tāni sarvāṇi anyāni api sarveṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu ca śāstreṣu adṛṣṭa pūrvāṇi bahūni āścaryāṇi paśya iha mama ekasmin dehe tatra api ekastham eka deśa stham sacarācaram kṛtsnam jagat paśya yad ca anyat draṣṭum icchasi tad api eka deha eka deśa eva paśya aham mama deha eka deśe sarvam jagad darśayiṣyāmi tvam tu anena niyata parimita vastu grāhiṇā prākṛtena sva cakṣuṣā mām tathābhūtam sakala itara visajātīyam aparimeyam draṣṭum na śakṣyase tava divyam aprākṛtam mad darśana sādhanam cakṣuḥ dadāmi paśya me yogam aiśvaram mada sādhāraṇam yogam paśya mama ananta jñāna ādi yogam ananta vibhūti yogam ca paśya iti arthaḥ evam uktvā sārathye avasthitaḥ pārtha mātula jaḥ mahā yoga īśvaraḥ hariḥ mahā āścarya yogānām īśvaraḥ para brahma bhūtaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paramam aiśvaram svāsa ādhāraṇam rūpam pārthāya pitṛṣvasuḥ pṛthāyāḥ putrāya darśayām āsa tad vividha vicitra nikhila jagat āśrayam viśvasya praśāsitṛ ca rūpam tad ca īdṛśam aneka vaktra nayanam aneka adbhuta darśanam aneka divya ābharaṇam divya aneka udyata āyudham divya mālya ambara dharam divya gandha anulepanam sarva āścarya mayam devam anantam viśvatomukham devam dyotamānam anantam kāla traya varti nikhila jagat āśrayatayā deśa kāla pariccheda anarham viśvatomukham viśva diḥ varti mukham sva ucita divya ambara gandha mālya ābharaṇa āyudha anvitam tejasaḥ aparimita tva darśana artham idam akṣaya tejassvarūpam iti arthaḥ tatra anantāyām avistāre ananta bāhu udara vaktra netre aparimita tejaske aparimita divya āyudha upete sva ucita aparimita divya bhūṣaṇe divya mālya ambara dhare divya gandha anulepane ananta āścarya maye devadevasya divye śarīre anekadhā pravibhaktam brahma ādi vividha vicitra deva tiryak manuṣya sthāvara ādi bhoktṛ varga pṛthivī antarikṣa svarga pātāla atala vitala sutala ādi bhoga sthāna bhogya bhoga upakaraṇ prakṛti puruṣa ātmakam kṛtsnam jagat  aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate  hanta te kathayiṣyāmi vibhūtīḥ ātmanaḥ śubhāḥ  aham ātmā guḍākeśa sarva bhūta āśaya sthitaḥ ādityānām aham viṣṇuḥ ityādinā na tad asti vinā yad syāt mayā bhūtam carācaram  viṣṭabhya aham idam kṛtsnam eka aṃśena sthitaḥ jagat ityantena uditam ekastham eka deśa stham pāṇḍavaḥ bhagavat prasāda labdha tad darśana anuguṇa divya cakṣuḥ apaśyat tataḥ dhanañjayaḥ mahā āścaryasya kṛtsnasya jagataḥ sva deha eka deśena āśraya bhūtam kṛtsnasya pravartayitāram ca āścaryatama ananta jñāna ādi kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇam devam dṛṣṭvā vismaya āviṣṭaḥ hṛṣṭa romā śirasā daṇḍavat  praṇamya kṛtāñjaliḥ abhāṣata deva tava dehe sarvān devān paśyāmi tathā sarvān prāṇi viśeṣāṇām saṃghān tathā brahmāṇam caturmukham aṇḍa adhipatim tathā īśam kamalāsana stham kamala āsane brahmaṇi sthitam īśam tad mate avasthitam tathā deva ṛṣi pramukhān sarvān ṛṣīn uraga an  ca vāsuki takṣaka ādīn dīptān aneka bāhu udara vaktra netram ananta rūpam tvām sarvataḥ paśyāmi viśveśvara viśvasya niyantaḥ viśvarūpa viśva śarīra yataḥ tvam anantaḥ ataḥ tava na antam na madhyam na punar tava ādim ca paśyāmi tejaḥ rāśim sarvataḥ dīptimantam samantāt durnirīkṣam dīpta anala arka dyutim aprameyam tvām kirīṭinam gadinam cakriṇam ca paśyāmi upaniṣatsu dve vidye veditavye ityādiṣu veditavyatayā nirdiṣṭam paramam akṣaram tvam eva asya viśvasya param nidhānam viśvasya asya parama ādhāra bhūta ḥ tvam eva tvam avyayaḥ vyaya rahitaḥ yad svarūpaḥ yad guṇaḥ yad vibhavaḥ ca tvam tena eva rūpeṇa sarvadā avatiṣṭhase śāśvata dharma goptā śāśvatasya nityasya vaidikasya dharmasya evam ādibhiḥ avatāraiḥ tvam eva goptā sanātanaḥ tvam puruṣaḥ mataḥ me veda aham etam puruṣam mahāntaṃ  parāt param puruṣam iti ādiṣu uditaḥ sanātana puruṣa ḥ tvam eva iti me mataḥ jñātaḥ yad ukula tilaka ḥ tvam evaṃbhūta idānīm sākṣātkṛtaḥ mayā iti arthaḥ anādi madhya antam ādi madhya anta rahitam ananta vīryam anavadhika atiśaya vīryam vīrya śabdaḥ pradarśana arthaḥ anavadhika atiśaya jñāna balāi śvarya vīrya śakti tejasām nidhim iti arthaḥ ananta bāhum asaṃkhyeya bāhum saḥ api pradarśana arthaḥ ananta bāhu udara pāda vaktra ādikam śaśi sūrya netram śaśivat  sūryavac ca prasāda pratāpa yukta sarva netram deva ādīn anukūlān namaskāra ādi kurvāṇān prati prasādaḥ tad viparītān asura rākṣasa ādīn prati pratāpaḥ rakṣāṃsi bhītāni diśaḥ dravanti sarve namasyanti ca siddha saṃghāḥ iti hi vakṣyate dīpta hutāśa vaktram pradīpta kāla analavat  saṃhāra anuguṇa vaktram sva tejasā viśvam idam tapantam tejaḥ para abhibhavana sāmarthyam svakīyena tejasā viśvam idam tapantam tvām paśyāmi evambhūtam sarvasya sraṣṭāram sarvasya ādhāra bhūtam sarvasya praśāsitāram sarvasya saṃhartāram jñāna ādi parimita guṇa sāgaram ādi madhya anta rahitam evaṃbhūta divya deham tvām yathā upadeśam sākṣāt karomi iti arthaḥ ekasmin divya dehe aneka udara ādikam katham ittham upapadyate ekasmāt kaṭi pradeśāt ananta parimāṇāt ūrdhvam udgatā yathā udita udara ādayaḥ adhaḥ ca yathā udita divya pādāḥ tatra ekasmin mukhe netra dvayam iti ca na virodhaḥ dyu śabdaḥ pṛthivī śabdaḥ ca ubhau uparitanānām adhastanānām ca lokānām pradarśana arthau dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ antaram avakāśaḥ yasmin  avakāse sarve lokāḥ tiṣṭhanti sarvaḥ ayam avakāśaḥ diśaḥ ca sarvāḥ tvayā ekena vyāptāḥ dṛṣṭvā adbhutam rūpam ugram tava idam anantāyām avistāram ati adbhutam ati ugram ca rūpam dṛṣṭvā lokatrayam pravyathitam yuddha didṛkṣayā āgateṣu brahma ādi deva asura pitṛ gaṇa siddha gandharva yakṣa rākṣaseṣu pratikūla anukūla madhya stha rūpam lokatrayam sarvam pravyathitam atyanta bhītam mahātman aparicchedya manaḥ vṛtte eteṣām api arjunasya eva viśva āśraya rūpa sākṣātkāra sādhanam divyam cakṣuḥ bhagavatā dattam kim artham iti ced arjunāya svāiśvaryam sarvam pradarśayitum ata idam ucyate dṛṣṭvā adbhutam rūpam ugram tava idam lokatrayam pravyarthitam mahātman iti amī sura saṃghāḥ utkṛṣṭā aḥ tvām viśva āśrayam avalokya hṛṣṭa manasaḥ tvan samīpam viśanti teṣu eva kecid ati ugram ati adbhutam ca tava ākāram ālokya bhītāḥ prāñjalayaḥ sva jñāna anuguṇam stuti rūpāṇi vākyāni gṛṇanti uccārayanti apare mahā ṛṣi saṃghāḥ siddha saṃghāḥ ca parāvara tattva yāthātmya vidaḥ svasti iti uktvā puṣkalābhiḥ bhavat anurūpābhiḥ stutibhiḥ stuvanti ūṣmapāḥ pitaraḥ u ūṣma bhāgā hi pitaraḥ iti śruteḥ ete sarve vismayam āpannāḥ tvām vīkṣante bahvībhiḥ daṃṣṭrābhiḥ ati bhīṣaṇa ākāram lokāḥ pūrva uktāḥ pratikūla anukūla madhya sthāḥ trividhāḥ sarva eva aham ca tad evam īdṛśam rūpam dṛṣṭvā atīva vyathitā bhavāmaḥ namaḥ śabdaḥ tad akṣare parame vyoman āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt  kṣayantam asya rajasaḥ parāke  yaḥ asya adhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman ityādi śruti siddhi triguṇa prakṛti atīta parama vyoma vācī sa vikārasya prakṛti tattvasya puruṣasya ca sarva avasthasya kṛtsnasya āśraya tayā nabhaḥ spṛśam iti vacanāt  dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ idam antaram hi vyāptam iti pūrva ukta tvāt ca dīptam aneka varṇam vyātta ānanam dīpta viśāla netram tvām dṛṣṭvā pravyathita antarātmā atyanta bhīta manāḥ dhṛtim na vindāmi dehasya dhāraṇam na labhe manasaḥ ca indriyāṇām ca śamam na labhe viṣṇaḥ vyāpin sarva vyāpinam atimātram ati adbhutam ati ghoram ca tvām dṛṣṭvā praśithika sarva avayavaḥ vyākula indriyaḥ ca bhavāmi iti arthaḥ yuga anta kāla analavat  sarva saṃhāre pravṛttāni ati ghorāṇi tava mukhāni dṛṣṭvā diśaḥ na jāne sukham ca na labhe jagatām nivāsa deveśa brahma ādīnām īśvarāṇām api parama maheśvara mām prati prasannaḥ bhava yathā aham prakṛtim gataḥ bhavāmi tathā kurv iti arthaḥ vaktrāṇi te tvaramāṇā viśanti daṃṣṭrā karālāni bhayānakāni kecid vilagnā daśana antareṣu saṃdṛśyante cūrṇitaiḥ uttamāṅgaiḥ amī dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāḥ duryodhana āt ayaḥ sarve bhīṣmaḥ droṇaḥ sūtaputraḥ karṇaḥ ca tad pakṣīyaiḥ avanipāla samūhaiḥ sarvaiḥ asmadīyaiḥ api kaiścid yodha mukhyaiḥ saha tvaramāṇā daṃṣṭrā karālāni bhayānakāni tava vaktrāṇi vināśāya viśanti tatra kecid cūrṇitaiḥ uttamāṅgaiḥ daśāna antareṣu vilagnāḥ saṃdṛśyante yathā pradīpta jvalanam pataṅgā viśanti nāśāya samṛddha vegāḥ tathā eva nāśāya viśanti lokāḥ tava api vaktrāṇi samṛddha vegāḥ ete rāja lokāḥ bahavaḥ nadīnām ambu pravāhāḥ samudram iva pradīpta jvalanam iva ca śalabhāḥ tava vaktrāṇi abhivijvalanti svayam eva tvaramāṇā ātma nāśāya viśanti rāja lokān samagrān jvaladbhiḥ vadanaiḥ grasamānaḥ kopa vegena tad rudhira avasiktam oṣṭha puṭa ādikam lelihyase punar punar lehanam karoṣi tava ati ghorā bhāsaḥ raśmayaḥ tejobhiḥ svakīyaiḥ prakāśaiḥ jagat samagram āpūrya pratapanti darśaya ātmānam avyayam iti tava aiśvaryam niraṅkuśam sākṣāt kartum prārthitena bhavatā niraṅkuśam aiśvaryam darśayatā ati ghora rūpam idam āviṣkṛtam ati ghora rūpaḥ kaḥ bhavān kim kartum pravṛtta iti bhavantam jñātum icchāmi tava abhipretām pravṛttim na jānāmi etad ākhyāhi me namaḥ astu te deva vara prasīda namaḥ te astu sarva īśvara evam kartum anena abhiprāyeṇa idam saṃhartṛ rūpam āviṣkṛtam iti uktvā prasanna rūpa ḥ ca bhava kalayati gaṇayati iti kālaḥ sarveṣām dhārtarāṣṭra pramukhānām rāja lokānām āyuḥ avasānam gaṇayan  aham tad kṣaya kṛt ghora rūpeṇa pravṛddhaḥ rāja lokān samāhartum ābhimukhyena saṃhartum iha pravṛttaḥ asmi ataḥ mad saṃkalpāt eva tvām ṛte api tvad udyogāt rte api ete dhārtarāṣṭra pramukhāḥ tava pratyanīkeṣu ye avasthitā yodhāḥ te sarve na bhaviṣyanti vinaṅkṣyanti tasmāt tvam tān prati yuddhāya uttiṣṭha tān śatrūn jitvā yaśaḥ labhasva dharmyam rājyam ca samṛddham bhuṅkṣva mayā eva ete kṛta aparādhāḥ pūrvam eva nihatāḥ hanane viniyuktāḥ tvam tu teṣām hanane nimitta mātram bhava mayā hanyamānānām śatra ādi sthānīyaḥ bhava savyasācin ṣaca samavāye savyena śara sacana śīlaḥ savyasācī savyena api kareṇa śara samavāya karaḥ kara dvayena yoddhum samartha iti arthaḥ droṇa bhīṣma karṇa ādīn kṛta aparādha tayā mayā eva hanane viniyuktān tvam jahi tvam hanyāḥ etān gurūn bandhūn  ca anyān api bhoga saktān katham haniṣyāmi iti mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ tān uddiśya dharma adharma bhayena bandhu snehena kāruṇyena ca mā vyathām kṛthāḥ yataḥ te kṛta aparādhā mayā eva hanane viniyuktāḥ ataḥ nirviśaṅkaḥ yudhyasva raṇe sapatnān jetāsi jeṣyasi na eteṣām vadhe nṛśaṃsa tā gandhaḥ api tu jaya eva labhyata iti arthaḥ etad aśrita vātsalya jaladheḥ keśavasya vacanam śrutvā arjuna ḥ tasmai namaskṛtya bhīta bhītaḥ bhūyaḥ tam praṇamya kṛtāñjaliḥ vepamānaḥ kirīṭī sa gadgadam āha sthāne yuktam yad etad yuddha didṛkṣayā āgatam aśeṣa deva gandharva siddha yakṣa vidyādhara kinnara kiṃpuruṣa ādikam jagat tvad prasādāt tvām sarveśvaram avalokya tava prakīrtyā sarvam prahṛṣyati anurajyate ca yad ca tvām avalokya rakṣāṃsi bhītāni sarvā diśaḥ pradravanti sarve siddha saṃghāḥ siddha ādi anukūla saṃghāḥ namasyanti ca tad etad sarvam yuktam iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ ananta deveśa jagannivāsa tvam eva akṣaram na kṣarati iti akṣaram jīva ātma tattvam na jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit iti ādi śruti siddhaḥ jīvātmā hi na kṣarati sat asac ca tvam eva sat asat śabda nirdiṣṭam kārya kāraṇa bhāvena avasthitam prakṛti tattvam nāma rūpa vibhāgavat tayā kārya avastham sat śabda nirdiṣṭam tad anarhatayā kāraṇa avastham asat śabda nirdiṣṭam ca tvam eva tad param yad tasmāt prakṛteḥ prakṛti saṃbandhinaḥ ca jīvātmanaḥ param anyan mukta ātma tattvam yad tad api tvam eva jagati sarvaḥ veditā vedyam ca sarvam tvam eva evam sarva ātma tayā avasthitaḥ tvam eva param ca dhāma sthānam prāpya sthānam iti arthaḥ tvayā tatam viśvam ananta rūpa tvayā ātma tvena viśvam cit acit miśram jagat tatam vyāptam namaḥ purastād atha pṛṣṭhataḥ te namaḥ astu te sarvata eva sarva ananta vīrya amita vikramaḥ tvam sarvam samāpnoṣi tataḥ asi sarvaḥ amita vīrya aparimita parākramaḥ tvam sarva ātma tayā samāpnoṣi tataḥ sarvaḥ asi yataḥ tvam sarvam cit acit vastu jātam ātma tayā samāpnoṣi ataḥ sarvasya cit acit vastu jātasya tvad śarīra tayā tvad prakāra tvāt sarva prakāra ḥ tvam eva sarva śabda vācyaḥ asi iti arthaḥ tvam akṣaram sat asat  vāyuḥ yamaḥ agniḥ ityādi sarva sāmānādhikaraṇya nirdeśasya ātmatayā vyāptiḥ eva hetuḥ iti su vyaktam uktam tvayā tatam viśvam ananta rūpa  sarvam samāpnoṣi tataḥ asi sarvaḥ iti ca yaḥ ca apahāsa artham asatkṛtaḥ asi vihāra śayyā āsana bhojaneṣu ekaḥ atha vā api acyuta tad samakṣam tad kṣāmaye tvām aham aprameyam tava ananta vīrya tva amita vikrama tva sarva antarātma tva sraṣṭṛ tva ādikaḥ yaḥ mahimā tam imam ajānatā mayā pramādān mohāt praṇayena cira paricayena vā sakhā iti mama vayasyaḥ iti matvā he kṛṣṇa he yādava he sakhā iti tvayi prasabham vinaya apetam yad uktam yad ca prihāsa artham sarvadā eva satkāra arha ḥ tvam asatkṛtaḥ asi vihāra śayyā āsana bhojaneṣu ca saha kṛteṣu ekānte vaḥ samakṣam vā yad asatkṛtaḥ asi tad sarvam tvām aprameyam aham kṣāmaye apratima prabhāva tvam asya sarvasya carācarasya lokasya pitā asi asya lokasya guru ḥ ca asi ataḥ tvam asya carācarasya lokasya garīyān pūjyatamaḥ na tvad samaḥ asti abhyadhikaḥ kutaḥ anyaḥ lokatraye api tvad anyaḥ kāruṇya ādinā kena api guṇena na tvad samaḥ asti kutaḥ abhyadhikaḥ yasmāt tvam sarvasya pitā pūjyatamaḥ guru ḥ ca kāruṇya ādi guṇaiḥ ca sarva adhikaḥ asi tasmāt tvām īśam īḍyam praṇamya praṇidhāya ca kāyam prasādaye yathā kṛta aparādhasya api putrasya yathā ca sakhyuḥ praṇāma pūrvam prārthitaḥ pitā vā sakhā vā prasīdati tathā tvam parama kāruṇikaḥ priyāya me sarvam soḍhum arhasi adṛṣṭa pūrvam ati adbhutam ati ugram ca tava rūpam dṛṣṭvā hṛṣitaḥ asmi prītaḥ asmi bhayena pravyathitam ca me manaḥ ataḥ tad eva tava su prasannam rūpam me darśaya prasīda deveśa jagannivāsa mayi prasādam kuru devānām brahma ādīnām api īśa nikhila jagat āśraya bhūta tathā eva pūrvavat kirīṭinam gadinam cakra hastam tvām draṣṭum icchāmi ataḥ tena eva pūrva siddhena catur bhujena rūpeṇa yuktaḥ bhava sahasra bāhaḥ viśvamūrte idānīm sahasra bāhu tvena viśva śarīra tvena dṛśyamāna rūpa ḥ tvam tena eva rūpeṇa yuktaḥ bhava iti arthaḥ yad me tejaḥ mayam tejasām rāśiḥ viśvam viśvātma bhūtam anantam antarahitam pradarśana artham idam ādi madhya anta rahitam ādyam mad vyatiriktasya kṛtsnasya ādi bhūtam tvad anyena kena api na dṛṣṭa pūrvam rūpam tad idam prasannena mayā mad bhaktāya te darśitam ātma yogāt atmanaḥ satya saṃkalpa tva yogāt evaṃrūpaḥ yathāvat avathitaḥ aham mayi bhaktimataḥ tvad taḥ anyena ekānta bhakti rahitena kena api puruṣeṇa veda yajña ādibhiḥ kevalaiḥ draṣṭum na śakyaḥ īdṛśa ghora rūpa darśanena te yā vyathā yaḥ ca vimūḍha bhāvaḥ vartate tad ubhayam mā bhūt tvayā abhyasta pūrvam eva saumyam rūpam darśayāmi tad eva idam mama rūpam prapaśya evam pāṇḍu tanayam bhagavān vasudeva sūnuḥ uktvā bhūyaḥ svakīyam eva catur bhujam rūpam darśayām āsa aparicitarupa darśanena bhītam enam punar api paricita saumya vapuḥ bhūtvā āśvāsayām āsa ca mahātmā satya saṅkalpaḥ asya sarva īśvarasya parama puruṣasya parasya brahmaṇaḥ jagat upakṛti martyasya vasudeva sūnoḥ catur bhujam eva svakīyam rūpam kaṃsāt bhīta vasudeva prārthanena ākaṃsa vadhāt bhuja dvayam upasaṃhṛtam paścāt āviṣkṛtam ca jātaḥ asi deva deveśa śaṅkha cakra gadā dhara divyam rūpam idam deva prasādena upsaṃhara anavadhika atiśaya saundarya saukumārya lāvaṇya ādi yuktam tava eva asādhāraṇam manuṣya tva saṃsthāna saṃsthitam ati saumyam idam tava rūpam dṛṣṭvā idānīm sa cetāḥ saṃvṛttaḥ asmi prakṛtim gata ḥ ca mama idam sarvasya praśāsane avasthitam sarva asrayam sarva kāraṇa bhūtam rūpam yad dṛṣṭavān asi tad su durdarśam na kena api draṣṭum śakyam asya rūpasya devāḥ api nityam darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ na tu dṛṣṭavantaḥ bhaktyā tu ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidhaḥ arjuna jñātum draṣṭum ca tattvena praveṣṭum ca parantapa vedaiḥ adhyāpana pravacana adhyayana śravaṇa japa viṣayaiḥ yāga dāna homa tapobhiḥ ca mad bhakti virahitaiḥ kevalaiḥ yathāvat avasthitaḥ aham draṣṭum aśakyaḥ ananyayā tu bhaktyā tattvata ḥ śāstraiḥ jñātum tattvataḥ sākṣāt kartum tattvataḥ praveṣṭum ca śakyaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ na ayam ātmā pravacanena labhyaḥ na medhayā na bahunā śrutena yam eva eṣa vṛṇute tena labhya ḥ tasya eṣa ātmā vivṛṇute tanūm svām iti veda adhyayana ādīni sarvāṇi karmāṇi mad ārādhana rūpāṇi iti yaḥ karoti sa mad karma kṛt mad paramaḥ sarveṣām ārambhāṇām aham eva parama uddeśyaḥ yasya sa mad paramaḥ mad bhaktaḥ atyartha mad priya tvena mad kīrtana stuti dhyāna arcana praṇāma ādibhiḥ vinā ātma dhāraṇam alabhamānaḥ mad eka prayojana tayā yaḥ satatam tāni karoti sa mad bhaktaḥ saṅga varjitaḥ mad eka priya tvena itara saṅgam asahamānaḥ nirvairaḥ sarva bhūteṣu mad saṃśleṣa viyoga eka sukha duḥkha svabhāva tvāt sva duḥkhasya sva aparādhana nimitta tva anusaṃdhānāt ca sarva bhūtānām parama puruṣa paratantra tva anusaṃdhānāt ca sarva bhūteṣu vaira nimitta abhāvāt teṣu nirvairaḥ ya evam bhūtaḥ sa mām iti mām yathāvat avasthitam prāpnoti nirasta avidyā ādi aśeṣa doṣa gandhaḥ mad eka anubhavaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ evam mad karma kṛt ityādinā uktena prakāreṇa satata yuktāḥ bhagavantam tvām eva param prāpyam manvānāḥ ye bhaktāḥ tvām sakala vibhūti yuktam anavadhika atiśaya saundarya sauśīlya sārvajñi satya saṃkalpa tva ādi ananta guṇa sāgaram paripūrṇam upāsate ye ca api akṣaram pratyagātma svarūpam tad eva ca avyaktam cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa anabhivyakta svarūpam upāsate teṣām ubhayeṣām ke yoga vittamāḥ ke sva sādhyam prati śīghra gāmina iti arthaḥ bhavāmi na cirāt pārtha iti uttaratra yoga vittama tvam śaighrya viṣayam iti hi vyañjayiṣyate atyartha mad priya tvena manaḥ mayi āveśya śraddhayā parayā upetāḥ nitya yuktāḥ nitya yogam kāṅkṣamāṇāḥ ye mām upāsate prāpya viṣayam manaḥ mayi āveśya ye mām upāsata iti arthaḥ te yuktatamāḥ mām sukhena acirāt prāpnuvanti iti arthaḥ sanniyamya indriya grāmam sarvatra sama buddhayaḥ te prāpnuvanti mām eva sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ kleśaḥ adhikatara ḥ teṣām avyakta āsakta cetasām avyaktā hi gatiḥ duḥkham dehavadbhiḥ avāpyate ye tu akṣaram pratyagātma svarūpam anirdeśyam dehāt anyatayā deva ādi śabda anirdeśyam tataḥ eva cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇānabhivyaktam sarvatragam acintyam ca sarvatra deva ādi deheṣu vartamānam api tad visajātīya tayā tena tena rūpeṇa cintayitum anarham tataḥ eva kūṭastham sarva sādhāraṇam tad tad deva ādi asādhāraṇa ākāra asaṃbaddham iti arthaḥ apariṇāmi tvena svāsa ādhāraṇa ākārān na calati na cyavata iti acalam tataḥ eva dhruvam nityam sat niyāmya indriya grāmam cakṣuḥ ādikam indriya grāmam sarvam sva vyāpārebhya ḥ samyak niyamya sarvatra sama buddhayaḥ sarvatra deva ādi viṣama ākāreṣu deheṣu avasthiteṣu ātmasu jñāna eka ākāra tayā sama buddhayaḥ tataḥ eva sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ sarva bhūta ahita rahita tvāt nivṛttāḥ sarva bhūta ahita rahita tvam hi ātmanaḥ deva ādi viṣama ākāra abhimāna nimittam ya evam akṣaram upāsate te api mām prāpnuvanti eva mad samāna ākāram asaṃsāriṇam ātmānam prāpnuvanti eva iti arthaḥ mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ iti hi vakṣyate śrūyate ca nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti tathā akṣara śabda nirdiṣṭāt kūṭasthād anya tvam parasya brahmaṇaḥ vakṣyate kūṭasthaḥ akṣara ucyate uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anyaḥ iti atha parā yayā tad akṣaram adhikgamyate iti akṣara vidyāyām tu akṣara śabda nirdiṣṭam param eva brahma bhūta yoni tva ādeḥ teṣām avyakta āsakta cetasām kleśa ḥ tu adhikataraḥ avyaktā hi gatiḥ avyakta viṣayā manaḥ vṛttiḥ dehavadbhiḥ deha ātmā abhimāna yuktaiḥ duḥkhena avāpyate dehavantaḥ hi deham eva ātmānam manyante teṣām aham samuddhartā mṛtyu saṃsāra sāgarāt bhavāmi na cirāt pārtha mayi āveśita cetasām ye tu laukikāni deha yātrā aśeṣa bhūtāni deha dhāraṇa arthāni ca aśana ādīni karmāṇi vaidikāni ca yaga dāna homa tapaḥ prabhṛtīni sarvāṇi sa kāraṇāni sa uddeśyāni adhyātma cetasā mayi saṃnyasya mad parāḥ mad eka prāpyāḥ ananyena eva yogena ananya prayojanena yogena mām dhyāyanta upāsate dhyāna arcana praṇāma stuti kīrtana ādīni svayam eva atyartha priyāṇi prāpya samāni kurvantaḥ mām upāsata iti arthaḥ teṣām mad prāpti virodhitayā mṛtyu bhūtāt saṃsāra ākhyāt sāgarāt aham acireṇa eva kālena samuddhartā bhavāmi ataḥ atiśayita puruṣa artha tvāt sulabha tvāt aciralabhya tvāt ca mayi eva mana ādhatsva mayi manassamādhānam kuru mayi buddhim niveśaya aham eva parama prāpya iti adhyavasāyam kuru ata ūrdhvam mayi eva nivasiṣyasi aham eva parama prāpya iti adhyavasāya pūrvaka manaḥ niveśana anantaram eva mayi nivasiṣyasi iti arthaḥ atha sahasā eva mayi sthiram cittam samādhātum na śaknoṣi tataḥ abhyāsa yogena mām āptum iccha svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya saundarya sauśīlya sauhārda vātsalya kāruṇya mādhurya gāmbhīryāu dārya śairya vīrya parākrama sārvajñya satya kāma tva satyaḥ nikhila heya pratyanīke mayi niratiśaya prema garbha smṛti abhyāsa yogena sthiram citta samādhānam labdhvā mām prāptum iccha atha evaṃvidha smṛti abhyāse api asamarthaḥ asi mad karma paramaḥ bhava madīyāni karmāṇi ālaya nirmāṇa udyona karaṇa pradī pāra upaṇa mārjana abhyukṣaṇa upalepana puṣpa āharaṇa pūjā pravartana nāma saṃkīrtana pradakṣiṇa stuti namaskāra ādīni tāni atyartha priya tvena ācara atyartha priya tvena mad artham karmāṇi kurvan  api acirāt abhyāsa yoga pūrvikām mayi sthirām citta sthitim labdhvā mad prāpti rūpām siddhim avāpsyasi atha mad yogam āśritya etad api kartum na śaknoṣi mad guṇa anusandhāna kṛtamad eka priya tva ākāram bhakti yogam āśritya bhakti yoga aṅkura rūpam etad mad karmā api kartum na śaknoṣi tataḥ akṣara yogam ātma svabhāva anusandhāna rūpam para bhakti jananam pūrva ṣaṭka uditam āśritya tad upāya tayā sarva karma phala tyāgam kuru mad priya tvena mad eka prāpyatā buddhiḥ hi prakṣīṇa aśeṣa pāpasya eva jāyate yata ātmavān yatamanaskaḥ tataḥ anabhisaṃhita phalena mad ārādhana rūpeṇa anuṣṭhitena karmaṇā siddhena ātma dhyānena nivṛtta avidyā ādi sarva tirodhāne mad śeṣa tā eka svarūpe pratyagātmani sākṣātkṛte sati mayi parā bhaktiḥ svayam eva utpadyate tathā ca vakṣyate sva karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ iti ārabhya vimucya nirmamaḥ śāntaḥ brahma bhūyāya kalapate brahma bhūtaḥ prasanna ātmā na śocati na kāṅkṣati samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu mad bhaktim labhate parām iti atyartha prīti virahitāt karkaśa rūpāt smṛti abhyāsāt akṣara yāthātmya anusandhāna pūrvakam tadā aparokṣya jñānam eva ātma hita tvena viśiṣyate ātma aparokṣya jñānāt api aniṣpanna rūpāt tad upāya bhūta ātma dhyānam eva ātma hita tve viśiṣyate tad dhyānāt api aniṣpanna rūpāt tad upāya bhūtam phala tyāgena anuṣṭhitam karma eva viśiṣyate anabhisaṃhita phalāt anuṣṭhitāt karmaṇaḥ anantaram eva nirasta pāpa tayā manasaḥ śāntiḥ bhaviṣyati śānte manasi ātma dhyānam saṃpatsyate dhyāna āt ca tadā aparokṣyam tadā aparokṣyāt parā bhaktiḥ iti bhakti yoga abhyāsa aśaktasya ātma niṣṭhā eva śreyasī ātma niṣṭhasya api aśānta manasaḥ niṣṭhā prāptaye antargata ātma jñāna anabhisaṃhita phala karma niṣṭhā eva śreyasi iti arthaḥ santuṣṭaḥ satatam yogī yata ātmā dṛḍha niścayaḥ mayi arpita manaḥ buddhiḥ yaḥ mad bhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥ adveṣṭā sarva bhūtānām vidviṣatām apakurvatām api sarveṣām bhūtānām adveṣṭā mad aparādha anuguṇam īśvara preritāni etāni bhūtāni dviṣanti apakurvanti ca iti anusandadhānaḥ teṣu dviṣatsu apkurvatsu ca sarva bhūteṣu maitrīm matim kurvan maitraḥ teṣu eva duḥkhiteṣu karuṇām kurvan karuṇaḥ nirmamaḥ deha indriyeṣu tad saṃbandhiṣu ca nirmamaḥ nirahaṅkāraḥ deha ātmā abhimāna rahitaḥ tataḥ eva sama duḥkha sukhaḥ sukha duḥkha āgamayoḥ sa aṅkalpikayoḥ harṣa udvega rahitaḥ kṣamī sparśa prabhavayoḥ avarjanīyayoḥ api tayoḥ vikāra rahitaḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ yadṛcchā upanatena yena kena api deha dhāraṇa dravyeṇa saṃtuṣṭaḥ satatam yogī satatam prakṛti viyukta ātma anusandhāna paraḥ yata ātmā niyamita manaḥ vṛttiḥ dṛḍha niścayaḥ adhyātma śāstra uditeṣu artheṣu dṛḍha niścayaḥ mayi arpita manaḥ buddhiḥ bhagavān vāset eva eva anabhisaṃhita phalena anuṣṭhitena karmaṇā ārādhyate ārādhita ḥ ca mama ātma aparokṣyam sādhayiṣyati iti mayi arpita manaḥ buddhiḥ ya evaṃbhūtaḥ mad bhaktaḥ evam karma yogena mām bhajamānaḥ yaḥ sa me priyaḥ yasmāt karma niṣṭhāt puruṣān nimitta bhūtāl lokaḥ na udvijate yaḥ loka udvega karam karma kiñcid api na karoti iti arthaḥ lokāt ca nimitta bhūtāt yaḥ na udvijate yam uddiśya sarva lokaḥ na udvega karam karma karoti sarva avirodhi tva niścayāt ata eva kañcana prati harṣeṇa kañcana prati amarṣeṇa kañcana prati bhayena kañcana prati udvegena mukta h evaṃbhūtaḥ yaḥ saḥ api mama priyaḥ anapekṣaḥ ātma vyatirikte kṛtsne vastuni anapekṣaḥ śuciḥ śāstra vihita dravya vardhita kāyaḥ dakṣaḥ śāstrīya kriyā upādāna samarthaḥ anyatra udāsīnaḥ gana vyathaḥ śāstrīya kriyā nirvṛttau avarjanīya śīta uṣṇa puruṣa sparśa ādi duḥkheṣu vyathā rahitaḥ sarva ārambha parityāgī śāstrīya vyatirikta sarva karma ārambha parityāgī ya evaṃbhūtaḥ mad bhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥ yaḥ na hṛṣyati yad manuṣyāṇām harṣa nimittam priya jātam tad prāpya yaḥ karma yogī na hṛṣyati yad ca apriyam tad prāpya na dveṣṭi yad ca manuṣyāṇām śoka nimittam bhāryā putra vitta kṣaya ādikam tad prāpya na śocati tathāvidham aprāptam ca na kāṅkṣati śubha aśubha parityāgī pāpavat  puṇyasya api bandha hetu tva aviśeṣāt ubhaya parityāgī ya evaṃbhūtaḥ bhaktimān sa me priyaḥ tulya nindā stutiḥ maunī saṃtuṣṭaḥ yena kenacid aniketaḥ sthira matiḥ bhaktimān me priyaḥ naraḥ adveṣṭā sarva bhūtānām  ityādinā śatru mitra ādiṣu dveṣa ādi rahita tvam uktam atra teṣu sannihiteṣu api sama citta tvam tataḥ api atiriktaḥ viśeṣa ucyate ātmani sthiram ati tvena niketana ādiṣu asakta iti aniketaḥ tataḥ eva māna avamāna ādiṣu api samaḥ ya evaṃbhūtaḥ bhaktimān sa me priyaḥ dharmyam ca amṛtam ca iti dharmya amṛtam ye tu prāpya samam prāpakam bhakti yogam yathā uktam mayi āveśya manaḥ ye mām ityādinā uktena prakāreṇa upāsate te bhaktāḥ atitarām mama priyāḥ idam śarīram devaḥ aham manuṣyaḥ aham sthūlaḥ aham kṛśaḥ aham iti ātmanaḥ bhoktrā saha sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīyamānam bhoktuḥ ātmanaḥ artha antara bhūtasya bhoga kṣetram iti śarīra yāthātmya vidbhiḥ abhidhīyate etad avayavaśaḥ saṃghāta rūpeṇa ca idam aham vedmi iti yaḥ vetti tam vedya bhūtāt asmāt veditṛ tvena artha antara bhūtam kṣetrajña iti tad vidaḥ ātma yāthātmya vidaḥ prāhuḥ yadi api deha vyatirikta ghaṭa ādi artha anusandhāna velāyām deva u aham manuṣyaḥ aham ghaṭa ādikam jānāmi iti deha sāmānā adhikaraṇyena jñātāram ātmānam anusandhatte tathā api deha anubhava velāyām deham api ghaṭa ādikam iva idam aham vedmi iti vedya tayā veditā anubhavati iti vedituḥ ātmanaḥ vedya tayā śarīram api ghaṭa ādivat  artha antara bhūtam tathā ghaṭa ādeḥ iva vedya bhūtāc charīrāt api veditā kṣetrajñaḥ artha antara bhūtaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyena pratīti ḥ tu vastutaḥ śarīrasya gaḥ tva ādivat  atma viśeṣaṇa tā eka svabhāvatayā tad apṛthak siddheḥ upapannā tatra vedituḥ asādhāraṇa ākārasya cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇā viṣaya tvāt yoga saṃskṛta manaḥ viṣaya tvāt ca prakṛti sannidhānāt eva mūḍhāḥ prakṛti ākāram eva veditāram paśyanti tathā ca vakṣyati utkrāmantam sthitam vā api bhuñjānam vā guṇa anvitam vimūḍhā na anupaśyanti paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣaḥ iti deva manuṣya ādi sarva kṣetreṣu veditṛ tva ākāram kṣetrajñam ca mām viddhi mad ātmakam viddhi kṣetrajñam ca api iti api śabdāt kṣetram api mām viddhi iti uktam iti gamyate yathā kṣetram kṣetrajña viśeṣaṇa tā eka svabhāvatayā tad apṛthak siddheḥ tad sāmāna adhikaraṇyena eva nirdeśyam tathā kṣetram kṣetrajñam ca mad viśeṣaṇa tā eka svabhāva tayā mada pṛthak siddheḥ mad sāmāna adhikaraṇyena eva nirdeśyau viddhi pṛthivī ādi saṃghāta rūpasya kṣetrasya kṣetrajñasya ca bhagavat śarīra tā eka svarūpa tayā bhagavat ātmaka tvam śrutayaḥ vadanti yaḥ pṛthivyām tiṣṭhan pṛthivyāḥ antaraḥ yam pṛthivī na veda yasya pṛthivī śarīram yaḥ pṛthivīm antaraḥ yamayati sa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ iti ārabhya ya ātmani tiṣṭhan ātmanaḥ antaraḥ yam ātmā na veda yasya ātmā śarīram ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati sa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ iti ādyāḥ idam eva antaryāmi tayā sarva kṣetrajñānām ātma tvena avasthānam bhagavataḥ tad sāmāna adhikaraṇyena vyapadeśa hetuḥ aham ātmā guḍākeśa sarva bhūta āśaya sthitaḥ  na tad asti vinā yad syāt mayā bhūtam carācaram  viṣṭabhya aham idam kṛtsnam eka aṃśena sthitaḥ jagat iti purastād upariṣṭāt ca abhidhāya madhye sāmānādhikaraṇyena vyapadiśati ādityānām aham viṣṇuḥ ityādinā yad idam kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ viveka viṣayam tayoḥ mad ātmaka tva viṣayam ca jñānam uktam tad eva upādeyam jñānam iti mama matam kecid āhuḥ kṣetrajñam ca api mām viddhi iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena ekatvam avagamyate tataḥ ca īśvarasya eva sataḥ ajñānāt kṣetrajña tvam iva bhavati iti abhyupagantavyam tad nivṛtti arthaḥ ca ayam ekatva upadeśaḥ anena ca āptatama bhagavat upadeśena rajjuḥ eṣā na sarpaḥ iti āpta upadeśena sarpa tva bhrama nivṛttivat  kṣetrajña tva bhramaḥ nivartate iti te praṣṭavyāḥ ayam upadeṣṭā bhagavān vāsudevaḥ parameśvaraḥ kim ātma yāthātmya sākṣātkāreṇa nivṛtta ajñānaḥ uta na iti nivṛtta ajñānaḥ ced nirviśeṣa cit mātra eka svarūpe ātmani anya tad rūpa adhyāsa asaṃbhāvanayā kaunteya ādi bheda darśanam tān praty upadeśa ādi vyāpārāḥ ca na saṃbhavanti atha ātma sākṣātkāra abhāvāt anivṛtta ajñānaḥ na tarhi ajña tvāt eva ātma jñāna upadeśa saṃbhavaḥ upadekṣyanti te jñānam jñāninaḥ tattva darśinaḥ iti hi uktam ata evam ādivādā anākalita śruti smṛti itihāsa purāṇa nyāyasva vāc virodhaiḥ ajñānibhiḥ jagat mohanāya pravartitā iti anādaraṇīyāḥ atra idam tattvam acit vastunaḥ cit vastunaḥ parasya ca brahmaṇaḥ bhogya tvena bhoktṛ tvena ceśitṛ tvena ca svarūpa vivekam āhuḥ kāścana śrutayaḥ asmān māyī sṛjate viśvam etad tasmin  ca anyaḥ māyayā sanniruddhaḥ  māyām tu prakṛtim vidyān māyinam tu maheśvaraṃ  kṣaram pradhānam amṛta akṣaram haraḥ kṣara ātmānau  īśate deva ekaḥ amṛta akṣaram haraḥ iti bhoktā nirdiśyate pradhānam ātmanaḥ bhogya tvena harati iti haraḥ sa kāraṇam karaṇa adhipa adhipaḥ na ca asya kaściñ janitā na ca adhipaḥ  pradhāna kṣetrajñapatiḥ guṇa īśaḥ  patim viśvasya ātma īśvaram śāśvatam śivam acyutam  jñā ājñau dvau  ajau  īśani īśau  nityaḥ nityānām cetanaḥ cetanānām ekaḥ bahūnām yaḥ vidadhāti kāmān  bhoktā bhogyam preritāram ca matvā  pṛthak ātmānam preritāram ca matvā juṣṭaḥ tataḥ tena amṛta tvam eti  tayoḥ anyaḥ pippalam svāt v atty anaśnan  anyaḥ abhicākaśīti  ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām bahvīm prajām janayantīm sarūpām ajaḥ hi ekaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ anuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ anyaḥ ityādyāḥ atra api ahaṅkāra iti iyam me bhinnā prakṛtiḥ aṣṭadhā aparā iyam itaḥ tu anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām jīva bhūtāṃ  sarva bhūtāni kauntteya prakṛtim yānti māmikām kalpa kṣaye punar tāni kalpa ādau visṛjāmi aham tad kṣetram yad ca yad dravyam yādṛḥ ca yeṣām āśraya bhūtam yad vikāri ye ca asya vikārāḥ yataḥ ca yataḥ hetoḥ idam utpannam yasmai prayojanāya utpannam iti arthaḥ yad yad svarūpam ca idam sa ca yaḥ sa ca kṣetrajñaḥ yaḥ yad svarūpaḥ yad prabhāvaḥ ca ye ca asya prabhāvāḥ tad sarvam samāsena saṃkṣepeṇa mattaḥ śṛṇu tad idam kṣetra kṣetrajñayāthātmyam ṛṣibhiḥ parāśara ādibhiḥ bahudhā bahu prakāram gītam aham tvam ca tathā anye ca bhūtaiḥ uhyāma pārthiva guṇa pravāha patitaḥ bhūta vargaḥ api yāti ayam icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham saṃghāta ḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ etad kṣetram samāsena sa vikāram udāhṛtam mahābhūtāni ahaṃkāraḥ buddhiḥ avyaktam eva ca iti kṣetra ārambhaka dravyāṇi pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśāḥ mahābhūtāni ahaṃkāraḥ bhūtādiḥ buddhiḥ mahān avyaktam prakṛtiḥ indriyāṇi daśa ekam ca pañca ca indriya gocarā iti kṣetra āśritāni tattvāni śrotra tvac cakṣuḥ jihvā ghrāṇāni pañca jñāna indriyāṇi vāc pāṇi pāda pāyu upasthāni pañca karmendriyāṇi iti tāni daśa ekam iti manaḥ indriya gocarāḥ ca pañca śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāḥ icchā dveṣaḥ sukham duḥkham iti kṣetra kāryāṇi kṣetra vikārā ucyante yadi api icchā dveṣa sukha duḥkhāni ātma dharma bhūtāni tathā api ātmanaḥ kṣetra saṃbandha prayuktāni iti kṣetra kārya tayā kṣetra vikārā ucyante teṣām puruṣa dharma tvam puruṣaḥ sukha duḥkhānām bhoktṛ tve hetuḥ ucyate iti vakṣyate saṃghāta ḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ ādhṛtiḥ ādhāraḥ sukha duḥkhe bhuñjānasya bhoga apavargau sādhayataḥ ca cetanasya ādhāratayā utpannaḥ bhūta saṃghātaḥ prakṛti ādi pṛthivī anta dravya ārabdham indriya āśraya bhūtam icchā dveṣa sukha duḥkha vikāri bhūta saṃghāta rūpam cetana sukha duḥkha upabhoga ādhāra tva prayojanam kṣetram iti uktam bhavati etad kṣetram samāsena saṃkṣepeṇa sa kivāram sa kāryam udāhṛtam amāni tvam utkṛṣṭa janeṣu avadhīraṇā rahita tvam adambhi tvam dhārmika tva yaśaḥ prayojana tayā dharma anuṣṭhānam dambhaḥ tad rahita tvam ahiṃsā vāc manaḥ kāyaiḥ para pīḍā rahita tvam kṣāntiḥ paraiḥ pīḍyamānasya api tān prati avikṛta citta tvam ārjavam parān prati vāc manaḥ kāya prabhṛtīnām eka rūpa tā ācārya upāsanam ātma jñāna pradāyini ācārye praṇipāta paripraśna sevā ādi nirata tvam śaucam ātma jñāna tad sādhana yogya tā manaḥ vāc kāya gatā śāstra siddhā stairyam adhyātma śāstra udite arthe niścala tvam ātma vinigrahaḥ ātma svarūpa vyatirikta viṣayebhyaḥ manasaḥ nivartanam indriya artheṣu vairāgyam ātma vyatirikteṣu viṣayeṣu sadoṣa tā anusaṃdhānena udvejanam anahaṃkāraḥ anātmani dehe ātma abhimāna rahita tvam pradarśana artham idam anātmīyeṣu ātmīya abhimāna rahita tvam ca vivakṣitam janma mṛtyu jarā vyādhi duḥkha doṣa anudarśanam sa śarīra tve janma mṛtyu jarā vyādhi duḥkha rūpasya doṣasya āvarjanīyatva anusaṃdhānam asaktiḥ ātma vyatirikta parigraheṣu saṅga rahita tvam anabhiṣvaṅgaḥ putra dāra gṛha ādiṣu teṣu śāstrīya karma upakaraṇa tva atirekeṇa śleṣa rahita tvam saṃkalpa prabhaveṣu iṣṭa aniṣṭa upa nipāteṣu harṣa udvega rahita tvam mayi sarva īśvare ca aikāntya yogena sthirā bhaktiḥ jana varjita deśa vāsi tvam jana saṃsadi ca aprītiḥ ātmani jñānam adhyātma jñānam tad niṣṭha tvam tattva jñāna artha cintanam tattva jñāna prayojanam yad cintanam tad nirata tvam iti arthaḥ jñāyate anena ātmā iti jñānam ātma jñāna sādhanam iti arthaḥ kṣetra saṃbandhinaḥ puruṣasya āmāni tva ādikam uktam guṇa bṛnham eva ātma jñāna upayogi etad vyatiriktam sarvam kṣetra kāryam ātma jñāna virodhi iti ajñānam amāni tva ādibhiḥ sādhanaiḥ jñeyam prāpyam yad pratyagātma svarūpam tad pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā janma jarā maraṇa ādi prākṛta dharma rahitam amṛtam ātmānam prāpnoti ādiḥ yasya na vidyate tad anādi asya hi pratyak ātmana utpattiḥ na vidyate tataḥ eva antaḥ na vidyate śrutiḥ ca na jāyate mriyate vā vipaścit iti mad param aham paraḥ yasya tad mad param itaḥ tu anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām jīva bhūtām iti hi uktam bhagavat śarīra tayā bhagavat śeṣa tā eka rasam hi ātma svarūpam tathā ca śrutiḥ ya ātmani tiṣṭhan ātmanaḥ antaraḥ yam atmā na veda yasya ātmā śarīram ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati iti tathā sa kāraṇam karaṇa adhipa adhipaḥ na ca asya kaściñ janitā na ca adhipaḥ  pradhāna kṣetrajñapatiḥ guṇa īśaḥ iti ādikā brahma bṛhat tva guṇa yogi śarīra ādeḥ artha antara bhūtam svataḥ śarīra ādibhiḥ pariccheda rahitam kṣetrajña tattvam iti arthaḥ sa ca ānantyāya kalpate iti hi śrūyate śarīra paricchinna tvam aṇu tvam ca asya karma kṛtam karma bandhān muktasya ānantyam ātmani api brahma śabdaḥ prayujyate sa guṇān samatītya etān brahma bhūyāya kalpate brahmaṇaḥ hi pratiṣṭhā aham amṛtasya avyayasya ca  brahma bhūtaḥ prasanna ātmā na śocati na kāṅkṣati samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu mad bhaktim labhate parām sarvataḥ pāṇi pādam tad pariśuddha ātma svarūpam sarvataḥ pāṇi pāda kārya śaktam tathā sarvataḥ akṣi śiraḥ mukham sarvataḥ śrutimat sarvataḥ cakṣuḥ ādi kārya kṛt pāṇi pādaḥ javanaḥ grahītā paśyati acakṣuḥ sa śṛṇoti akarṇaḥ iti parasya brahmaṇaḥ apāṇi pādasya api sarvataḥ pāṇi pāda ādi kārya kṛt tvam śrūyate pratyak ātmanaḥ api pariśuddhasya tad sāmya āpattyā sarvataḥ pāṇi pāda ādi kārya kṛt tvam śruti siddham eva tadā vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti hi śrūyate idam jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ iti ca vakṣyate loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati loke yad vastu jātam tad sarvam vyāpya tiṣṭhati pariśuddha svarūpam deśa ādi pariccheda rahita tayā sarva gatam iti arthaḥ sarva indriya guṇa ābhāsam sarva indriya guṇaiḥ ābhāsaḥ yasya tad sarva indriya ābhāsam indriya guṇā indriya vṛttayaḥ indriya vṛttibhiḥ api viṣayān jñatum samartham iti arthaḥ svabhāvataḥ sarva indriya vivarjitam vinā eva indriya vṛttibhiḥ svata eva sarvam jānāti iti arthaḥ asaktam svabhāvataḥ deva ādi deha saṅga rahitam sarva bhṛc ca eva deva ādi sarva deha bharaṇa samartham ca sa ekadhā bhavati tridhā bhavati ityādi śruteḥ nirguṇam tathā svabhāvataḥ sattva ādi guṇa rahitam guṇa bhoktṛ ca sattva ādīnām guṇānām bhoga samartham ca pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni parityajya aśarīraḥ bahiḥ vartate teṣām antar ca vartate jakṣat krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ strībhiḥ vā yānaiḥ vā ityādi śruti siddha svacchanda vṛttiṣu acaram caram eva ca svabhāvataḥ acaram caram ca dehi tve sūkṣma tvāt tad avijñeyam evam sarva śakti yuktam sarvajñām tad atma tattvam asmin kṣetre vartamānam api ati sūkṣma tvāt dehāt pṛthaktvena saṃsāribhiḥ avijñeyam dūra stham ca antike ca tad amāni tvādi ukta guṇa rahitānām viparīta guṇāṇām puṃsām sva dehe vartamānam api ati dūra stham tathā amāni tva ādi guṇa upetānām tad eva antike vartate deva manuṣya ādi bhūteṣu sarvatra sthitam ātma vastu veditṛ tva eka ākāra tayā avibhaktam aviduṣām deva ādi ākāreṇa ayam devaḥ manuṣyaḥ iti vibhaktam iva ca sthitam devaḥ aham manuṣyaḥ aham iti deha sāmānā adhikaraṇyena anusandhīyamānam api veditṛ tvena dehāt artha antara bhūtam jñātum śakyam iti ādau  uktam eva etad yaḥ vetti iti idānīm prakāra antaraiḥ ca jñātum śakyam iti āja bhūta bhartṛ ca iti bhūtānām pṛthivī ādīnām deha rūpeṇa saṃhatānām yad bhartṛ tad bhartavyebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ artha antaram jñeyam artha antaram iti jñātum śakyam iti arthaḥ tathā grasiṣṇu anna ādīnām bhautikānām grasiṣṇu grasyamānebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ grasitṛ tvena artha antra bhūtam iti jñātum śakyam prabhaviṣṇu ca prabhava hetuḥ ca grastānām anna ādīnām ākāra antareṇa pariṇatānām prabha hetuḥ tebhyaḥ artha antaram iti jñātum śakyam iti arthaḥ mṛta śarīre grasana prabhava ādīnām adarśanān na bhūta saṃghāta rūpam kṣetram grasana prabhava bharaṇa hetuḥ iti niścīyate jyotiśām dīpa āditya maṇi prabhṛtīnām api tad eva jyotiḥ prakāśakam dīpāt itya ādīnām api ātma prabhā rūpam jñānam eva prakāśakam dīpa ādayaḥ tu viṣaya indriya sannikarṣa virodhi saṃtama sa nirasana mātram kurvate tāvan mātreṇa teṣām prakāśaka tvam tamasaḥ param ucyate tamaḥ śabdaḥ sūkṣma avastha prakṛti vacanaḥ prakṛteḥ param ucyata iti arthaḥ ataḥ jñānam jñeyam jñāna eka ākāram iti jñeyam tad ca jñāna gamyam amāni tva ādibhiḥ jñāna sādhanaiḥ uktaiḥ prāpyam iti arthaḥ hṛdi sarvasya viṣṭhitam sarvasya manuṣya ādeḥ hṛdi viśeṣaṇa avasthitam sannihitam evam mahābhūtāni ahaṅkāraḥ ityādinā saṃghāta ḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ  iti antena kṣetra tattvam samāsena uktam amāni tvam ityādinā tattva jñāna artha cintanam iti antena jñātavyasya ātma tattvasya jñāna sādhanam uktam ana ādi mad param ityādinā hṛdi sarvasya viṣṭhitam iti antena jñeyasya kṣetrajñasya yāthātmyam ca saṃkṣepeṇa uktam mad bhaktaḥ etad kṣetrayāthātmyam kṣetrād vivikta ātma svarūpa prāpti upāya yāthātmyam kṣetrajñayāthātmyam ca vijñāya mad bhāvāya upapadyate mama yaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ asaṃsāri tvam asaṃsāri tva prāptaye upapannaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ prakṛti puruṣau ubhau anyonya saṃsṛṣṭau anādī iti viddhi bandha hetu bhūtān vikārān icchā dveṣa ādīn amāni tva ādikāṃḥ ca guṇām mokṣa hetu bhūtān prakṛti saṃbhavān viddhi puruṣeṇa saṃsṛṣṭā iyam anādi kāla pravṛttā kṣetra ākāra pariṇātā prakṛtiḥ sva vikāraiḥ icchā dveṣa ādibhiḥ puruṣasya bandhu hetuḥ bhavati sā eva āmāni tva ādibhiḥ sva vikāraiḥ puruṣasya apavarga hetuḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ kāryam śarīram kāraṇāni jñāna karma ātmakāni sa manaskāni indriyāṇi teṣām kriyā kāri tve puruṣa adhiṣṭhitā prakṛtiḥ eva hetuḥ puruṣa adhiṣṭhita kṣetra ākāra pariṇata prakṛti āśrayāḥ bhoga sādhana bhūtāḥ kriyā iti arthaḥ puruṣasya adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam eva tad apekṣayā kartā śāstra arthavat tva at iti ādikam uktam śarīra adhiṣṭhāna prayatna hetu tvam eva hi puruṣasya kartṛ tvam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭaḥ puruṣaḥ sukha duḥkhānām bhoktṛ tve hetuḥ sukha duḥkha anubhava āśraya iti arthaḥ pūrva pūrva prakṛti pariṇāma rūpa deva manuṣya ādi yoni viśeṣeṣu sthitaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ tad tad yoni prayukta sattva ādi guṇa mayeṣu sukha duḥkha ādiṣu saktaḥ tad sādhana bhūteṣu puṇya pāpa karmasu pravartate tataḥ tad puṇya pāpa phala anubhavāya sat asat yoniṣu sādhu asādhuṣu yoniṣu jāyate tataḥ ca karma ārabhate tataḥ jāyate yāvat amāni tva ādikān ātma prāpti sādhana bhūtān guṇān sevate tāvat eva saṃsarati tad idam uktam kāraṇam guṇa saṅgaḥ asya sat asat yoni janmasu iti asmin dehe avasthitaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ deha pravṛtti anuguṇa saṅkalpa ādi rūpeṇa dehasya upadraṣṭā anumantā ca bhavati tathā dehasya bhartā ca bhavati tathā deha pravṛtti janita sukha duḥkhayoḥ bhoktā ca bhavati evam deha niyamanena deha bharaṇena deha śeṣi tvena ca deha indriya manāṃsi prati maheśvaraḥ bhavati tathā ca vakṣyate śarīram yad avāpnoti yad ca api utkrāmati īśvaraḥ gṛhītvā etāni saṃyāti vāyuḥ gandhān iva āśayāt enam ukta svabhāvam puruṣam ukta svabhāvām ca prakṛtim vakṣyamāṇa svabhāva yuktaiḥ sattva ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ saha yaḥ vetti yathāvat vivekena jānāti sa sarvathā deva manuṣya ādi deheṣu atimātra kliṣṭa prakāreṇa vartamānaḥ api na bhūyaḥ abhijāyate na bhūyaḥ prakṛtyā saṃsargam arhati aparicchinna jña anala kaṣaṇam apahata pāpmānam ātmānam tad deha avasāna samaye prāpnoti iti arthaḥ kecid niṣpanna yogāḥ ātmani śarīre avasthitam ātmānam ātmanā manasā dhyānena yogena paśyanti anye ca aniṣpanna yogāḥ sāṃkhyena yogena jñāna yogena yoga yogyam manaḥ kṛtvā ātmānam paśyanti apare jñāna yogān adhikāriṇaḥ tad adhikāriṇaḥ ca sukara upāya saktāḥ vyapadeśya āḥ ca karma yogena antargata jñānena manasaḥ yoga yogya tām āpādya ātmānam paśyanti anye tu karma yoga ādiṣu ātma avalokana sādhaneṣu anadhikṛtāḥ anyebhyaḥ tattva darśibhyaḥ jñānibhyaḥ śrutvā karma yoga ādibhiḥ ātmānam upāsate te api ātma darśanena mṛtyum atitaranti ye śruti parāyaṇāḥ śravaṇa mātra niṣṭhāḥ ete ca śravaṇa niṣṭhāḥ pūta pāpāḥ krameṇa karma yoga ādikam ārabhya atitaranti eva mṛtyum api śabda āt ca pūrva bhedaḥ avagamyate yāvat sthāvara jaṅgama ātmanā sattvam jāyate tāvat kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ itaretara saṃyogāt eva jāyate saṃyuktam eva jāyate na tu itaretara viyuktam iti arthaḥ evam itaretara yukteṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu deva ādi viṣama ākārāt viyuktam tatra tatra tad tad deha indriya manāṃsi prati parameśvara tvena sthitam ātmānam jñātṛ tvena samāna ākāram teṣu deha ādiṣu vinaśyatsu vināśānarha svabhāvena avinaśyantam yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati sa ātmānam yathāvat avasthitam paśyati yaḥ tu deva ādi viṣama ākāreṇa ātmānam api viṣama ākāram janma vināśa ādi yuktam ca paśyati sa nityam eva saṃsarati iti abhiprāyaḥ sarvatra deva ādi śarīreṣu tad tad śeṣi tvena ādhāra tayā viyantṛ tayā ca sthitam īśvaram ātmānam deva ādi viṣama ākāra viyuktam jñāna eka ākāra tayā samam paśyan ātmanā manasā svam ātmānam na hinasti rakṣati saṃsārān mocayati tataḥ tasmāt jñātṛ tayā sarvatra samāna ākāra darśanāt parām gatim yāti gamyata iti gatiḥ param gantavyam yathāvat avasthitam ātmānam prāpnoti deva ādi ākāra yukta tayā sarvatra viṣamam ātmānam paśyan ātmānam hinasti bhava jaladhi madhye prakṣipati sarvāṇi karmāṇi kārya kāraṇa kartṛ tve hetuḥ prakṛtiḥ ucyate iti pūrva ukta rītyā prakṛtyā kriyamāṇāni iti yaḥ paśyati tathā ātmānam jñāna ākāram akartāram ca yaḥ paśyati tasya prakṛti saṃyoga ḥ tad adhiṣṭhānam tad janya sukha duḥkha anubhavaḥ ca karma rūpa ajñāna kṛtāni iti ca yaḥ paśyati sa ātmānam yathāvat avasthitam paśyati prakṛti puruṣa tattva dvaya ātmakeṣu deva ādiṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu satsu teṣām deva tva manuṣya tva hrasva tva dīrgha tva ādi pṛthagbhāvam ekastham eka tattva stham prakṛti stham yadā paśyati na ātma stham tataḥ eva prakṛtita eva uttarottara putra pautra ādi bheda vistāram ca yadā paśyati tadā eva brahma saṃpadyate anavacchinnam jñāna eka ākāram ātmānam prāpnoti iti arthaḥ ayam paramātmā dehān niṣkṛṣya sva svabhāvena nirūpitaḥ śarīra sthaḥ api anādi tvāt anārabhya tvāt avyayaḥ vyaya rahitaḥ nirguṇa tvāt sattva ādi guṇa rahita tvān na karoti na lipyate deha svabhāvaiḥ na lipyate yathā ākāśam sarva gatam api sarvaiḥ vastubhiḥ saṃyuktam api saukṣmyāt sarva vastu svabhāvaiḥ na lipyate tathā ātmā ati saukṣmyāt sarvatra deva manuṣya ādau dehe avasthitaḥ api tad tad deha svabhāvaiḥ na lipyate yathā eka ādityaḥ svayā prabhayā kṛtsnam imam lokam prakāśayati tathā kṣetram api kṣetrī mama idam kṣetram īdṛśam iti kṛtsnam bahiḥ antar ca āpādatala mastakam svakīyena jñānena prakāśayati ataḥ prakāśya al lokāt prakāśaka āt ityavat  veditṛ tvena vedya bhūtāt asmāt kṣetrād atyanta vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam ukta lakṣaṇa ātmā iti arthaḥ evam uktena prakāreṇa kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ antaram viśeṣam viveka viṣaya jñāna ākhyena cakṣuṣā ye viduḥ bhūta prakṛti mokṣam ca te param yānti nirmukta bandham ātmānam prāpnuvanti mokṣyate anena iti mokṣaḥ amāni tva ādikam mokṣa sādhanam iti arthaḥ kṣetra kṣetrajñayoḥ viveka viṣayeṇa uktena jñānena tayoḥ vivekam viditvā bhūta ākāra pariṇata prakṛti mokṣa upāyam amāni tva ādikam ca āgamya ya ācaranti te nirmukta bandhāḥ svena rūpeṇa avasthitam anavacchinna jñāna lakṣaṇam ātmānam prāpnuvanti iti arthaḥ param pūrva uktāt anyat prakṛti puruṣa antargatam eva sattva ādi guṇa viṣayam jñānam bhūyaḥ pravakṣyāmi tad ca jñānam sarveṣām prakṛti puruṣa viṣaya jñānānām uttamam yaj jñānam jñātvā sarve munayaḥ tad manana śīlāḥ itaḥ saṃsāra bandhāt parām siddhim gatāḥ parām pariśuddha ātma svarūpa prāpti rūpām siddhim avāptāḥ idam vakṣyamāṇam jñānam upaśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ mad sāmyam prāptāḥ sarge api na upajāyante na sṛji karmatām bhajante pralaye na vyathanti ca na ca saṃhṛti karmatām kṛtsnasya jagataḥ yoni bhūtam mama mahat brahma yad tasmin garbham dadhāmi aham bhūmiḥ āpaḥ analaḥ vāyuḥ kham manaḥ buddhiḥ eva ca ahaṅkāra iti iyam me bhinnā prakṛtiḥ aṣṭadhā sarvāsu deva gandharva yakṣa rākṣasa manuṣya paśu mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpa ādiṣu yoniṣu tad tad mūrtayaḥ yāḥ saṃbhavanti jāyante tāsām brahma mahat yoniḥ kāraṇam mayā saṃyojita cetana vargā mahat ādi viśeṣa anta avasthā prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam iti arthaḥ aham bīja pradaḥ pitā tatra tatra ca tad tad karma anuguṇyena cetana vargasya saṃyojakaḥ ca aham iti arthaḥ sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi trayaḥ guṇāḥ prakṛteḥ svarūpa anubandhinaḥ svabhāva viśeṣāḥ prakāśa ādi kārya eka nirūpaṇīyāḥ prakṛti avasthāyām anudbhūtāḥ tad vikāreṣu mahat ādiṣu udbhūtāḥ mahat ādi viśeṣa antaiḥ ārabdha deva manuṣya ādi deha saṃbandhinam enam dehinam avyayam svataḥ guṇa saṃbandhān arham dehe vartamānam nibadhnanti dehe vartamāna tva upādhinā nibadhnanti iti arthaḥ tatra sattva rajaḥ tamaḥ tu sattvasya svarūpam īdṛśam nirmala tvāt prakāśakam prakāśa sukha āvaraṇa svabhāva rahita tā nirmala tvam prakāśa sukha janana ekānta svabhāva tayā prakāśa sukha hetu bhūtam iti arthaḥ prakāśaḥ vastu yātha ātmya avabodhaḥ anāmayam āmaya ākhyam kāryam na vidyata iti anāmayam aroga tā hetuḥ iti arthaḥ eṣa sattva ākhyaḥ guṇa u dehinam enam sukha saṅgena jñāna saṅgena ca badhnāti puruṣasya sukha saṅgam jñāna saṅgam ca janayati iti arthaḥ jñāna sukhayoḥ saṅge hi jāte tad sādhaneṣu laukika vaidikeṣu pravartate tataḥ ca tad phala anubhava sādhana bhūtāsu yoniṣu jāyata iti sattvam sukha jñāna saṅga dvāreṇa puruṣam badhnāti jñāna sukha jananam punar api tayoḥ saṅga jananam ca sattvam iti uktam bhavati rajaḥ rāga ātmakam rāga hetu bhūtam rāgaḥ yoṣit puruṣayoḥ anya anya spṛhā tṛṇa āsaṅga samudbhavam tṛṣṇā saṅgayoḥ udbhava sthānam tṛṣṇā saṅga hetu bhūtam iti arthaḥ tṛṣṇā śabda ādi sarva viṣaya spṛhā saṅgaḥ putra mitra ādiṣu saṃbandhiṣu saṃśleṣa spṛhā tad rajaḥ dehinam karmasu kriyāsu spṛhā janana dvāreṇa nibadhnāti kriyāsu hi spṛhayā yāḥ kriyā ārabhate dehī tāḥ ca puṇya pāpa rūpā iti tad phala anubhava sādhana bhūtāsu yoniṣu janma hetavaḥ bhavanti ataḥ karma saṅga dvāreṇa rajaḥ dehinam nibadhnāti tad evam rajaḥ rāga tṛṣṇā saṅga hetuḥ karma saṅga hetuḥ ca iti uktam bhavati jñānāt anyat iha ajñānam abhipretam jñānam vastu yathātmya avabodhaḥ tasmāt anyat tad viparyaya jñānam tamaḥ tu vastu yāthātmya via parīta viṣaya jñāna jam mohanam sarva dehinām mohaḥ viparyaya jñānam viparyaya jñāna hetuḥ iti arthaḥ tad tamaḥ pramāda ālasya nidrā hetu tayā tad dvāreṇa dehinam nibadhnāti pramādaḥ kartavyāt karmaṇaḥ anyatra pravṛtti hetu bhūtam anavadhānam ālasyam karmasu anārambha svabhāvaḥ stabdha tā iti yāvat puruṣasya indriya pravartana śrāntyā sarva indriya pravartana uparatiḥ nidrā tatra bāhya indriya pravartana uparamaḥ svapnaḥ manasaḥ api uparatiḥ suṣuptiḥ sattvam sukha saṅga pradhānam rajaḥ karma saṅga pradhānam tamaḥ tu vastu yāthātmya jñānam āvṛtya viparīta jñāna hetu tayā kartavya viparīta pravṛtti saṅga pradhānam yadi api sattva āt yaḥ trayaḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭa ātma svarūpa anubandhinaḥ tathā api prācīna karma vaśāt deha api āyana bhūta āhāra vaiṣamyāt ca sattva ādayaḥ paraspara samudbhava abhibhava rūpeṇa vartante rajaḥ tamasī kadācid abhibhūya sattvam udriktam vartate tathā tamaḥ sattve abhibhūya rajaḥ kadācid kadācid ca rajaḥ sattve abhibhūya tamaḥ % sarveṣu cakṣuḥ ādiṣu jñāna dvāreṣu yadā vastu yāthātmya prakāśe jñānam upajāyate tadā tasmin dehe sattvam pravṛddham iti vidyāt yam saṃsāra ākhyam aśvatham ūrdhva mūlam adhaḥ śākham avyayam prāhuḥ śrutayaḥ u ūrdhva mūlaḥ avākcha ākha eṣaḥ aśvattha ḥ sanātanaḥ  u ūrdhva mūlam avāk chākham vṛkṣam yaḥ veda saṃprti ityādyāḥ sapta loka upari niviṣṭa catur mukha ādi tvena tasya ūrdhva mūla tvam pṛthivī nivāsi sakala nara paśu mṛga krimi kīṭa pataṅga sthāvara anta tayā adhaḥ śākha tvam asaṅga hetu bhūtāt samyak jñana udayāt pravāha rūpeṇa ācchedya tvena avyaya tvam yasya ca aśvatthasya chandāṃsi parṇāni āhuḥ chandāṃsi śrutayaḥ vāyavyam śvetam ālabheta bhūti kāmaḥ  ā aindrāgnam ekādaśa kapālam nirvapet prajā kāmaḥ ityādi śruti pratipāditaiḥ kāmya karmabhiḥ vardhate ayam saṃsāra vṛkṣa iti chandāṃsi eva asya parṇāni parṇaiḥ hi vṛkṣaḥ vardhate yaḥ tam evaṃbhūtam aśvattham veda sa veda vid vedaḥ hi saṃsāra vṛkṣa cheda upāyam vadati chedya vṛkṣa svarūpa jñānam chedana upāya jñana upayogī iti veda vid iti ucyate brahma loka mūlasya asya vṛkṣasya manuṣya agrasya adhaḥ manuṣya loke mūlāni anusantatāni tāni ca karma anubandhīni karmāṇi eva anubandhīni mūlāni adhaḥ manuṣya loke ca bhavanti iti arthaḥ manuṣya tva avasthāyām kṛtaiḥ hi karmabhiḥ adhaḥ manuṣya paśu ādayaḥ ūrdhvam ca deva ādayaḥ bhavanti tataḥ padam tad parimārgitavyam yasmin gatā na nivartanti bhūyaḥ enam ukta prakāram su virūḍha mūlam suṣṭhu vividham rūḍha mūlam aśvattham samyak jñāna mūlena dṛḍhena guṇa maya bhoga asaṃga ākhyena śastreṇa chitvā tataḥ viṣaya asaṃgāt dhetoḥ tad padam parimārgitavyam anveṣaṇīyam yasmin gatā bhūyaḥ na nivartante ajñāna ādi nivṛttaye tam eva ca ādyam kṛtsnasya ādi bhūtam mayā adhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaram  aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate  mattaḥ parataram na anyat kiñcid asti dhanañjaya iti ādiṣu uktam ādyam puruṣam eva śaraṇam prapadyet tam eva śaraṇam prapadyeta yataḥ yasmāt kṛtsnasya sraṣṭuḥ iyam guṇa maya bhoga saṅga pravṛttiḥ purāṇī purātanī prasṛtā uktam hi mayā etad pūrvam eva daivī hi eṣā guṇa mayī mam māyā dūratyayā mām eva ye prapadyante māyām etām taranti te iti prapadyeyataḥ pravṛttiḥ iti vā pāṭhaḥ tam eva ca ādyam puruṣam prpadya śaraṇam upagamya iyataḥ ajñāna nivṛtti ādeḥ kṛstnasya etasya sādhana bhūtāḥ pravṛttiḥ purāṇī purātanī praṛtā purātanānām mumukṣūṇām pravṛttiḥ purāṇī purātanā hi mumukṣavaḥ mām eva śaraṇam upagamya nirmukta bandha aḥ saṃjātā iti arthaḥ evam mām śaraṇam upagamya nirmāna mohāḥ nirgata an ātma ātma abhimāna rūpa mohāḥ jita saṅga doṣā jita guṇa maya bhoga saṅga ākhya doṣāḥ adhyātma nityāḥ ātmani yaj jñānam tad adhyātmam ātma jñāna niratāḥ vinivṛtta kāmāḥ vinivṛtta tad itara kāmāḥ sukha duḥkha sajñaiḥ dvandva aiḥ ca vimuktāḥ amūḍhāḥ ātma anātma svabhava jñāḥ tad avyayam padam gacchanti anavacchinna jñāna ākāram ātmānam yathā avasthitam prāpnuvanti mām śaraṇam upagatānām mad prasāda ādeḥ eva etāḥ sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ suśakāḥ siddhi paryantā bhavanti iti arthaḥ tad atma jyotiḥ na sūryaḥ bhāsayate na śaśāṅkaḥ na pāvakaḥ ca jñānam eva hi sarvasya prakāśakam bāhyāni tu jyotīṃṣi viṣaya indriya saṃbandha virodhita monirasana dvāreṇa upakārakāṇi asya ca prakāśakaḥ yogaḥ tad virodhi ca anādikarma tad nivartanam ca uktam bhagavat prapatti mūlam asaṅga ādi yad gatvā punar na nivartante tad paramam dhāma param jyotiḥ mama madīyam mad vibhūti bhūtaḥ mama aṃśa iti arthaḥ āditya ādīnām api prakāśaka tvena tasya parama tvam āditya ādīni hi jyotīṃṣi na jñāna jyotiṣaḥ prakāśakāni jñānam eva sarvasya prakāśakam ittham ukta svarūpaḥ sanātanaḥ mama aṃśa eva san kaścid anādi karma rūpa avidyā veṣṭitaḥ jīva bhūtaḥ jīva loke vartamānaḥ deva manuṣya ādi prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣa śarīra sthāni manaṣṣaṣṭhāni indriyāṇi karṣati kaścid ca pūrva uktena mārgeṇa asyā avidyāyāḥ muktaḥ svena rūpeṇa avatiṣṭhate jīva bhūta ḥ tu ati saṃkucita jñānāiśvaryaḥ karma labdha prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣa rūpa śarīra sthānām indriyāṇām manaṣṣaṣṭhānām īśvaraḥ tāni karma anuguṇam itaḥ tataḥ karṣati yad śarīram avāpnoti yamāc charīrāt utkrāmati tatra ayam indriyāṇām īśvaraḥ etāni indriyāṇi bhūta sūkṣmaiḥ saha gṛhītvā saṃyāti vāyuḥ gandhān iva āśayāt yathā vāyuḥ sraj candana kastūrikā ādyāśayāt tad sthānāt sūkṣma avayavaiḥ saha gandhān gṛhītvā anyatra saṃyāti tadvat iti arthaḥ etāni manaṣṣaṣṭhāni indriyāṇi adhiṣṭhāya sva sva viṣaya vṛtti anuguṇāni kṛtvā tān śabda ādīn viṣayān upasevate upabhuṅkte evam guṇa anvitam sattva ādi guṇa maya prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣa manuṣya tva ādi saṃsthāna piṇḍa saṃsṛṣṭam piṇḍa viśeṣāt utkrāmantam piṇḍa viśeṣe avathitam vā guṇa mayān viṣayān bhuñjānam vā kadācid api prakṛti pariṇāma viśeṣa manuṣya tva ādi piṇḍād vilakṣaṇam jñāna eka ākāram vimūḍhā na anupaśyanti vimūḍhāḥ manuṣya tva ādi piṇḍa ātma tva abhimāninaḥ jñāna cakṣuṣaḥ tu piṇḍa ātma viveka viṣaya jñānavantaḥ sarva avastham api enam vivikta ākāram eva paśyanti mad prapatti pūrvakam karma yoga ādiṣu yatamānāḥ taiḥ nirmala antaḥkaraṇā yoginaḥ yoga ākhyena cakṣuṣā ātmani śarīre avasthitam api śarīrāt viviktam svena rūpeṇa avasthitam enam paśyanti yatamānā api akṛtātmānaḥ mad prapatti virahiṇaḥ tataḥ eva asaṃskṛta manasaḥ tataḥ eva acetasaḥ ātma avalokana samartha cetaḥ rahitāḥ na enam paśyanti akhilasya jagataḥ bhāsakam eteṣām āditya ādīnām yad tejaḥ tad madīyam tejaḥ taiḥ taiḥ ārādhitena mayā tebhyaḥ dattam iti viddhi % aham pṛthivīm āviśya sarvāṇi bhūtāni ojasā mama apratihata sāmarthyena dhārayāmi tathā aham amṛta rasa maya ḥ somaḥ bhūtvā sarva oṣadhīḥ puṣṇāmi ahiṃsā satyam akrodha ḥ tyāgaḥ śāntiḥ apaiśunam dayā bhūteṣu aloluptvam mārdavam hrīḥ acāpalam tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucam adrohaḥ na ati mānitā bhavanti saṃpadam daivīm abhi jātasya bhārata iṣṭa aniṣṭa viyoga saṃyoga rūpasya duḥkhasya hetu darśana jam duḥkham bhayam tad nivṛttiḥ abhayam sattva saṃśuddhiḥ sattvasya antaḥkaraṇasya rajaḥ tamobhyām aspṛṣṭa tvam jñāna yoga vyavasthitiḥ prakṛti viyukta ātma svarūpa viveka niṣṭhā dānam nyāya arjita dhanasya pātre pratipādanam damaḥ manasaḥ viṣaya unmukhya nivṛtti saṃśīlanam yajñaḥ phala abhisandhirahita bhagavat ārādhana rūpa mahā yajña ādi anuṣṭhānam svādhyāyaḥ sa vibhūteḥ bhagavataḥ tad ārādhana prakārasya ca pratipādakaḥ kṛtsnaḥ veda iti anusandhāya veda abhyāsa niṣṭhā tapaḥ kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa dvādaśī upavāsa ādeḥ bhagavat prīṇana karma yogya tā āpādanasya karaṇam ārjavam manaḥ vāc kāya vṛttīnām eka niṣṭhatā pareṣu ahiṃsā para pīḍā varjanam satyam yathā dṛṣṭa artha gocara bhūta hita vākyam akrodhaḥ para pīḍā phala citta vikāra rahita tvam tyāgaḥ ātma hita pratyanīka parigraha vimocanam śāntiḥ indriyāṇām viṣaya prāvaṇya nirodha saṃśīlanam apaiśunam para anartha kara vākya nivedana ākaraṇam dayā bhūteṣu sarva bhūteṣu duḥkha asahiṣṇu tvam aloluptvam alolupa tvam alolutvam iti vā pāṭhaḥ viṣayeṣu nisspṛha tvam iti arthaḥ mārdavam akāṭhinyam sādhu jana saṃśleṣa arhatā iti arthaḥ hrīḥ akārya karaṇe vrīḍā acāpalam spṛhaṇīya viṣaya sannidhau acañcala tvam tejaḥ durjanaiḥ anabhibhavanīya tvam kṣamā para nimitta pīḍā anubhave api pareṣu tam prati citta vikāra rahita tā dhṛtiḥ mahatyām api āpadi kṛtya kartavyatā avadhāraṇam śaucam bāhya antara karaṇānām kṛtya yogya tā śāstrīyā adrohaḥ pareṣu anuparodhaḥ pareṣu svacchanda vṛtti nirodha rahita tvam iti arthaḥ na ati mānitā asthāne garvaḥ atimāni tvam tad rahita tā ete guṇāḥ daivīm saṃpadam abhijātasya bhavanti deva saṃbandhinī saṃpad daivī devāḥ bhagavat ājñā anuvṛtti śīlāḥ teṣām saṃpad sā ca bhagavat ājñā anuvṛttiḥ eva tām abhijātasya tām abhimukhīkṛtya jātasya tām nivartayitum jātasya bhavanti iti arthaḥ dambhaḥ dhārmika tva khyāpanāya dharma anuṣṭhānam darpaḥ kṛtyā kṛtyauviveka karaḥ viṣaya anubhava nimittaḥ harṣaḥ atimānaḥ ca sva vidyā abhijanān anuguṇa u abhimānaḥ krodhaḥ para piḍā phala citta vikāraḥ pāruṣyam sādhūnām udvega karaḥ svabhāvaḥ ajñānam parāvara tattva kṛtya ākṛtyauvivekaḥ ete svabhāvāḥ āsurīm saṃpadam abhijātasya bhavanti asurāḥ bhagavat ājñāti vṛtti śīlāḥ śokam mā kṛthāḥ tvam tu daivīm saṃpadam abhijātaḥ asi pāṇḍava dhārmika agresarasya hi pāṇḍoḥ tanayaḥ tvam iti abhiprāyaḥ asmin karma loke karmakarāṇām bhūtānām sargaḥ dvividhau daivaḥ ca asuraḥ ca iti sargaḥ utpattiḥ prācīna puṇya pāpa rūpa karma vaśāt bhagavat ājñā anu vṛtti ta d viparīta karaṇāya utpatti kāla eva vibhāgena bhūtāni utpadyanta iti arthaḥ tatra daivaḥ sargaḥ vistaraśaḥ proktaḥ devānām mad ājñā anuvṛtti śīlānām utpattiḥ yad ācāra karaṇa arthā sa ācāraḥ karma yoga jñāna yoga bhakti yoga rūpaḥ vistaraśaḥ proktaḥ asurāṇām sargaḥ ca yad ācāra arthaḥ tam ācāram me śṛṇu mama sakāśāt śṛṇu pravṛttim ca nivṛttim ca abhyudaya sādhanam mokṣa sādhanam ca vaidikam dharmam āsurā na viduḥ na jānanti śaucam vaidika karma yogya tvam śāstra siddham tad bāhyam āntaram ca asureṣu na vidyate na api ca ācāraḥ tad bāhya antara śaucam yena sandhyā vandana ādinā ācāreṇa jāyate saḥ api ācāra ḥ teṣu na vidyate yathā uktam saṃdhyā hīnaḥ aśuciḥ nityam anarhaḥ sarva karmasu iti tathā satyam ca teṣu na vidyate yathā ajñāta bhūta hita rūpa bhāṣaṇam teṣu na vidyate asatyam jagad etad satya śabda nirdiṣṭa brahma kārya tayā brahma ātmakam iti na āhuḥ apratiṣṭham tathā brahmaṇi pratiṣṭhitam iti na vadanti brahmaṇā anantena dhṛtā hi pṛthivī sarvān lokān bibharti yathā uktam tena iyam nāga varyeṇa śirasā vidhṛtā mahī bibharti mālām lokānām sat eva asura mānuṣām iti anīśvaram satya saṃkalpena pareṇa brahmaṇā sarva īśvareṇa mayā etad niyamitam iti ca na vadanti aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate iti hi uktam vadanti ca evam aparaḥ para saṃbhūtam kim anyat yoṣit puruṣayoḥ paraspara saṃbandhena jātam idam manuṣya paśu ādikam upalabhyate anevaṃbhūtam kim anyat upalabhyate kiṃcid api na upalabhyata iti arthaḥ ataḥ sarvam idam jagat kāma hetukam iti etām dṛṣṭim avaṣṭabhya avalambya naṣṭa ātmānaḥ adṛṣṭa deha atirikta ātmānaḥ alpabuddhayaḥ ghaṭādi vaj jñeya bhūte dehe jñātṛ tvena deha vyatirikta ātma upalabhyata iti viveka akuśalāḥ ugra karmāṇaḥ sarveṣām hiṃsakā jagataḥ kṣayāya prabhavanti duṣpūram duṣprāpa viṣayam kāmam āśritya tad si sādhayiṣayā mohāt ajñānāt asat grāhān anyāya gṛhīta parigrahān gṛhītvā aśuci vratāḥ aśāstra vihita vrata yuktāḥ dambha māna mada anvitāḥ pravartante adya śvaḥ vā mumūrṣavaḥ cintām aparimeyām aparicchedyām pralaya antān prākṛta pralaya avadhi kāla sādhya viṣayām upāśritāḥ tathā kāma upabhoga paramāḥ kāma upabhoga eva parama puruṣa artha iti manvānāḥ etāvat iti niścitāḥ itaḥ adhikaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ na vidyata iti saṃjāta niścayāḥ āśā pāśa śataiḥ āśā ākhya pāśa śataiḥ baddhāḥ kāma krodha parāyaṇāḥ kāma krodha eka niṣṭhāḥ kāma bhoga artham anyāyena artha saṃcayān prati īhante idam kṣetra putra ādikam sarvam mayā mad sāmarthyena eva labdham na adṛṣṭa ādinā imam ca manoratham aham eva prāpsye na adṛṣṭa ādi sahitaḥ idam dhanam mad sāmarthyena labdham me asti idam api punar me mad sāmarthyena eva bhaviṣyati īśvaraḥ aham svādhīnaḥ aham anyeṣām ca aham eva niyantā aham bhogī svata eva aham bhogī na adṛṣṭa ādibhiḥ siddhaḥ aham svatassiddhaḥ aham na kasmāccid adṛṣṭa ādeḥ tathā svata eva balavān svata eva sukhī aham svataḥ ca āḍhyaḥ asmi abhijanavān asmi svata eva uttama kule prasūtaḥ asmi asmin loke mayā sadṛśaḥ kaḥ anyaḥ sva sāmarthya labdha sarva vibhavaḥ vidyate aham svayam eva yakṣye dāsyāmi modiṣye iti ajñāna vimohitāḥ īśvara anugraha nirapekṣeṇa svena eva yāga dāna ādikam kartum śakyam iti ajñāna vimohitā manyante adṛṣṭa īśvara ādi sahakāram ṛte svena eva sarvam kartum śakyam iti kṛtvā evam kuryām tad ca kuryām anya t ca kuryām iti aneka citta vibhrāntāḥ evaṃrūpeṇa moha jālena samāvṛtāḥ kāma bhogeṣu prakarṣeṇa saktāḥ madhye mṛtāḥ aśucau narake patanti ātmanā eva saṃbhāvitāḥ ātmanā eva ātmānam saṃbhāvayanti iti arthaḥ stabdhāḥ paripūrṇam manyamānā na kiṃcid kurvāṇāḥ katham dhana māna mada anvitāḥ dhanena vidyā abhijana abhimānena ca janita mada anvitāḥ nāma yajñaiḥ nāma prayojanaiḥ yaṣṭa iti nāma mātra prayojanaiḥ yajñaiḥ yajante tad api dambhena hetunā yaṣṭṛ tva khyāpanāya avidhi pūrvakam ayathā codanam yajante ananya apekṣaḥ aham eva sarvam karomi iti evaṃrūpam ahaṃkāram āśritāḥ tathā sarvasya karaṇe mad balam eva paryāptam iti ca balam ataḥ mad sadṛśaḥ na kaścid asti iti ca darpam evaṃbhūtasya mama kāma mātreṇa sarvam saṃpatsyata iti kāmam mama ye aniṣṭa kāriṇaḥ tān sarvān haniṣyāmi iti ca krodham evam etān saṃśritāḥ sva deheṣu para deheṣu ca avasthitam sarvasya kārayitāram puruṣottamam mām abhyasūyakāḥ pradviṣantaḥ kuyuktibhiḥ mad sthitau doṣam āviṣkurvantaḥ mām asahamānāḥ ahaṃkāra ādikān saṃśritā yāga ādikam sarvam kriyā jātam kurvata iti arthaḥ ya evam mām dviṣanti tān krūrān nara adhamān aśubhān aham ajasram saṃsāreṣu janma jarā maraṇa ādi rūpeṇa parivartamāneṣu saṃtāneṣu tatra api āsurīṣu eva yoniṣu kṣipāmi madānukūlya pratyanīkeṣu eva janmasu kṣipāmi tad tad janma prāpti anuguṇa pravṛtti hetu bhūta buddhiṣu krūrāsu aham eva saṃyojayāmi iti arthaḥ mad ānukūlya pratyanīka janma āpannāḥ punar api janmani janmani mūḍhāḥ mad viparīta jñānā mām aprāpya eva asti bhagavān sarva īśvaraḥ vāsudevaḥ iti jñānam aprāpya tataḥ tataḥ janmanaḥ adhamām eva gatim yānti asya asura svabhāva rūpasya narakasya etad trividham dvāram tad ca ātmanaḥ nāśanam kāmaḥ krodhaḥ lobha iti trayāṇām svarūpam pūrvam eva vyākhyātam dvāram mārgaḥ hetuḥ iti arthaḥ tasmāt etad trayam tyajet tasmāt ati ghora naraka hetu tvāt kāma krodha lobhānām etad tritayam dūrataḥ parityajet etaiḥ kāma krodha lobhaiḥ tamaḥ dvāraiḥ mad viparīta jñāna hetubhiḥ vimukaḥ naraḥ ātmanaḥ śreya ācarati labdha mad viṣaya jñānaḥ mada ānukūlye prayatate tataḥ mām eva parām gatim yāti śāstram vedāḥ vidhiḥ anuśāsanam veda ākhyam mad anuśāsanam utsṛjya yaḥ kāma kārataḥ vartate svacchanda anuguṇa mārgeṇa vartate na sa siddhim avāpnoti na kām api āmuṣmikīm siddhim avāpnoti na sukham kiṃcid avāpnoti na parām gatim kutaḥ parām gatim prāpnoti iti arthaḥ tasmāt kārya akārya vyvasthitau upādeyān upādeya vyavasthāyām śāstram eva tava pramāṇam dharmaśāstra itihāsa purāṇa ādi upabṛṃhitā vedāḥ yad eva puruṣottama ākhyam param tattvam tad prīṇana rūpam tad prāpti upāya bhūtam ca karma avabodhayanti tad śāstra vidhāna uktam tattvam karma ca jñātvā yathāvat anyūna atiriktam vijñāya kartum tvam arhasi tad eva upādātum arhasi śāstra vidhim utsṛjya śraddhayā anvitā ye yajante teṣām niṣṭhā kā kim sattvam āhosvit rajaḥ atha tamaḥ niṣṭhā sthitiḥ sthīyate asmin  iti sthitiḥ sattva ādiḥ eva niṣṭhā iti ucyate teṣām kim sattve sthitiḥ kim vā rajasi kim vā tamasi iti arthaḥ sarveṣām dehinām śraddhā trividhā bhavati sā ca svabhāva jā svabhāvaḥ svāsa ādhāraṇaḥ bhāvaḥ prācīna vāsanā nimittaḥ tad tad ruci viśeṣaḥ yatra ruciḥ tatra śraddhā jāyate śraddhā hi sva abhimatam sādhayati etad iti viśvāsa pūrvikā sādhane tvarā vāsanā ruciḥ ca śraddhā ca ātma dharmāḥ guṇa saṃsarga jāḥ teṣām ātma dharmāṇām vāsanā ādīnām janakāḥ deha indriya antaḥkaraṇa viṣaya gatā dharmāḥ kārya eka nirūpaṇīyāḥ sattva āt ayaḥ guṇāḥ sattva ādi guṇa yukta deha ādi anubhava jā iti arthaḥ tataḥ ca iyam śraddhā sāttvikī rājasī tāmasī ca iti trividhā tām imām śraddhām śṛṇu sā śraddhā yad svabhāvā tam svabhāvam śṛṇv iti arthaḥ sattvam antaḥkaraṇam sarvasya puruṣasya antaḥkaraṇa anurūpā śraddhā bhavati antaḥkaraṇam yādṛśa guṇa yuktam tad viṣayā śraddhā jāyata iti arthaḥ sattva śabdaḥ pūrva uktānām deha indriya ādīnām pradarśana arthaḥ śraddhāmayaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ śraddhā mayaḥ śraddhā pariṇāmaḥ yaḥ yad śraddhaḥ yaḥ puruṣaḥ yādṛśyā śraddhayā yuktaḥ sa eva saḥ sa tādṛśa śraddhā pariṇāmaḥ puṇya karma viṣaye śraddhā yukta ḥ ced puṇya karma phala saṃyuktaḥ bhavati iti śraddhā pradhānaḥ phala saṃyoga iti uktam bhavati sattva guṇa pracurāḥ sāttvikyā śraddhayā yuktāḥ devān yajante duḥkha asaṃbhinna utkṛṣṭa sukha hetu bhūta deva yāga viṣayā śraddhā sāttvikī iti uktam bhavati rājasā yakṣa rakṣāṃsi yajante anye tu tāmasā janāḥ pretān bhūta gaṇān yajante duḥkha saṃbhinna alpa sukha jananī rājasī śraddhā duḥkha prāya ati alpa sukha jananī tāmasi iti arthaḥ karśayantaḥ śarīra stham bhūta grāmam acetasaḥ mām ca eva antar śarīra stham tān viddhi āsura niścayān aśāstra vihitam ati ghoram api tapaḥ ye janāḥ tapyante pradarśana artham idam aśāstra vihitam bahu āyāsam yāga ādikam ye kurvate dambha ahaṃkāra saṃyuktāḥ kāma rāga bala anvitāḥ śarīra stham pṛthivī ādi bhūta samūham karśayantaḥ mad aṃśa bhūtam jīvam ca antar śarīra stham karśayantaḥ ye tapyante yāga ādikam ca kurvate tān āsura niścayān viddhi asurāṇām niścaya āsuraḥ niścayaḥ asurā hi mad ājñā viparīta kāriṇaḥ mad ājñā viparīta kāri tvāt teṣām sukha lava saṃbandhaḥ na vidyate api tu ananartha vrāte patanti iti pūrvam eva uktam patanti narake aścau iti āhāraḥ api sarvasya prāṇi jātasya sattva ādi guṇatraya anvayena trividhaḥ priyaḥ bhavati tathā eva yajñaḥ api trividhaḥ tathā tapaḥ dānam ca teṣām bhedam imam śṛṇu teṣām āhāra yajña tapaḥ dānānām sattva ādi bhedena imam ucyamānam bhedam śṛṇu sattva guṇa upetasya sattva mayā āhārāḥ priyā bhavanti sattva mayāḥ ca āhārā āyuḥ vivardhanāḥ punar api sattvasya vivardhanāḥ sattvam antaḥkaraṇam antaḥkaraṇa kāryam jñānam iha sattva śabdena ucyate sattvāt saṃjāyate jñānam iti sattvasya jñāna vivṛddhi hetutvāt āhāraḥ api sattvam ayaḥ jñāna vivṛddhi hetuḥ tathā bala ārogyayoḥ api vivardhanāḥ sukha prītyoḥ api vivardhanāḥ pariṇāma kāle svayam eva sukhasya vivardhanāḥ tathā prīti hetu bhūta karma ārambha dvāreṇa prīti vardhanāḥ rasyāḥ madhura rasa upetāḥ snigdhāḥ sneha yuktāḥ sthirāḥ sthira pariṇāmāḥ hṛdyāḥ ramaṇīya veṣāḥ evaṃvidhāḥ sattva mayā āhārāḥ sāttvikasya puruṣasya priyāḥ kaṭu rasāḥ amla rasāḥ lavaṇotkaṭāḥ ati uṣṇāḥ ati tīkṣaṇāḥ rūkṣāḥ vidāhinaḥ ca iti kaṭu amla lavaṇa ati uṣṇa tīkṣṇa rūkṣa vidāhinaḥ atiśaitya ati taikṣṇya ādinā durupayoga aḥ tīkṣṇāḥ śoṣa karā rūkṣāḥ tāpa karā vidāhinaḥ evaṃvidhā āhārā rājasasya iṣṭāḥ te ca rajaḥ maya tvāt duḥkha śoka āmaya vardhanāḥ rajaḥ vardhanāḥ ca yātayāmam cira kāla avasthitam gata rasam tyakta svābhāvika rasam pūti durgandha upetam paryuṣitam kāla atipattyā rasa antara āpannam ucchiṣṭam guru ādibhyaḥ anyeṣām bhukta śiṣṭam amedhyam ayajña arham ayajña śiṣṭam iti arthaḥ evaṃvidham tamaḥ mayam bhojanam tāmasapriyam bhavati bhujyata iti āhāra eva bhojanam punar ca tamasaḥ vardhanam ataḥ hita eṣibhiḥ sattva vivṛddhaye sāttvika āhāra eva sevyaḥ phala ākāṅkṣā rahitaiḥ puruṣaiḥ vidhi dṛṣṭaḥ śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ mantra dravya kriyā ādibhiḥ yuktaḥ yaṣṭavyam eva iti bhagavat ārādhana tvena svayaṃprayojana tayā yaṣṭavyam iti manaḥ samādhāya yaḥ yajña ijyate sa sāttvikaḥ phala abhisandhi yuktaiḥ dambha garbhaḥ yaśaḥ phalaḥ ca yaḥ yajña ijyate tam yajñam rājasam viddhi vidhi hīnam brāhmaṇa ukti hīnam sat ācāra yuktaiḥ vidvadbhiḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ yajasva iti ukti hīnam iti arthaḥ asṛṣṭa annam acodita dravyam mantra hīnam adakṣiṇam śraddhā virahitam ca yajñam tāmasam paricakṣate deva dvija guru prājñānām pūjanam śaucam tīrtha snāna ādikam ārjavam yathā manaḥ śarīra vṛttam brahmacaryam yoṣitsu bhogya tā buddhi yukta īkṣaṇa ādi rahita tvam ahiṃsā aprāṇi pīḍā etad charīram tapa ucyate pareṣām anudvega karam satyam priya hitam ca yad vākyam svādhyāya abhyasanam ca iti etad vāc mayam tapa ucyate manaḥ prasādaḥ manasaḥ krodha ādi rahita tvam saumya tvam manasaḥ pareṣām abhyudaya prāvaṇyam maunam manasā vāc pravṛtti niyamanam ātma vinigrahaḥ manaḥ vṛtteḥ dhyeya viṣaye avasthāpanam bhāva śuddhiḥ ātma vyatirikta viṣaya cintā rahita tvam etad mānasam tapaḥ aphala ākāṅkṣibhiḥ phala ākāṅkṣā rahitaiḥ yuktaiḥ parama puruṣa ārādhana rūpam idam iti cintā yuktaiḥ naraiḥ parayā śraddhayā yad trividham tapaḥ kāya vāc manobhiḥ taptam tad sāttvikam paricakṣate manasā ādaraḥ satkāraḥ vācā praśaṃsā mānaḥ śarīraḥ namaskāra ādiḥ pūjā phala abhisandhi pūrvakam satkāra ādi artham ca dambhena hetunā yad tapaḥ kriyate tad iha rājasam proktam svarga ādi phala sādhana tvena asthira tvāt calam adhruvam cala tvam pāta bhayena calana hetu tvam adhruva tvam kṣayiṣṇu tvam mūḍhāḥ avivekinaḥ mūḍha grāheṇa mūḍhaiḥ kṛtena abhiniveśena ātmanaḥ śakti ādikam aparīkṣya ātma pīḍayā yad tapaḥ kriyate parasya utsādana artham ca yad kriyate tad tāmasam udāhṛtam phala abhisandhiḥ ahitam dātavyam iti deśe kāle pātre ca anupakāriṇe yad dānam dīyate tad dānam sāttvikam smṛtam pratyupakāra kaṭākṣa garbham phalam uddiśya ca parikliṣṭam akalyāṇa dravya kam yad dānam dīyate tad rājasam udāhṛtam adeśa kāle apātrebhyaḥ ca yad dānam dīyate asatkṛtam pāda prakṣālana ādi gaurava rahitam avajñātam sa avajñam anupacāra yuktam yad dīyate tad tāmasam udāhṛtam om tad sat iti trividhaḥ ayam nirdeśaḥ śabdaḥ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ brahmaṇaḥ anvayī bhavati brahma ca vedaḥ veda śabdena vaidikam karma ucyate vaidikam yajña ādikam yajña ādikam karma om tad sat iti śabda anvitam bhavati om iti śabdasya anvayaḥ vaidika karma aṅga tvena prayoga ādau prayujyamāna tayā tad sat iti śabdayoḥ anvayaḥ pūjya tvāya vācakatayā tena trividhena śabdena anvitā brāhmaṇāḥ vedān vayinaḥ traivarṇikāḥ vedāḥ ca yajñāḥ ca purā vihitāḥ purā mayā eva nirmitā iti arthaḥ tasmāt brahma vādinām veda ādinām traivarṇikānām yajña dāna tapaḥ kriyāḥ vidhāna uktāḥ veda vidhāna uktāḥ ādau om iti udāhṛtya satatam sarvadā pravartante vedāḥ ca om iti udāhṛtya ārabhyante evam vedānām vaidikānām ca yajña ādīnām karmaṇām om iti śabda anvayaḥ varṇitaḥ om iti śabda anvita veda dhāraṇāt tad anvita yajña ādi karma karaṇa āt ca brāhmaṇa śabda nirdiṣṭānām traivarṇikānām api om iti śabda anvayaḥ varṇitaḥ phalam anabhisandhāya veda adhyayana yajña tapaḥ dāna kriyāḥ mokṣa kāṅkṣibhiḥ traivarṇikaiḥ yāḥ kriyante tāḥ brahma prāpti sādhana tayā brahma vācinā tad iti śabdena nirdeśyāḥ sa vaḥ kaḥ kim yad tad padam anuttamam iti tad śabdaḥ hi brahma vācī prasiddhaḥ evam veda adhyayana yajña ādīnām mokṣa sādhana bhūtānām tad śabda nirdeśya tayā tad iti śabda anvaya uktaḥ traivarṇikānām api tathāvidha veda adhyayana ādi anuṣṭhānāt eva tad śabda anvaya upapannaḥ sadbhāve vidyamāna tāyām sādhu bhāve kalyāṇa bhāve ca sarva vastuṣu sat iti etad padam prayujyate loka vedayoḥ tathā kenacid puruṣeṇa anuṣṭhite laukike praśaste kalyāṇe karmaṇi sat karma idam iti sat śabdaḥ yujyate prayujyate iti arthaḥ ataḥ vaidikānām traivarṇikānām yajñe tapasi dāne ca sthitiḥ kalyāṇa tayā sat iti ucyate karma ca tad arthīyam traivarṇikā arthīyam yajña dāna ādikam sat iti eva abhidhīyate tasmāt vedāḥ vaidikāni karmāṇi brāhmaṇa śabda nirdiṣṭāḥ traivarṇikāḥ ca om tad sat iti śabda anvaya rūpa lakṣaṇena avedebhyaḥ ca avaidikebhyaḥ ca vyāvṛttā veditavyāḥ aśraddhayā kṛtam śāstrī iyam api homa ādikam asad iti ucyate kutaḥ na ca tad pretya naḥ iha na mokṣāya na sāṃsārikāya ca phalāya iti tyāga saṃnyāsau hi mokṣa sādhana tayā vihitau na karmaṇā na prajayā dhanena tyāgena eke amṛta tvam ānaśuḥ vedānta vijñāna su niścita artha aḥ saṃnyāsa yogāt yatayaḥ śuddha sattvāḥ te brahma loke tu para anta kāle para amṛtāt parimucyanti sarve kecana vidvāṃsaḥ kāmyānām karmaṇām nyāsam svarūpa tyāgam saṃnyāsam viduḥ kecid ca vicakṣaṇāḥ nityānām naimittikānām ca kāmyānām sarveṣām karmaṇām phala tyāga eva mokṣa śāstreṣu tyāga śabda artha iti prāhuḥ tatra śāstrīya tyāgaḥ kāmya karma svarūpa viṣayaḥ sarva karma phala viṣaya iti vivādam pradarśayan ekatra saṃnyāsa śabdam itaratra tyāga śabdam prayuktavān ataḥ tyāga saṃnyāsa śabdayoḥ eka artha tvam aṅgīkṛtam iti jñāyate tathā niścayam śṛṇu me tatra tyāge bharata sattama iti tyāga śabdena eva nirṇaya vacanāt  niyatasya tu saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇaḥ na upapadyate mohāt tasya parityāgaḥ tāmasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ eke manīṣiṇaḥ kāpilāḥ vaidikāḥ ca tad mata anusāriṇaḥ rāga ādi doṣavat  bandhaka tvāt sarvam yajña ādikam karma mumukṣuṇā tyājyam iti prāhuḥ apare paṇḍitāḥ yajña ādikam karma na tyājyam iti prāhuḥ tatra evam vādi vipratipanne tyāge tyāga viṣayam niścayam matta ḥ śṛṇu tyāgaḥ kriyamāṇeṣu eva vaidikeṣu karmasu phala viṣaya tayā karma viṣaya tayā kartṛ tva viṣaya tayā ca pūrvam eva hi mayā trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasya adhyātma cetasā nirāśīḥ nirmamaḥ bhūtvā yuddhi asva vigata jvaraḥ iti karma janyam svarga ādikam phalam mama na syāt iti phala tyāgaḥ madīya phala sādhana tayā madīyam idam karma iti karmaṇi mamatāyāḥ parityāgaḥ karma viṣaya ḥ tyāgaḥ sarva īśvare kartṛ tva anusaṃdhānena ātmanaḥ kartṛ tā tyāgaḥ kartṛ tva viṣaya ḥ tyāgaḥ yajña dāna tapaḥ prabhṛtīni varṇa āśrama saṃbandhīni karmāṇi manīṣiṇām manana śīlānām pāvanāni mananam upāsanam mumukṣūṇām yāvajjīvam upāsanam kurvatām upāsana niṣpatti virodhi prācīna karma vināśanāni iti arthaḥ yasmān manīṣiṇām yajña dāna tapaḥ prabhṛtīni pāvanāni tasmāt upāsanavat  etāni api yajña ādi karmāṇi mad ārādhana rūpāṇi saṅgam karmaṇi mamatām phalāni ca tyaktvā aharahar āprayāṇāt upāsana nivṛttaye mumukṣuṇā kartavyāni iti mama niścitam uttamam matam niyatasya nitya naimittikasya mahāyajña ādeḥ karmaṇaḥ saṃnyāsaḥ tyāgaḥ na upapadyate śarīra yātrā api ca tena prasiddhyet akarmaṇaḥ iti śarīra yātrāyāḥ eva asiddheḥ śarīra yātrā hi yajña śiṣṭa aśanena nirvartyamānā samyak jñānāya prabhavati anyathā te tu agham bhuñjate pāpāḥ iti ayajña śiṣṭa agha rūpa aśana āpyāyanam manasaḥ viparīta jñānāya bhavati anna mayam hi somya manaḥ iti annena hi mana āpyāyateāhāra śuddhau sattva śuddhi ḥ sattva śuddhau dhruvā smṛtiḥ smṛti lambhe sarva granthīnām vipramokṣaḥ yadi api paraṃparayā mokṣa sādhana bhūtam karma tathā api duḥkha ātmaka dravya arjana sādhya tvāt bahu āyāsa rūpa tayā kāya kleśa kara tvāt ca manasaḥ avasāda karam iti tad bhītyā yoga niṣpattaye jñāna abhyāsa eva yatanīya iti yaḥ mahāyajña ādi āśrama karma parityajet sa rājasam rajaḥ mūlam tyāgam kṛtvā tad ayathā avasthita śāstra artha rūpam iti jñāna utpatti rūpam tyāga phalam na labhate ayathāvat prajānāti buddhi ḥ sā pārtha rājasī iti hi vakṣyate na hi karma dṛṣṭa dvāreṇa manaḥ prasāda hetuḥ api tu bhava gad prasāda dvāreṇa nitya naimittika mahā yajña ādi varṇa āśrama vihitam karma mad ārādhana rūpa tayā kāryam svayaṃprayojanam iti matvā saṅgam karmaṇi mamatām phalam ca tyaktvā yad kriyate sa tyāgaḥ sāttvikaḥ mataḥ sa sattva mūlaḥ yathā avasthita śāstra artha jñāna mūla iti arthaḥ sattvam hi yathā avasthita vastu jñānam utpādayati iti uktam sattvāt saṃjāyate jñānam iti vakṣyate ca pravṛttim ca nivṛttim ca kārya akāryam bhaya abhaye bandham mokṣam ca yā vetti buddhiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikī evam sattva samāviṣṭaḥ medhāvī yathā avasthita tattva jñānaḥ tataḥ eva cchinna saṃśayaḥ karmaṇi saṅga phala kartṛ tva tyāgī na dveṣṭy akuśalam karma śukale ca karmaṇi na anuṣajjate akuśalam karma aniṣṭa phalam kuśalam ca karma iṣṭa rūpa svarga putra paśu annādya ādi phalam sarvasmin karmaṇi mamatā rahita tvāt tyakta brahma vyatirikta sarva phala tvāt tyakta kartṛ tva āc ca tayoḥ kriyamāṇayoḥ prīti dveṣau na karoti aniṣṭa phalam pāpam karma atra prāma ādikam abhipretam nāvirataḥ duścaritān na aśāntaḥ na asamāhitaḥ nāśa anta mānasaḥ vā api prajñānena enam āpnuyāt na hi dehabhṛtā dhriyamāṇa śarīreṇa karmāṇi aśeṣataḥ tyaktum śakyam deha dhāraṇa arthānām aśana pāna ādīnām tad anubandhinām ca karmaṇām avarjanīya tvāt tad artham ca mahāyajña ādi anuṣṭhānam avarjanīyam yaḥ tu teṣu mahāyajña ādi karmasu phala tyāgī sa eva tyāgena eke amṛta tvam ānaśuḥ ityādi śāstreṣu tyāgī iti abhidhīyate phalatyāgī iti pradarśana artham phala kartṛ tva karma saṅgānām tyāgī iti trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ iti prakramāt aniṣṭam naraka ādi phalam iṣṭam svarga ādi miśram aniṣṭa saṃbhinnam putra paśu annādya ādi etad trividham karmaṇaḥ phalam atyāginām kartṛ tvam amatā phala tyāga rahitānām pretya bhavati pretya karma anuṣṭhāna uttara kālam iti arthaḥ na tu saṃnyāsinām kvacid na tu kartṛ tva ādi parityāginām kvacid api mokṣa virodhi phalam bhavati etad uktam bhavati yadi api agnihotra mahā yajña ādīni tāni eva tathā api jīvana adhikāra kāma adhikārayoḥ iva mokṣa adhikāre ca viniyoga pṛthaktvena parihriyate mokṣa viniyoga ḥ ca tam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣanti yajñena dānena tapasā anāśakena ityādibhiḥ iti tad evam kriyamāṇeṣu eva karmasu kartṛ tva ādi parityāgaḥ śāstra siddhiḥ saṃnyāsaḥ sa eva ca tyāga iti uktaḥ % sāṃkhyā buddhiḥ sāṃkhye kṛtānte yathā avasthita tattva viṣayayā vaidikyā buddhyā anusaṃhite nirṇaye sarva karmaṇām siddhaye utpattaye proktāni pañca etāni kāraṇāni nibodhe me mama sakāśāt anusaṃdhatsva vaidikī hi buddhiḥ śarīra indriya prāṇa jīva ātma upakaraṇam paramātmānam eva kartāram avadhārayati ya ātmani tiṣṭhan ātmanaḥ antaraḥ yam ātmā na veda yasya ātmā śarīram ya ātmānam antaraḥ yamayati sa ta ātmā antaryāmy amṛtaḥ  antaḥ praviṣṭaḥ śāstā janānām sarva ātmā ityādiṣu tad idam āha adhiṣṭhānam tathā kartā karaṇam ca pṛthagvidham vividhā ca pṛthak ceṣṭā daivam ca eva atra pañcamam śarīra vāc manobhiḥ yad karma prārabhate naraḥ nyāyyam vā viparītam vā pañca ete tasya hetavaḥ nyāyye śāstra siddhe viparīte pratiṣiddhe vā sarvasmin karmaṇi śarīre vācike mānase ca pañca ete hetavaḥ adhiṣṭhānam śarīram adhiṣṭhīyate jīva ātmanā iti mahābhūta saṃghāta rūpam śarīram adhiṣṭhānam tathā kartā jīvātmā asya jīva ātmanaḥ jñātṛ tvam kartṛ tvam ca jñaḥ ata eva  kartā śāstra arthavat tvāt  iti ca sūtra upapāditam karaṇam ca pṛthagvidham vāc pāṇi pāda ādi pañcakam samanaskam karmendriyam pṛthagvidham karma niṣpattau pṛthak vyāpāram vividhā ca pṛthak ceṣṭā ceṣṭā śabdena pañca ātmā vāyuḥ abhidhīyate tad vṛtti vācinā śarīra indriya dhāraṇasya prāṇa apāna ādi bheda bhinnasya vāyoḥ pañca ātmanaḥ vividhā ca ceṣṭā vividhā vṛttiḥ daivam ca eva atra pañcamam atra karma hetu kalāpe daivam pañcamam paramātmā antaryāmī karma niṣpattau pradhāna hetuḥ iti arthaḥ uktam hi sarvasya ca aham hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ mattaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam ca iti vakṣyati ca īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan sarva bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā  iti paramātmā āyattam ca jīvātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam parāt tu tad śruteḥ ityādi upapāditam nanu evam paramātmā āyatte jīvātmanaḥ kartṛ tve jīvātmā karmaṇi aniyojyaḥ bhavati iti vidhi niṣedha śāstrāṇi anarthakāni syuḥ idam api codyam sūtrakāreṇa parihṛtam kṛta prayatna apekṣaḥ tu vihita pratiṣiddha avaiya arthyādibhyaḥ iti etad uktam bhavati parama ātmanā dattaiḥ tad ādhāraiḥ ca karaṇa kalebara ādibhiḥ tadā āhita śaktibhiḥ svayam ca jīvātmā tad ādhāra ḥ tadā āhita śakti ḥ san karma niṣpattaye sva icchayā karaṇa ādi adhiṣṭhāna ākāram prayatnam ca ārabhate tad antar avasthitaḥ paramātmā sva anum ati dānena tam
