pravartayati iti jīvasya api sva buddhyā eva pravṛtti hetu tvam asti yathā gurutara śilā mahīruha ādi calana ādi phala pravṛttiṣu bahu puruṣa sādhyāsu bahūnām hetu tvam vidhi niṣedha bhāj tvam ca iti tatra evam sati kartāram ātmānam kevalam tu yaḥ paśyati akṛtabuddhi tvān na sa paśyati durmatiḥ evam vastutaḥ paramātma anumati pūrvake jīvātmanaḥ kartṛ tve sati tatra karmaṇi kevalam ātmānam eva kartāram yaḥ paśyati sa durmatiḥ viparīta matiḥ akṛtabuddhi tvāt aniṣpanna yathā avasthita vastu buddhi tvān na paśyati na yathā avasthitam kartāram paśyati yasya na ahaṃkṛtaḥ bhāvaḥ buddhiḥ yasya na lipyate hatvā api sa imān  lokān na hanti na nibadhyate parama puruṣa kartṛ tva anusaṃdhānena yasya bhāvaḥ kartṛ tva viṣayaḥ manaḥ vṛtti viśeṣaḥ na ahaṃkṛtaḥ na aham abhimāna kṛtaḥ aham karomi iti jñānam yasya na vidyata iti arthaḥ buddhiḥ yasya na lipyate asmin karmaṇi mama kartṛ tva abhāvāt etad phalam na mayā saṃbadhyate na ca madīyam karma iti yasya buddhiḥ jāyata iti arthaḥ sa imān lokān yuddhe hatvā api tān na nihanti na kevalam bhīṣma ādīn iti arthaḥ tataḥ tena yuddha ākhyena karmaṇā na nibadhyate tad phalam na anubhavati iti arthaḥ sarvam idam akartṛ tva ādi anusandhānam sattva guṇa vṛddhyā eva bhavati iti sattvasya upādeya tā ājñāpanāya karmaṇi sattva ādi guṇa kṛtam vaiṣamyam prapañcayiṣyan karma codanā prakāram tāvat āha jñānam jñeyam parijñātā trividhā karma codanā kāraṇam karma kartā iti trividhaḥ karma saṃgrahaḥ jñānam kartavya karma viṣayam jñānam jñeyam ca kartavyam karma parijñātā tasya boddha iti trividhā karma codanā bodha boddhavya boddhṛ yuktaḥ jyotiṣṭoma ādi karma vidhiḥ iti arthaḥ tatra boddhavya rūpam karma trividham saṃgṛhyate karaṇam karma kartā iti karaṇam sādhana bhūtam dravya ādikam karma yāga ādikam kartā anuṣṭhātā iti jñānam karma ca kartā ca tridhā eva guṇa bhedataḥ procyate guṇa saṃkhyāne yathā avac śṛṇu tāni api kartavya karma viṣayam jñānam anuṣṭhīyamānam ca karma tasya anuṣṭhātā ca sattva ādi guṇa bhedataḥ trividhā eva procyate guṇa saṃkhyāne guṇa kārya gaṇane yathā avac śṛṇu tāni api tāni guṇataḥ bhinnāni jñāna ādīni yathā avac śṛṇu sarva bhūteṣu yena ekam bhāvam avyayam īkṣate avibhaktam vibhakteṣu tad jñānam viddhi sāttvikam brāhmaṇa kṣatriya brahmacāri gṛhastha ādi rūpeṇa vibhakteṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu karma adhikāriṣu yena jñānena ekam ātma ākhyam bhāvam tatra api avibhaktam brāhmaṇa tva ādi aneka ākāreṣu api bhūteṣu sita dīrgha ādi vibhāgavatsu jñāna ākāre ātmani vibhāga rahitam avyayam vyaya svabhāveṣu api brāhmaṇa ādi śarīreṣu avyayam avikṛtam phala ādi saṅgān arham ca karma adhikāra velāyām īkṣate tad jñānam sāttvikam viddhi pṛthaktvena tu yaj jñānam nānā bhāvān pṛthagvidhān vetti sarveṣu bhūteṣu tad jñānam viddhi rājasam sarveṣu bhūteṣu brāhmaṇa ādiṣu brāhmaṇa ādi ākāra pṛthaktvena ātma ākhyān api bhāvān nānā bhūtān sita dīrgha ādi pṛthaktvena ca pṛthagvidhān phala ādi saṃyoga yogyān karma adhikāra velāyām yaj jñānam vetti tad jñānam rājasam viddhi yad tu kṛtsnavat  ekasmin kārye saktam ahetukam atattva arthavat alpam ca tad tāmasam udāhṛtam yad tu jñānam ekasmin kārye ekasmin kartavye karmaṇi preta bhūta gaṇa ādi ārādhana rūpe ati alpa phale kṛtsna phalavat  saktam ahetukam vastu taḥ tu akṛtsna phalavat tayā tathāvidha saṅga hetu rahitam atattva arthavat pūrvavat eva ātmani pṛthaktva ādi yukta tayā mithyā bhūta artha viṣayam ati alpa phalam ca preta bhūta ādi ārādhana viṣaya tvāt alpam ca tad jñānam tāmasam udāhṛtam evam kartavya karma viṣaya jñānasya adhikāra velāyām adhikārī aṃśena guṇataḥ traividhyam uktvā anuṣṭheyasya karmaṇaḥ guṇataḥ traividhyam āha niyatam saṅga rahitam arāga dveṣataḥ kṛtam aphala prepsunā karma yad tad sāttvikam ucyate niyatam sva varṇa āśrama ucitam saṅga rahitam kartṛ tva ādi saṅga rahitam arāga dveṣataḥ kṛtam kīrti rāgāt akīrti dveṣā c ca na kṛtam adambhena kṛtam iti arthaḥ aphala prepsunā aphala abhisandhinā kāryam iti eva kṛtam yad karma tad sāttvikam ucyate yad tu kāma īpsunā karma sa ahaṅkāreṇa vā punar kriyate bahula āyāsam tad rājasam udāhṛtam yad tu punar kāma īpsunā phala prepsunā sa ahaṃkāreṇa vā vā śabda ḥ ca arthe kartṛ tva abhimāna yuktena ca bahula āyāsam yad karma kriyate tad rājasam bahula āyāsam idam karma mayā eva kriyata iti evaṃrūpa abhimāna yuktena yad karma kriyate tad rājasam iti arthaḥ anubandham kṣayam hiṃsām anavekṣya ca pauruṣam mohāt ārabhyate karma yad tad tāmasam ucyate kṛte karmaṇi anubadhyamānam duḥkham anubandhaḥ kṣayaḥ karmaṇi kriyamāṇe artha vināśaḥ hiṃsā tatra prāṇi pīḍā pauruṣam ātmanaḥ karma samāpana sāmarthyam etāni anavekṣya avimṛśya mohāt parama puruṣa kartṛ tva ajñānāt yad karma ārabhyate tad tāmasam ucyate mukta saṅgaḥ anahaṃvā ādī dhṛti utsāha samanvitaḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ nirvikāraḥ kartā sāttvika ucyate mukta saṅgaḥ phala saṅga rahitaḥ anahaṃvādī kartṛ tva abhimāna rahitaḥ dhṛti utsāha samanvitaḥ ārabdhe karmaṇi yāvat karma samāptya varjanīya duḥkha dhāraṇam dhṛtiḥ utsāhaḥ udyukta cetaḥ tvam tābhyām samanvitaḥ siddhi asiddhyoḥ nirvikāraḥ yuddha ādau karmaṇi tad upakaraṇa bhūta dravya arjana ādiṣu ca siddhi asiddhyoḥ avikṛta cittaḥ kartā sāttvika ucyate ragī karma phala prepsuḥ lubdhaḥ hiṃsā ātmakaḥ aśuciḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ kartā rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ rāgī yaśaḥ arthī karma phala prepsuḥ karma phala arthī lubdhaḥ karma apekṣita dravya vyaya svabhāva rahitaḥ hiṃsā ātmakaḥ parān pīḍayitvā taiḥ karma kurvāṇaḥ aśuciḥ karma apekṣita śuddhi rahitaḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ yuddha ādau karmaṇi jaya ādi siddhi asiddhyoḥ harṣa śoka anvitaḥ kartā rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ayuktaḥ prākṛtaḥ stabdhaḥ śaṭhaḥ naikṛti kaḥ alasaḥ viṣa ādī dīrghasūtrī ca kartā tāmasa ucyate ayuktaḥ śāstrīya karma ayogyaḥ vikarma sthaḥ prākṛtaḥ anadhigata vidyaḥ stabdhaḥ anārambha śīlaḥ śaṭhaḥ abhicāra ādi karma ruciḥ naikṛtikaḥ vañcana paraḥ alasaḥ ārabdheṣu api karmasu manda pravṛttiḥ viṣa ādī atimātra avasāda śīlaḥ dīrghasūtrī abhicāra ādi karma kurvan pareṣu dīrgha kāla varti anartha paryālocana śīlaḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ yaḥ kartā sa tāmasaḥ evam kartavya karma viṣaya jñāne kartavye ca karmaṇi anuṣṭhātari ca guṇataḥ traividhyam uktam idānīm sarva tattva sarva puruṣa artha niścaya rūpāyāḥ buddheḥ dhṛteḥ ca guṇataḥ traividhyam āha buddheḥ bhedam dhṛteḥ ca eva guṇataḥ trividham śṛṇu procyamānam aśeṣeṇa pṛthaktvena dhanaṃjaya buddhiḥ viveka pūrvakam niścaya rūpam jñānam dhṛtiḥ ārabdhāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ vighna upanipāte api dhāraṇam tayoḥ sattva ādi guṇataḥ trividham bhedam pṛthaktvena procyamānam yathā avac śṛṇu pravṛttim ca nivṛttim ca kārya akārye bhaya abhaye bandham mokṣam ca yā vetti buddhiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikī pravṛttiḥ abhyudaya sādhana bhūtaḥ dharmaḥ nivṛttiḥ mokṣa sādhana bhūtaḥ tav ubhau yathā avasthitau yā buddhiḥ vetti kārya akārye sarva varṇānām pravṛtti nivṛtti dharmayoḥ anyatara niṣṭhānām deśa kāla avasthā viśeṣeṣu idam kāryam idam akāryam iti yā vetti bhaya abhaye śāstra ativṛttiḥ bhaya sthānam tad anuvṛttiḥ abhaya sthānam bandham mokṣam ca saṃsāra yāthātmyam tad vigamayāthātmyam ca yā vetti sā sāttvikī buddhiḥ yathā dharmam adharmam ca kāryam ca akāryam eva ca ayathāvat prajānāti buddhiḥ sā pārtha rājasī yathā pūrva uktam dvividham dharmam tad viparītam ca tad niṣṭhānām deśa kāla avasthā ādiṣu kāryam ca akāryam ca yathāvan na jānāti sā rājasī buddhiḥ adharmam dharmam iti yā manyate tamasā āvṛtā sarva arthān viparītān  ca buddhiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī tāmasī tu buddhiḥ tamasā āvṛtā satī sarva arthān viparītān manyate adharmam dharmam dharmam ca adharmam santam ca artham asantam asantam ca artham santam param ca tattvam aparam aparam ca tattvam param evam sarvam viparītam manyata iti arthaḥ dhṛtyā yayā dhārayate manaḥ prāṇa indriya kriyāḥ yogena avyabhicāriṇyā dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikī yayā dhṛtyā yogena avyabhicāriṇyā manaḥ prāṇa indriyāṇām kriyāḥ puruṣaḥ dhārayate yogaḥ mokṣa sādhana bhūtam bhagavat upāsanam yogena prayojana bhūtena avyabhicāriṇyā yoga uddeśena pravṛttā aḥ tad sādhana bhūtāḥ manaḥ prabhṛtīnām kriyāḥ yayā dhṛtyā dhārayate sā sāttvikī iti arthaḥ yayā tu dharma kāma arthān dhṛtyā dhārayate arjuna prasaṅgena phala ākāṅkṣī dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha rājasī phala ākāṅkṣī puruṣaḥ prakṛṣṭa saṅgena dharma kāma arthān yayā dhṛtyā dhārayate sā rājasī dharma kāma artha śabdena tad sādhana bhūtāḥ manaḥ prāṇa indriya kriyā lakṣyante phala ākāṅkṣi iti atra api phala śabdena rāja satvāt dharma kāma arthā eva vivakṣitāḥ ataḥ dharma kāma artha apekṣayā manaḥ prabhṛtīnām kriyā yayā dhṛtyā dhārayate sā rājasi iti uktam bhavati yayā svapnam bhayam śokam viṣādam madam eva ca na vimuñcati durmedhā dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha tāmasī yayā dhṛtyā svapnam nidrām madam viṣaya anubhava janitam madam svapna madav uddiśya pravṛttā manaḥ prāṇa ādīnām kriyāḥ durmedhā na vimuñcati dhārayati bhaya śoka viṣāda śabda āḥ ca bhaya śoka ādi dāyi viṣaya parāḥ tad sādhana bhūtāḥ ca manaḥ prāṇa ādi kriyā yayā dhārayate sā dhṛtiḥ tāmasī sukham tu idānīm trividham śṛṇu me bharata ṛṣabha pūrva uktāḥ sarve jñāna karma kartrādayaḥ yad cheṣa bhūtāḥ tad ca sukham guṇataḥ trividham idānīm śṛṇu abhyāsāt ramate yatra duḥkhāntam ca nigacchati yad tad agre viṣam iva pariṇāme amṛta upamam tad sukham sāttvikam proktam ātma buddhi prasāda jam yasmin sukhe cira kāla abhyāsāt krameṇa niratiśayām ratim prāpnoti duḥkhāntam ca nigacchati nikhilasya sāṃsārikasya duḥkhasya antam nigacchati tad eva viśinaṣṭi yad tad sukham agre yoga upakrama velāyām bahu āyāsa sādhya tvāt vivikta svarūpasya ananubhūta tvāt ca viṣam iva duḥkham iva bhavati pariṇāme amṛta upamam pariṇāme vipāke abhyāsa balena vivikta ātma svarūpa āvirbhāve amṛta upamam bhavati tad ca ātma buddhi prasāda jam ātma viṣayā buddhiḥ ātma buddhiḥ tasyāḥ nivṛtta sakala itara viṣaya tvam prasādaḥ nivṛtta sakala itara viṣaya buddhyā vivikta svabhāva ātma anubhava janitam sukham amṛta upamam bhavati tad sukham sāttvikam proktam viṣaya indriya saṃyogāt yad tad agre amṛta upamam pariṇāme viṣam iva tad sukham rājasam smṛtam agre anubhava velāyām viṣaya indriya saṃyogāt yad tad amṛtam iva bhavati pariṇāme vipāke viṣayāṇām sukhatā nimitta kṣudh ādau nivṛtte tasya ca sukhasya niraya ādi nimitta tvāt viṣam iva pītam bhavati tad sukham rājasam smṛtam yad agre ca anubandhe ca sukham mohanam ātmanaḥ nidrā ālasya pramāda uttham tad tāmasam udāhṛtam yad sukham agre ca anubandhe ca anubhava velāyām vipāke ca ātmanaḥ mohanam moha hetuḥ bhavati mohaḥ atra yathā avasthitavastu aprakāśaḥ abhipretaḥ nidrā ālasya pramāda uttham nidrā ālasya pramāda janitam nidrādayaḥ hi anubhava velāyām api moha hetavaḥ nidrāyāḥ moha hetu tvam spṛṣṭam ālasyam indriya vyāpāram āndyam indriya vyāpāram āndye ca jñānam āndyam bhavati eva pramādaḥ kṛtyān avadhāna rūpa iti tatra api jñānam āndyam bhavati tataḥ ca tayoḥ api moha hetu tvam tad sukham tāmasam udāhṛtam ataḥ mumukṣuṇā rajaḥ tamasī abhibhūya sattvam eva upādeyam iti uktam bhavati na tad asti pṛthivyām vā divi deveṣu vā punar sattvam prakṛti jaiḥ muktam yad ebhiḥ syāt tribhiḥ guṇaiḥ pṛthivyām manuṣya ādiṣu divi deveṣu vā prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭeṣu brahma ādiṣu sthāvara anteṣu prakṛti jaiḥ ebhiḥ tribhiḥ guṇaiḥ muktam yad sattvam prāṇi jātam na tad asti tyāgena eke amṛta tvam ānaśuḥ ityādiṣu mokṣa sādhana tayā nirdiṣṭaḥ tyāgaḥ saṃnyāsa śabda arthāt ananyaḥ sa ca kriyamāṇeṣu eva karmasu kartṛ tva tyāga mūlaḥ phala karmaṇā ūḥ tyāgaḥ kartṛ tva tyāgaḥ ca parama puruṣe kartṛ tva anusaṃdhānena iti uktam etad sarvam sattva guṇa vṛddhi kāryam iti sattva upādeyata ājñāpanāya sattva rajaḥ tamasām kārya bhedāḥ prapañcitāḥ idānīm evaṃbhūtasya mokṣa sādhana tayā kriyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥ parama puruṣa ārādhana veṣatām tathā anuṣṭhitasya ca karmaṇaḥ tad prāpti lakṣaṇam phalam pratipādayitum brāhmaṇa ādi adhikāriṇām svabhāva anubandhi sattva ādi guṇa bheda bhinnam vṛttyā saha kartavya karma svarūpam āha brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām śūdrāṇām ca paraṃtapa karmāṇi pravibhaktāni svabhāva prabhavaiḥ guṇaiḥ brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām svakīyaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ brāhmaṇa ādi janma hetu bhūtam prācīnakarma iti arthaḥ tad prabhavāḥ sattva āt ayaḥ guṇāḥ brāhmaṇasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ abhibhavena udbhūtaḥ sattva guṇaḥ kṣatriyasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ tamaḥ sattva abhibhavena udbhūtaḥ rajaḥ guṇaḥ vaiśyasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ sattva rajaḥ abhibhavena alpa udrikta ḥ tamaḥ guṇaḥ śūdrasya svabhāva prabhavaḥ tu rajaḥ sattva abhibhavena ati udrikta ḥ tamaḥ guṇaḥ ebhiḥ svabhāva prabhavaiḥ guṇaiḥ saha pravibhaktāni karmāṇi śāstraiḥ pratipāditāni brāhmaṇa ādaya evaṃguṇakāḥ teṣām ca etāni karmāṇi vṛttayaḥ ca etāḥ iti hi vibhajya pratipādayanti śāstrāṇi śamaḥ damaḥ tapaḥ śaucam kṣāntiḥ ārjavam eva ca jñānam vijñānam āstikyam brāhmam karma svabhāva jam śamaḥ bāhya indriya niyamanam damaḥ antaḥkaraṇa niyamanam tapaḥ bhoga niyamana rūpaḥ śāstra siddhaḥ kāya kleśaḥ śaucam śāstrīya karma yogya tā kṣāntiḥ paraiḥ pīḍyamānasya api avikṛta citta tā ārjavam pareṣu manaḥ anurūpam bāhya ceṣṭā prakāśanam jñānam parāvara tattva yāthātmya jñānam vijñānam para tattva gata asā dhāraṇa viśeṣa viṣayam jñānam āstikyam vaidikasya kṛtsnasya satya tā niścayaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ kena api hetunā cālayitum aśakya iti arthaḥ bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ vāsudevaḥ para brahma śabda abhideyaḥ nirasta nikhila doṣa gandhaḥ svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya jñāna śakti ādi asaṅkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇaḥ nikhila veda vedānta vedyaḥ sa eva nikhila jagat eka kāraṇam nikhila jagat ādhāra bhūtaḥ nikhilasya sa eva pravartayitā tad ārādhana bhūtam ca vaidikam kṛtsnam karma taiḥ taiḥ ārādhitaḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣa ākhyam phalam prayacchati iti asya arthasya satya tā niścaya āstikyam vedaiḥ ca sarvaiḥ aham eva vedyaḥ  aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate  mayi sarvam idam protam  bhoktāram yajña tapasām jñātvā mām śāntim ṛcchati  mattaḥ parataram na anyat kiñcid asti dhanañjaya  yataḥ pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yena sarvam idam tatam sva karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ  yaḥ mām ajam anādim ca vetti loka maheśvaram iti hi ucyate tad etad brāhmaṇasya svabhāva jam karma śairyam tejaḥ dhṛtiḥ dākṣyam yuddhe ca api apalāyanam dānam īśvara bhāvaḥ ca kṣātram karma svabhāva jam śairyam yuddhe nirbhaya praveśa sāmarthyam tejaḥ paraiḥ anabhibhavanīya tā dhṛtiḥ ārabdhe karmaṇi vighna upanipāte api tad samāpana sāmarthyam dākṣyam sarva kriyā nirvṛtti sāmarthyam yuddhe ca api apalāyanam yuddhe ca ātma maraṇa niścaye api anirvartanam dānam ātmīyasya dhanasya para sva tva āpādana paryanta ḥ tyāgaḥ īśvara bhāvaḥ sva vyatirikta sakala jana niyamana sāmarthyam etad kṣatriyasya svabhāva jam karma kṛṣi gorakṣya vāṇijyam vaiśyam karma svabhāva jam kṛṣiḥ satya utpādanam karṣaṇam gorakṣyam paśu pālanam iti arthaḥ vāṇijyam dhana sañcaya hetu bhūtam kraya vikraya ātmakam karma etad vaiśyasya svabhāva jam karma paricaryā ātmakam karma śūdrasya api svabhāva jam pūrva varṇa traya paricaryā rūpam śūdrasya svabhāva jam karma tad etad caturṇā varṇānām vṛttibhiḥ saha kartavyānām śāstra vihitānām yajña ādi karmaṇām pradarśana artham uktam yajñādayaḥ hi trayāṇām varṇānām sādhāraṇāḥ śamādayaḥ api trayāṇām varṇānām mumukṣūṇām sādhāraṇāḥ brāhmaṇasya tu sattva udrekasya svābhāvika tvena śama dama ādayaḥ sukha upādānā iti kṛtvā tasya śama ādaya svabhāva jam karma iti uktam kṣatriya vaiśyayoḥ tu svataḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ pradhāna tvena śama damādayaḥ duḥkha upādānā iti kṛtvā na tad karma iti uktam brāhmaṇasya vṛttiḥ yājana adhyāpana pratigrahāḥ kṣatriyasya janapada paripālanam vaiśyasya ca kṛṣyādayaḥ yathā uktāḥ śūdrasya tu kartavyam vṛttiḥ ca pūrva varṇa traya paricaryā eva sve sve karmaṇi abhirataḥ saṃsiddhim labhate naraḥ sva karma nirataḥ siddhim yathā vindati tad śṛṇu sve sve yathā udite karmaṇi abhirataḥ naraḥ saṃsiddhim parama pada prāptim labhate sva karma nirataḥ yathā siddhim vindati parama padam prāpnoti tathā śṛṇu yataḥ pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yena sarvam idam tatam sva karmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhim vindati mānavaḥ yataḥ bhūtānām utpatti ādikā pravṛttiḥ yena ca sarvam idam tatam sva karmaṇā tam mām indra ādi antarātma tayā avasthitam abhyarcya mad prasādān mad prāpti rūpām siddhim vindati mānavaḥ matta eva sarvam utpadyate mayā ca sarvam idam tatam iti pūrvam eva uktam aham kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ tathā mattaḥ parataram na anyat kiṃcid asti dhanañjaya  mayā tatam idam sarvam jagad avyakta mūrtinā  mayā adhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaram  aham sarvasya prabhavaḥ matta ḥ sarvam pravartate ityādiṣu śreyān svadharmaḥ viguṇaḥ para dharmāt su anuṣṭhitāt evam tyakta kartṛ tva ādikaḥ mad ārādhana rūpaḥ svadharmaḥ svena eva upādātum yogyaḥ dharmaḥ prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭena hi puruṣeṇa indriya vyāpāra rūpaḥ karma yoga ātmakaḥ dharmaḥ sukaraḥ bhavati ataḥ karma yoga ākhyaḥ svadharmaḥ viguṇaḥ api para dharmāt indriya jaya nipuṇa puruṣa dharmāj jñāna yogāt sakala indriya niyamana rūpa tayā sa pramādāt kadācid su anuṣṭhitāc śreyān tad eva upapādayati svabhāva niyatam karma kurvan na āpnoti kilbiṣam prakṛti saṃsṛṣṭasya puruṣasya indriya vyāpāra rūpa tayā svabhāvata eva niyata tvāt karmaṇaḥ karma kurvan kilbiṣam saṃsāram na prāpnoti apramāda tvāt karmaṇaḥ jñāna yogasya sakala indriya niyamana sādhya tayā sa pramāda tvāt tad niṣṭhaḥ tu pramādāt kilbiṣam pratipadyeta api ataḥ karma niṣṭhā eva jyāyasi iti tṛtīyā adhyāya uktam smārayati sahajam karma kaunteya sa doṣam api na tyajet sarva ārambhā hi doṣeṇa dhūmena agniḥ iva āvṛtāḥ ataḥ sahaja tvena sukaram apramādam ca karma sa doṣam sa duḥkham api na tyajet jñāna yoga yogyaḥ api karma yogam eva kurvīta iti arthaḥ sarva ārambhāḥ karma ārambhāḥ jñāna ārambhāḥ ca hi doṣeṇa duḥkhena dhūmena agniḥ iva āvṛtāḥ iyāṃ  tu viśeṣaḥ karma yogaḥ sukaraḥ apramādaḥ ca jñāna yoga ḥ tad viparītaḥ iti asakta buddhi ḥ sarvatra jita ātmā vigata spṛhaḥ naiṣkarmya siddhim paramām saṃnyāsena adhigacchati sarvatra phala ādiṣu asakta buddhiḥ jita ātmā jita manāḥ parama puruṣa kartṛ tva anusaṃdhānena ātma kartṛ tve vigata spṛhaḥ evam tyāgāt ananya tvena nirṇītena saṃnyāsena yuktaḥ karma kurvan paramām naiṣkarmya siddhim adhigacchati paramām dhyāna niṣṭhām jñāna yogasya api phala bhūtam adhigacchati iti arthaḥ vakṣyamāṇa dhyāna yoga avāptim sarva indriya karma uparatirūpām adhigacchati siddhim prāptaḥ yathā brahma tathā āpnoti nibodha me samāsena eva kaunteya niṣṭhā jñānasya yā parā siddhim prāptaḥ āprayāṇāt aharahar anuṣṭhīyamāna karma yoga niṣpādya dhyāna sidddhim prāptaḥ yathā yena prakāreṇa vartamānaḥ brahma prāpnoti tathā samāsena me nibodha tad eva brahma viśeṣyate niṣṭhā jñānasya yā para iti jñānasya dhyāna ātmakasya yā parā niṣṭhā parama prāpyam iti arthaḥ buddhyā viśuddhayā yuktaḥ dhṛti ātmānam niyamya ca śabda ādīn viṣayān  tyaktvā rāga dveṣau vyudasya ca vivikta sevī laghu āśī yatavāk kāya mānasaḥ dhyāna yoga paraḥ nityam vairāgyam samupāśritaḥ ahaṅkāram balam darpam kāmam krodham parigraham vimucya nirmamaḥ śāntaḥ brahma bhūyāya kalpate buddhyā viśuddhayā yathā avasthita ātma tattva viṣayayā yuktaḥ dhṛtyā ātmānam niyamya ca viṣaya vimukhīkaraṇena yoga yogyam manaḥ kṛtvā śabda ādīn viṣayān tyaktvā asannihitān kṛtvā tad nimittau ca rāga dveṣau vyudasya vivikta sevī sarvaiḥ dhyāna virodhibhiḥ vivikte deśe vartamānaḥ laghu āśī ati aśana anaśana rahitaḥ yatavāk kāya mānasaḥ dhyāna abhimukhīkṛta kāya vāc manaḥ vṛttiḥ dhyāna yoga paraḥ nityam evaṃbhūta ḥ san ā prāyāṇāt aharahar dhyāna yoga paraḥ vairāgyam samupāśritaḥ dhyeya tattva vyatirikta viṣaya doṣa avamarśena tatra tatra virāgatām vardhayan ahaṃkāram anātmani ātma abhimānam balam tad vṛddhi hetu bhūta vāsana balam tad nimittam darpam kāmam krodham parigraham vimucya nirmamaḥ sarveṣu anātmīyeṣu ātmīya buddhi rahitaḥ śāntaḥ ātma anubhava eka sukhaḥ evaṃbhūtaḥ dhyāna yogam kurvan brahma bhūyāya kalpate sarva bandha vinirmuktaḥ yathā avasthitam ātmānam anubhavati iti arthaḥ brahma bhūtaḥ prasanna ātmā na śocati na kāṅkṣati samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu mad bhaktim labhate parām brahma bhūtaḥ āvirbhūta aparicchinna jñāna eka ākāramat śeṣa ta eka svabhāva ātma svarūpaḥ itaḥ tu anyām prakṛtim viddhi me parām iti hi su śeṣa tā uktā prasanna ātmā kleśa karma ādibhiḥ akaluṣa svarūpaḥ mad vyatiriktam na kaṃcana bhūta viśeṣam prati śocati na kiṃcana kāṅkṣati api tu mad vyatirikteṣu sarveṣu bhūteṣu anādaraṇīya tāyām samaḥ nikhilam vastu jātam tṛṇavan manyamānaḥ mad bhaktim labhate parām mayi sarva īśvare nikhila jagat udbhava sthiti pralaya līle nirasta samasta heya gandhe anavadhika atiśaya asaṃkhyeya kalyāṇa guṇa gaṇa aika tāne lāvaṇya amṛta sāgare śrīmati puṇḍarīka nayane sva svāmini atyartha priya anubhava rūpām parām bhaktim labhate tad phalam āha bhaktyā mām abhijānāti yāvān yaḥ ca asmi tattvataḥ tataḥ mām tattvataḥ jñātvā viśate tad anantaram svarūpataḥ svabhāvataḥ ca yaḥ aham guṇataḥ vibhūtitaḥ api yāvānḥ ca aham tam mām evaṃrūpayā bhaktyā tattvataḥ abhijānāti mām tattvataḥ jñātvā tad anantaram tattva jñāna anantaram tataḥ bhaktitaḥ mām viśate praviśati tattvataḥ sva rūpa svabhāva guṇa vibhūti darśana uttara kāla bhāvinyā anavadhika atiśaya bhaktyā mām prāpnoti iti arthaḥ atra tataḥ iti prāpti hetu tayā nirdiṣṭā bhaktiḥ eva abhidhīyate bhaktyā tu ananyayā śakyaḥ iti tasya eva tattvataḥ praveśa hetutva abhidhānāt evam varṇa aśrama ucita nitya naimittika karmaṇām parityakta phala ādikānām parama puruṣa ārādhana rūpeṇa anuṣṭhitānām vipāka uktaḥ idānīm kāmyānām api karmaṇām uktena eva prakāreṇa anuṣṭhitānām sa eva vipāka iti āha sarva karmāṇi api sadā kurvāṇaḥ mad vyapāśrayaḥ mad prasādāt avāpnoti śāśvatam padam avyayam na kevalam nitya naimittikāni karmāṇi api tu sarvāṇi kāmyāni api karmāṇi mad vyāśrayaḥ mayi saṃnyasta kartṛ tva ādikaḥ kurvāṇaḥ mad prasādāt chāśvatam padam avyayam avikalam prāpnoti padyate gamyata iti padam mām prāpnoti iti arthaḥ yasmāt evam tasmāt cetasā sarva karmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya mad paraḥ buddhi yogam upāśritya mad citta ḥ satatam bhava cetasā ātmanaḥ madīya tvam anniyāmya tva buddhyā uktam hi mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasya adhyātma cetasā iti sarva karmāṇi sa kartṛkāṇi sārādhyāni mayi saṃnyasya mad paraḥ aham eva phala tayā prāpya iti anusaṃdhānaḥ karmāṇi kurvan imam eva buddhi yogam upāśritya satatam mad cittaḥ bhava mad cittaḥ sarva durgāṇi mad prasādāt tariṣyasi atha ced tvam ahaṃkārān na śroṣyasi vinaṅkṣyasi evam mad cittaḥ sarva karmāṇi kurvan sarvāṇi sāṃsārikāṇi durgāṇi mad prasādāt eva tariṣyasi atha tvam ahaṃkārāt aham eva kṛtyā kṛtya viṣayam sarvam jānāmi iti bhāvān mad uktam na śroṣyasi ced vinaṅkṣyasi vinaṣṭaḥ bhaviṣyasi na hi kaścid mad vyatiriktaḥ kṛtsnasya prāṇi jātasya kṛtyā ākṛtyayoḥ jñātā praśāsitā vā asti yadi ahaṅkāram āśritya na yotsya iti manyase mithyā eṣa vyavasāya ḥ te prakṛtiḥ tvām niyokṣyati yadi ahaṃkāram ātmani hita ahita jñāne svātantrya abhimānam āśritya mad niyogam anādṛtya na yotsya iti manyase eṣa te svātantrya vyavasāyaḥ mithyā bhaviṣyati yataḥ prakṛtiḥ tvām yuddhe niyokṣyati mad svātantrya udvignam tvām ajñam prakṛtiḥ niyokṣati tad upapādayati svabhāva jena kaunteya nibaddhaḥ svena karmaṇā kartum na icchasi yad mohāt kariṣyasi avaśaḥ api tad svabhāva jam hi kṣatriyasya karma śauryam svabhāva jena śaurya ākhyena svena karmaṇā nibaddhaḥ tad eva avaśaḥ paraiḥ dharṣaṇam asahamāna ḥ tvam eva tad yuddham kariṣyasi yad idānīm mohāt ajñānāt kartum na icchasi sarvam hi bhūta jātam sarva īśvareṇa mayā pūrva karma anuguṇyena prakṛti anuvartane niyamitam tad śṛṇu īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe arjuna tiṣṭhati bhrāmayan sarva bhūtāni yantra ārūḍhāni māyayā īśvaraḥ sarva niyamana śīlaḥ vāsudevaḥ sarva bhūtānām hṛd deśe sakala pravṛtti mūla jñāna udaya pradeśe tiṣṭhati katham kim kurvan  tiṣṭhati yantra ārūḍhāni sarva bhūtāni māyayā bhrāmayan svena eva nirmitam deha indriya avastham prakṛti ākhyam yantram ārūḍhāni sarva bhūtāni svakīyayā sattva ādi guṇa mayyā māyayā guṇa anuguṇam pravartayan  tiṣṭhati iti arthaḥ pūrvam api etad uktam sarvasya ca aham hṛdi sanniviṣṭaḥ mattaḥ smṛtiḥ jñānam apohanam ca iti matta ḥ sarvam pravartate iti ca ya ātmani tiṣṭhan iti ādikā śrutiḥ ca etad māyā nivṛtti hetum āha tam eva śaraṇam gaccha sarva bhāvena bhārata tad prasādāt parām śāntim sthānam prāpsyasi śāśvatam yasmāt evam tasmāt tam eva sarvasya praśāsitāram āśrita vātsalyena tvad sārathye avasthitam ittham kuru  iti ca śāsitāram sarva bhāvena sarva ātmanā śaraṇam gaccha sarva ātmanā anuvartasva anyathā api tad māyā preritena ajñena tvayā yuddha ādi karaṇam avarjanīyam tathā sati naṣṭaḥ bhaviṣyasi ataḥ tad ukta prakāreṇa yuddha ādikam kurv iti arthaḥ evam kurvāṇaḥ tad prasādāt parām śāntim sarva karma bandha upaśamam śāśvatam ca sthānam prāpsyasi yad abhidhīyate śruti śataiḥ tad viṣṇoḥ paramam padam sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ te ha nākam mahimānaḥ sacante yatra pūrve sādhyāḥ santi devāḥ  yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathama jā ye purāṇāḥ  pareṇa nākam nihitam guhāyām  yaḥ asya adhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman  atha yad ataḥ paraḥ divaḥ jyotiḥ dīpyate  saḥ adhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti tad viṣṇoḥ paramam padam ityādibhiḥ iti te jñānam ākhyātam guhyāt guhyataram mayā vimṛśya etad aśeṣeṇa yathā icchasi tathā kuru iti evam te mumukṣubhiḥ adhigantavyam jñānam sarvasmāt guhyāt guhyataram karma yoga viṣayam jñāna yoga viṣayam bhakti yoga viṣayam ca sarvam ākhyātam etad aśeṣeṇa vimṛśya sva adhikāra anurūpam yathā icchasi tathā kuru karma yogam jñāna yogam bhakti yogam vā yatheṣṭam ātiṣṭhā iti arthaḥ sarva guhyatamam bhūyaḥ śṛṇu me paramam vacaḥ iṣṭaḥ asi me dṛḍham iti tataḥ vakṣyāmi te hitam sarveṣu eteṣu guhyeṣu bhakti yogasya śraiṣṭhyād guhyatamam iti pūrvam eva uktam idam tu te guhyatamam pravakṣyāmi anasūyave iti ādau bhūyaḥ api tad viṣayam paramam me vacaḥ śṛṇu iṣṭaḥ asi me dṛḍham iti tataḥ te hitam vakṣyāmi mad manā bhava mad bhaktaḥ mad yājī mām namaskuru mām eva eṣyasi satyam te pratijāne priyaḥ asi me vedānteṣu veda aham etam puruṣam mahāntam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt tam evam vidvān amṛta iha bhavati na anyaḥ panthā vidyate ayanāya ityādiṣu vihitam vedanam dhyāna upāsana ādi śabda vācyam darśana samāna ākāram smṛti saṃtānam atyartha priyam iha mad manā bhava iti vidhīyate mad bhaktaḥ atyarthamad priyaḥ atyartha mad priya tvena niratiśaya priyām smṛti saṃtatim kuruṣva iti arthaḥ mad yājī tatra api mad bhakta iti anuṣajyate yajanam pūjanam atyartha priya mada ārādhana paraḥ bhava ārādhanam hi paripūrṇa śeṣa vṛttiḥ mām namaskuru namaḥ namanam mayi atimātra prahvībhāvam atyartha priyam kurv iti arthaḥ evam vartamānaḥ mām eva eṣyasi etad satyam te pratijāne tava pratijñām karomi na upacchandana mātram yataḥ tvam priyaḥ asi me priyaḥ hi jñāninaḥ atyartham aham sa ca mama priyaḥ iti pūrvam eva uktam yasya mayi atimātra tā prītiḥ vartate mama api tasmin atimātrā prītiḥ bhavati iti tad viyogam asahamānaḥ aham tam mām prāpayāmi ataḥ satyam eva pratijñātam mām eva eṣyasi iti sarva dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja aham tvā sarva pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ karma yoga jñāna yoga bhakti yoga rūpān sarvān dharmān parama niśśreyasa sādhana bhūtān mad ārādhana tvena atimātra prītyā yathā adhikāram kurvāṇa eva ukta rītyā phala karma kartṛ tva ādi parityāgena parityajya mām ekam eva kartāram ārādhyam prāpyam upāyam ca anusaṃdhatsva eṣa eva sarva dharmāṇām śastrīyaḥ parityāga iti niścayam śṛṇu me tatra tyāge bharata sattama tyāgaḥ hi puruṣa vyāghra trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ  iti ārabhya saṅgam tyaktvā phalam ca eva sa tyāga ḥ sāttivikaḥ mataḥ na hi dehabhṛtā śakyam tyaktum karmāṇi aśeṣataḥ yaḥ tu karma phala tyāgī sa tyāgī iti abhidhīyate  iti adhyāya ādau su dṛḍham upapāditam aham tvā sarva pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi evam vartamānam tvām mad prāpti virodhibhyaḥ anādi kāla saṃcita anantā kṛtya karaṇa kṛtya akaraṇa rūpebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ śokam mā kṛthāḥ atha vā sarva pāpa vinirmuktā atyartha bhagavat priya puruṣa nirvartya tvāt bhakti yogasya tad ārambha virodhi pāpānām ānantyāt tad prāyaścitta rūpaiḥ dharmaiḥ parimita kāla kṛtaiḥ teṣām dustara tayā ātmanaḥ bhakti yoga ārambhān arhatām ālocya śocataḥ arjunasya śokam apanudan śrī bhagavān uvāca sarva dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja iti bhakti yoga ārambha virodhi anādi kāla saṃcita nānāvidha ananta pāpa anuguṇān tad tad prāyaścitta rūpān kṛcchra cāndrāyaṇa kūśmāṇḍa vaiśvānara vrāta pati pavitra iṣṭi trivṛt agniṣṭoma ādikān nānāvidhān anantān  tvayā parimita kāla vartinā dūra nuṣṭhānān sarvān dharmān parityajya bhakti yoga ārambha siddhaye mām ekam parama kāruṇikam anālocita viśeṣa aśeṣa loka śaraṇyam āśrita vātsalya jaladhim śaraṇam prapadyasva aham tvā sarva pāpebhyaḥ yathā udita svarūpa bhakti ā ārambha virodhibhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpebhyaḥ mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ idam te na ātapaskāya na abhaktāya kadācana na ca aśuśrūṣave vācyam na ca mām yaḥ abhyasūyati idam te paramam guhyam śāstram mayā ākhyātam atapaskāya atapta tapase tvayā na vācyam tvayi vaktari mayi ca abhaktāya kadācana na vācyam tapta tapase ca abhaktāya na vācyam iti arthaḥ na ca aśuśrūṣave bhaktāya api aśuśrūṣave na vācyam na ca mām yaḥ abhyasūyati mad svarūpe mad aiśvarye mad guṇeṣu ca kathiteṣu yaḥ doṣam āviṣkaroti na tasmai vācyam asamāna vibhakti nirdeśaḥ tasya atyanta pariharaṇīya tā ājñāpanāya ya idam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu abhidhāsyati bhaktim mayi parām kṛtvā mām eva eṣyati asaṃśayaḥ idam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu yaḥ abhidhāsyati vyākhyāsyati saḥ mayi paramām bhaktim kṛtvā mām eva eṣyati na tatra saṃśayaḥ na ca tasmāt manuṣyeṣu kaścid me priya kṛttamaḥ bhavitā na ca me tasmāt anyaḥ priya taraḥ bhuvi sarveṣu manuṣyeṣu itaḥ pūrvam tasmāt anyaḥ manuṣyaḥ me na kaścid priya kṛt tamaḥ abhūt ita uttaram ca na bhavitā ayogyānām prathamam upādānam yogyānām akathanāt api tad kathanasya aniṣṭatama tvāt adhyeṣyate ca ya imam dharmyam saṃvādam āvayoḥ jñāna yajñena tena aham iṣṭaḥ syām iti me matiḥ ya imam āvayoḥ dharmyam saṃvādam adhyeṣyate tena jñāna yajñena aham iṣṭaḥ syām iti me matiḥ asmin yaḥ jñāna yajñaḥ abhidhīyate tena aham etad adhyayana mātreṇa iṣṭaḥ syām iti arthaḥ śraddhāvān anasūyuḥ ca śṛṇuyāt api yaḥ naraḥ saḥ api muktaḥ śubhān  lokān prāpnuyāt puṇya karmaṇām śraddhāvān anasūyuḥ ca yaḥ naraḥ śṛṇuyāt api tena śravaṇa mātreṇa saḥ api bhakti virodhi pāpebhyaḥ muktaḥ puṇya karmaṇām mad bhaktānām lokān samūhan prāpnuyāt kaścid etad śrutam pārtha tvayā ekāgreṇa cetasā kaccit ajñāna saṃmohaḥ pranaṣṭa ḥ te dhanañjaya mayā kathitam etad pārtha tvayā avahitena cetasā kaccit śrutam tava ajñāna saṃmohaḥ kaccit pranaṣṭaḥ yena ajñānena mūḍhaḥ na yotsyāmi iti uktavān arjuna uvāca naṣṭaḥ mohaḥ smṛtiḥ labdhā tvad prasādān mayā acyuta sthitaḥ asmi gata saṃdehaḥ kariṣye vacanam tava mohaḥ viparīta jñānam tvad prasādān mama tad vinaṣṭam smṛtiḥ yathā avasthita tattva jñānam tvad prasādāt eva tad ca labdham anātmani prakṛtau ātma abhimāna rūpaḥ mohaḥ parama puruṣa śarīra tayā tad ātmakasya kṛtsnasya cit acit vastunaḥ atadātma abhimāna rūpa ḥ ca nitya naimittika rūpasya karmaṇaḥ parama puruṣa ārādhana tayā tad prāpti upāya bhūtasya bandhaka tva buddhi rūpaḥ ca sarvaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ ātmanaḥ prakṛti vilakṣaṇa tva tad svabhāva rahita tā jñātṛ tva eka svabhāvatā parama puruṣa śeṣa tā tan niyāmya tva eka svarūpa tā jñānam nikhila jagat udbhava sthiti pralaya līlā aśeṣa doṣa pratyanīka kalyāṇa eka svarūpa svābhāvikāna vadhika atiśaya jñāna balāi śvarya vīrya śakti tejaḥ prabhṛt ca evaṃrūpa parāvara tattva yāthātmya vijñāna tad abhyāsa pūrvakāharahar upacīyamāna parama puruṣa prīti eka phala nitya naimittika karma niṣiddha parihā vedānta vedyaḥ parama puruṣaḥ vāsudevaḥ tvam iti jñānam ca labdham tataḥ ca bandha sneha kāruṇya pravṛddha viparīta jñāna mūlāt sarvasmāt avasādāt vimuktaḥ gata saṃdehaḥ svasthaḥ sthitaḥ asmi idānīm eva yuddha ādi kartavyatā viṣayam tava vacanam kariṣyati yathā uktam yuddha ādikam kariṣyati iti arthaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya sva putrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca yuddhe kim kariṣyanti iti pṛcchate sañjaya uvāca iti aham vāsudevasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ saṃvādam imam aśrauṣam adbhutam roma harṣaṇam iti evam vāsudevasya vasudeva sūnoḥ pārthasya ca tad pitṛṣvasuḥ putrasya ca mahātmanaḥ mahābuddheḥ tad pada dvandvam āśritasya imam roma harṣaṇam adbhutam saṃvādam aham yathā uktam aśrauṣam śrutavān aham vyāsa prasāda āt chrutavān etad guhyam aham param yogam yogeśvarāt kṛṣṇāt sākṣāt kathayataḥ svayam vyāsa prasādāt vyāsa anugraheṇa divya cakṣuḥ śrotra lābhāt etad param yoga ākhyam guhyam yogeśva rāj jñāna balāi śvarya vīrya śakti tejasām nidheḥ bhagavataḥ kṛṣṇāt svayam eva kathayataḥ sākṣāt śrutavān aham rājan saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya saṃvādam imam adbhutam keśava arjunayoḥ puṇyam hṛṣyāmi ca muhur muhur keśava arjunayoḥ imam puṇyam adbhutam saṃvādam sākṣāt chrutam smṛtvā muhur muhur hṛṣyāmi tad ca saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya rūpam ati adbhutam hareḥ vismayaḥ me mahān rājan hṛṣyāmi ca punar punar tad ca arjunāya prakāśitam aiśvaram hareḥ ati adbhutam rūpam mayā sākṣātkṛtam saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya hṛṣyataḥ me mahān vismayaḥ jāyate punar punar ca hṛṣyāmi kim atra bahunā uktena yatra yogeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ yatra pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ tatra śrīḥ vijayaḥ bhūtiḥ dhruvā nītiḥ matiḥ mama yatra yogeśvaraḥ kṛtsnasya uccāvaca rūpeṇa avasthitasya cetanasya acetanasya ca vastunaḥ ye ye svabhāva yogāḥ teṣām sarveṣām yogānām īśvaraḥ sva saṃkalpa āyattasva itara samasta vastu svarūpa sthiti pravṛtti bhedaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vasudeva sūnuḥ yatra ca pārthaḥ dhanurdharaḥ tad pitṛṣvasuḥ putraḥ tad pada dvandva eka āśrayaḥ tatra śrīḥ vijayaḥ bhūtiḥ nītiḥ ca dhruvā niścalā iti matiḥ mama iti
